Composition-Grounded Data Synthesis for Visual Reasoning
Authors: Xinyi Gu, Jiayuan Mao, Zhang-Wei Hong, Zhuoran Yu, Pengyuan Li, Dhiraj Joshi, Rogerio Feris, Zexue He
First: 2025-10-16T18:00:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T18:45:57+00:00
Comments: ICLR2026 camera-ready version. Project page: https://cogsynthesis.github.io
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Pretrained multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) demonstrate strong performance on diverse multimodal tasks, but remain limited in reasoning capabilities for domains where annotations are difficult to collect. In this work, we focus on artificial image domains such as charts, rendered documents, and webpages, which are abundant in practice yet lack large-scale human annotated reasoning datasets. We introduce COGS (COmposition-Grounded data Synthesis), a data-efficient framework for equipping MLLMs with advanced reasoning abilities from a small set of seed questions. The key idea is to decompose each seed question into primitive perception and reasoning factors, which can then be systematically recomposed with new images to generate large collections of synthetic question-answer pairs. Each generated question is paired with subquestions and intermediate answers, enabling reinforcement learning with factor-level process rewards. Experiments on chart reasoning show that COGS substantially improves performance on unseen questions, with the largest gains on reasoning-heavy and compositional questions. Moreover, training with a factor-level mixture of different seed data yields better transfer across multiple datasets, suggesting that COGS induces generalizable capabilities rather than dataset-specific overfitting. We further demonstrate that the framework extends beyond charts to other domains such as webpages.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向视觉推理的构图式数据合成方法
预训练多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在多样化多模态任务上展现出强大性能，但在标注数据难以获取的领域中，其推理能力仍存在局限。本研究聚焦于图表、渲染文档和网页等人工图像领域——这些领域在实践中数据丰富，却缺乏大规模人工标注的推理数据集。我们提出COGS（构图式数据合成框架），这是一种数据高效的方法，旨在通过少量种子问题赋予MLLMs高级推理能力。其核心思想是将每个种子问题解构为基本感知因子与推理因子，进而系统性地将这些因子与新图像重组，以生成大规模合成问答对。每个生成的问题均附带子问题与中间答案，支持通过因子级过程奖励进行强化学习。在图表推理任务上的实验表明，COGS能显著提升模型对未见问题的处理能力，尤其在强推理与组合型问题上效果最为突出。此外，采用不同种子数据的因子级混合训练策略，可提升模型在多个数据集间的迁移性能，这表明COGS能够诱导出泛化能力而非数据集特定的过拟合。我们进一步验证了该框架可扩展至网页等其他领域。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to enhance the reasoning capabilities of pretrained multimodal large language models (MLLMs) in artificial image domains like charts and webpages, where large-scale human-annotated reasoning datasets are scarce. The method introduces COGS, a data-efficient framework that decomposes a small set of seed questions into primitive perception and reasoning factors, then systematically recomposes these factors with new images to generate synthetic question-answer pairs, each accompanied by subquestions and intermediate answers for reinforcement learning with factor-level process rewards. Experimental results on chart reasoning demonstrate that COGS substantially improves performance on unseen questions, particularly on reasoning-heavy and compositional ones, and training with a factor-level mixture of seed data enhances transfer across multiple datasets, indicating generalizable capabilities; the framework also extends effectively to other domains such as webpages.
本研究的动机是提升预训练多模态大语言模型在图表和网页等人工图像领域的推理能力，这些领域缺乏大规模人工标注的推理数据集。方法上提出了COGS框架，它将少量种子问题分解为基本感知和推理因子，然后系统性地将这些因子与新图像重组，生成合成问答对，每个问题都配有子问题和中间答案，以支持基于因子级过程奖励的强化学习。实验结果表明，在图表推理任务中，COGS显著提升了模型对未见问题的性能，尤其在推理密集和组合型问题上效果最明显，且通过因子级混合种子数据训练能增强跨数据集的泛化能力，表明其诱导了可推广的推理技能；该框架还成功扩展到网页等其他领域。
Dual-Modality Multi-Stage Adversarial Safety Training: Robustifying Multimodal Web Agents Against Cross-Modal Attacks
Authors: Haoyu Liu, Dingcheng Li, Lukas Rutishauser, Zeyu Zheng
First: 2026-03-04T18:29:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T18:29:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal web agents that process both screenshots and accessibility trees are increasingly deployed to interact with web interfaces, yet their dual-stream architecture opens an underexplored attack surface: an adversary who injects content into the webpage DOM simultaneously corrupts both observation channels with a consistent deceptive narrative. Our vulnerability analysis on MiniWob++ reveals that attacks including a visual component far outperform text-only injections, exposing critical gaps in text-centric VLM safety training. Motivated by this finding, we propose Dual-Modality Multi-Stage Adversarial Safety Training (DMAST), a framework that formalizes the agent-attacker interaction as a two-player zero-sum Markov game and co-trains both players through a three-stage pipeline: (1) imitation learning from a strong teacher model, (2) oracle-guided supervised fine-tuning that uses a novel zero-acknowledgment strategy to instill task-focused reasoning under adversarial noise, and (3) adversarial reinforcement learning via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) self-play. On out-of-distribution tasks, DMAST substantially mitigates adversarial risks while simultaneously doubling task completion efficiency. Our approach significantly outperforms established training-based and prompt-based defenses, demonstrating genuine co-evolutionary progress and robust generalization to complex, unseen environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：双模态多阶段对抗安全训练：增强多模态网络代理抵御跨模态攻击的鲁棒性
同时处理网页截图与无障碍树的多模态网络代理正被日益广泛地部署于网页界面交互，但其双流架构暴露出一个尚未充分探索的攻击面：攻击者通过向网页DOM注入内容，可同时污染两个观测通道并构建一致的欺骗性叙述。我们在MiniWob++上的脆弱性分析表明，包含视觉组件的攻击效果远超纯文本注入，暴露出以文本为中心的视觉语言模型安全训练存在关键缺陷。基于此发现，我们提出双模态多阶段对抗安全训练框架，将代理与攻击者的交互形式化为双人零和马尔可夫博弈，并通过三阶段流程协同训练双方：(1) 基于强教师模型的模仿学习；(2) 采用新型零确认策略的预言机引导监督微调，使模型在对抗噪声中保持任务聚焦推理；(3) 通过群组相对策略优化的对抗强化学习自博弈。在分布外任务中，该框架显著降低对抗风险的同时将任务完成效率提升两倍。本方法显著优于现有基于训练与提示的防御方案，展现出真正的协同进化进展及对复杂未知环境的强泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the vulnerability of multimodal web agents, which process both screenshots and accessibility trees, to cross-modal adversarial attacks where injected webpage content corrupts both observation channels with a deceptive narrative. Motivated by findings that attacks with a visual component are far more effective than text-only injections, the authors propose Dual-Modality Multi-Stage Adversarial Safety Training (DMAST), a framework that formalizes the agent-attacker interaction as a two-player zero-sum Markov game and co-trains both players through a three-stage pipeline involving imitation learning, oracle-guided supervised fine-tuning with a zero-acknowledgment strategy, and adversarial reinforcement learning via Group Relative Policy Optimization self-play. Experimental results on out-of-distribution tasks show that DMAST substantially mitigates adversarial risks while simultaneously doubling task completion efficiency, significantly outperforming established training-based and prompt-based defenses and demonstrating robust generalization to complex, unseen environments.
本文针对处理截图和可访问性树的多模态网络代理的脆弱性，研究了跨模态对抗攻击，即攻击者注入网页内容会同时破坏两个观察通道并传递一致的欺骗性叙述。研究动机源于发现包含视觉成分的攻击远比纯文本注入更有效，作者提出了双模态多阶段对抗安全训练（DMAST）框架，该框架将代理与攻击者的交互形式化为两人零和马尔可夫博弈，并通过三阶段流程协同训练双方：模仿学习、采用零确认策略的预言机引导监督微调，以及基于群体相对策略优化的对抗性强化学习自博弈。在分布外任务上的实验结果表明，DMAST显著降低了对抗风险，同时将任务完成效率提高了一倍，明显优于现有的基于训练和提示的防御方法，并展现出对复杂未知环境的强大泛化能力。
A Constrained RL Approach for Cost-Efficient Delivery of Latency-Sensitive Applications
Authors: Ozan Aygün, Vincenzo Norman Vitale, Antonia M. Tulino, Hao Feng, Elza Erkip, Jaime Llorca
First: 2026-03-04T18:19:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T18:19:35+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 4 figures, accepted for publication in 2025 59th Asilomar Conference on Signals, Systems, and Computers
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Next-generation networks aim to provide performance guarantees to real-time interactive services that require timely and cost-efficient packet delivery. In this context, the goal is to reliably deliver packets with strict deadlines imposed by the application while minimizing overall resource allocation cost. A large body of work has leveraged stochastic optimization techniques to design efficient dynamic routing and scheduling solutions under average delay constraints; however, these methods fall short when faced with strict per-packet delay requirements. We formulate the minimum-cost delay-constrained network control problem as a constrained Markov decision process and utilize constrained deep reinforcement learning (CDRL) techniques to effectively minimize total resource allocation cost while maintaining timely throughput above a target reliability level. Results indicate that the proposed CDRL-based solution can ensure timely packet delivery even when existing baselines fall short, and it achieves lower cost compared to other throughput-maximizing methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种面向低延迟应用成本高效传输的约束强化学习方法
下一代网络旨在为需要及时且经济高效数据包传输的实时交互服务提供性能保障。在此背景下，目标是在满足应用层严格截止时限的前提下可靠传输数据包，同时最小化总体资源分配成本。现有研究多采用随机优化技术设计平均延迟约束下的动态路由与调度方案，但这些方法难以满足严格的逐包延迟要求。本文将最小成本延迟约束网络控制问题建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程，运用约束深度强化学习技术，在保持及时吞吐量高于目标可靠水平的同时有效降低总资源分配成本。实验表明，所提出的基于约束深度强化学习的解决方案能在现有基线方法失效时仍确保数据包及时传输，且相比其他吞吐量最大化方法具有更低的成本。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to provide performance guarantees for latency-sensitive applications in next-generation networks, this paper addresses the challenge of delivering packets within strict deadlines while minimizing resource costs. The method formulates the problem as a constrained Markov decision process and employs constrained deep reinforcement learning (CDRL) to dynamically optimize routing and scheduling. Experimental results demonstrate that the CDRL-based solution reliably meets per-packet delay requirements where existing baselines fail and achieves lower costs compared to throughput-maximizing alternatives.
本文针对下一代网络中延迟敏感型应用需在严格时限内交付数据包并最小化资源成本的挑战，提出了一种解决方案。方法将问题建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程，并采用约束深度强化学习（CDRL）来动态优化路由和调度。实验结果表明，基于CDRL的解决方案能在现有基线方法失效时仍确保数据包的及时交付，且相比其他最大化吞吐量的方法实现了更低的成本。
LadderSym: A Multimodal Interleaved Transformer for Music Practice Error Detection
Authors: Benjamin Shiue-Hal Chou, Purvish Jajal, Nick John Eliopoulos, James C. Davis, George K. Thiruvathukal, Kristen Yeon-Ji Yun, Yung-Hsiang Lu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-16T02:15:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T18:04:43+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Music learners can greatly benefit from tools that accurately detect errors in their practice. Existing approaches typically compare audio recordings to music scores using heuristics or learnable models. This paper introduces LadderSym, a novel Transformer-based method for music error detection. LadderSym is guided by two key observations about the state-of-the-art approaches: (1) late fusion limits inter-stream alignment and cross-modality comparison capability; and (2) reliance on score audio introduces ambiguity in the frequency spectrum, degrading performance in music with concurrent notes. To address these limitations, LadderSym introduces (1) a two-stream encoder with inter-stream alignment modules to improve audio comparison capabilities and error detection F1 scores, and (2) a multimodal strategy that leverages both audio and symbolic scores by incorporating symbolic representations as decoder prompts, reducing ambiguity and improving F1 scores. We evaluate our method on the MAESTRO-E and CocoChorales-E datasets by measuring the F1 score for each note category. Compared to the previous state of the art, LadderSym more than doubles F1 for missed notes on MAESTRO-E (26.8% -> 56.3%) and improves extra note detection by 14.4 points (72.0% -> 86.4%). Similar gains are observed on CocoChorales-E. Furthermore, we also evaluate our models on real data we curated. This work introduces insights about comparison models that could inform sequence evaluation tasks for reinforcement learning, human skill assessment, and model evaluation. Code: https://github.com/ben2002chou/LadderSYM
中文标题/摘要
标题：LadderSym：用于音乐练习错误检测的多模态交错Transformer
音乐学习者可从精准检测练习错误的工具中获益良多。现有方法通常通过启发式规则或可学习模型比对录音与乐谱。本文提出LadderSym，一种基于Transformer的音乐错误检测新方法。该方法基于对前沿技术的两项关键观察：（1）晚期融合限制了跨流对齐与多模态比对能力；（2）依赖乐谱音频会引入频谱模糊性，影响多音符音乐的检测性能。为此，LadderSym引入（1）配备跨流对齐模块的双流编码器以提升音频比对能力与错误检测F1分数；（2）通过将符号化乐谱表征作为解码器提示的多模态策略，降低模糊性并提升F1分数。我们在MAESTRO-E与CocoChorales-E数据集上通过各音符类别的F1分数评估方法性能。相较于现有最优技术，LadderSym在MAESTRO-E的漏音符检测F1分数提升超一倍（26.8%→56.3%），额外音符检测提升14.4个百分点（72.0%→86.4%），在CocoChorales-E数据集也取得类似提升。此外，我们在自建真实数据上进行了模型验证。本研究提出的比对模型见解可为强化学习序列评估、人类技能评估及模型评估任务提供参考。代码：https://github.com/ben2002chou/LadderSYM
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for accurate tools to assist music learners in practice, this paper introduces LadderSym, a Transformer-based method for detecting errors in musical performances. The method addresses limitations in prior approaches, such as late fusion hindering cross-modality alignment and reliance on score audio causing spectral ambiguity, by proposing a two-stream encoder with inter-stream alignment modules and a multimodal strategy that uses symbolic scores as decoder prompts. Experimental results on MAESTRO-E and CocoChorales-E datasets show significant improvements: for instance, F1 scores for missed notes more than doubled from 26.8% to 56.3% on MAESTRO-E, and extra note detection improved by 14.4 points to 86.4%, with similar gains on other datasets.
本文旨在为音乐学习者提供准确的练习错误检测工具，提出了LadderSym这一基于Transformer的方法。该方法针对现有方法中跨模态对齐能力不足和依赖乐谱音频导致频谱模糊等问题，通过引入带跨流对齐模块的双流编码器以及将符号乐谱作为解码器提示的多模态策略来改进。在MAESTRO-E和CocoChorales-E数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法显著提升了性能：例如在MAESTRO-E上，漏音符检测的F1分数从26.8%提高至56.3%，多余音符检测的F1分数提升了14.4个百分点至86.4%，在其他数据集上也观察到类似增益。
What Does Flow Matching Bring To TD Learning?
Authors: Bhavya Agrawalla, Michal Nauman, Aviral Kumar
First: 2026-03-04T17:51:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:51:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent work shows that flow matching can be effective for scalar Q-value function estimation in reinforcement learning (RL), but it remains unclear why or how this approach differs from standard critics. Contrary to conventional belief, we show that their success is not explained by distributional RL, as explicitly modeling return distributions can reduce performance. Instead, we argue that the use of integration for reading out values and dense velocity supervision at each step of this integration process for training improves TD learning via two mechanisms. First, it enables robust value prediction through \emph{test-time recovery}, whereby iterative computation through integration dampens errors in early value estimates as more integration steps are performed. This recovery mechanism is absent in monolithic critics. Second, supervising the velocity field at multiple interpolant values induces more \emph{plastic} feature learning within the network, allowing critics to represent non-stationary TD targets without discarding previously learned features or overfitting to individual TD targets encountered during training. We formalize these effects and validate them empirically, showing that flow-matching critics substantially outperform monolithic critics (2$\times$ in final performance and around 5$\times$ in sample efficiency) in settings where loss of plasticity poses a challenge e.g., in high-UTD online RL problems, while remaining stable during learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：流匹配为时序差分学习带来什么？
近期研究表明，流匹配在强化学习的标量Q值函数估计中具有显著效果，但其与标准评论家方法的差异机制尚不明确。与传统观点相反，我们发现其成功并非源于分布强化学习——显式建模回报分布反而可能降低性能。我们提出，该方法通过积分过程读取值函数，并在积分每一步施加密集速度监督，通过两种机制改进时序差分学习：首先，通过\emph{测试时恢复}实现稳健值预测——积分迭代计算能随着步数增加抑制早期估计误差，而传统单一评论家缺乏此机制；其次，在多个插值点监督速度场能诱导网络进行更\emph{可塑性}的特征学习，使评论家既能表征非平稳时序差分目标，又不会丢弃已学特征或对训练中单个目标过拟合。我们形式化论证了这些效应并通过实验验证：在可塑性缺失场景（如高UTD在线强化学习问题）中，流匹配评论家性能远超单一评论家（最终性能提升2倍，样本效率提升约5倍），且在学习过程中保持稳定。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates why flow matching, a technique for estimating Q-value functions, outperforms standard critic methods in reinforcement learning, challenging the assumption that its success stems from distributional RL. The authors propose that flow matching enhances temporal-difference learning through two key mechanisms: test-time recovery, where iterative integration during inference corrects early estimation errors, and increased plasticity in feature learning, which allows the network to adapt to non-stationary targets without forgetting. Experimental results demonstrate that flow-matching critics achieve roughly double the final performance and five times the sample efficiency of monolithic critics, particularly in challenging online RL scenarios with high update-to-data ratios, while maintaining stable training.
本文探讨了流匹配在强化学习中用于估计Q值函数时为何优于标准评论家方法，并反驳了其成功源于分布强化学习的观点。研究指出，流匹配通过两种机制改进时序差分学习：一是测试时恢复，即通过积分过程的迭代计算来修正早期估计误差；二是增强特征学习的可塑性，使网络能够适应非平稳目标而不会遗忘已学特征。实验结果表明，流匹配评论家在最终性能上约提升两倍，样本效率提高约五倍，尤其在高更新数据比的在线强化学习难题中表现稳定，显著超越了传统单体评论家。
Unraveling the Complexity of Memory in RL Agents: an Approach for Classification and Evaluation
Authors: Egor Cherepanov, Nikita Kachaev, Artem Zholus, Alexey K. Kovalev, Aleksandr I. Panov
First: 2024-12-09T14:34:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:39:28+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 6 figures, 9 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The incorporation of memory into agents is essential for numerous tasks within the domain of Reinforcement Learning (RL). In particular, memory is paramount for tasks that require the use of past information, adaptation to novel environments, and improved sample efficiency. However, the term "memory" encompasses a wide range of concepts, which, coupled with the lack of a unified methodology for validating an agent's memory, leads to erroneous judgments about agents' memory capabilities and prevents objective comparison with other memory-enhanced agents. This paper aims to streamline the concept of memory in RL by providing practical precise definitions of agent memory types, such as long-term vs. short-term memory and declarative vs. procedural memory, inspired by cognitive science. Using these definitions, we categorize different classes of agent memory, propose a robust experimental methodology for evaluating the memory capabilities of RL agents, and standardize evaluations. Furthermore, we empirically demonstrate the importance of adhering to the proposed methodology when evaluating different types of agent memory by conducting experiments with different RL agents and what its violation leads to.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解析强化学习智能体记忆复杂性：一种分类与评估方法
在强化学习领域，为智能体引入记忆机制对众多任务至关重要，尤其对需要利用历史信息、适应新环境和提升样本效率的任务具有决定性意义。然而，“记忆”一词涵盖的概念范畴广泛，加之缺乏验证智能体记忆的统一方法，导致对智能体记忆能力的误判，并阻碍其与其他记忆增强型智能体的客观比较。本文受认知科学启发，通过提供智能体记忆类型（如长时记忆与短时记忆、陈述性记忆与程序性记忆）的实用精确定义，旨在厘清强化学习中的记忆概念。基于这些定义，我们对不同类别的智能体记忆进行分类，提出评估强化学习智能体记忆能力的稳健实验方法，并建立标准化评估体系。此外，我们通过对不同强化学习智能体开展实验，实证证明了在评估各类智能体记忆时遵循所提方法的重要性，以及违反该方法可能导致的后果。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the ambiguous definitions and inconsistent evaluation of memory in reinforcement learning agents, which hinders objective comparisons, this paper proposes a classification framework for agent memory types inspired by cognitive science, such as long-term versus short-term and declarative versus procedural memory. The method involves establishing precise definitions, categorizing memory classes, and introducing a standardized experimental methodology to evaluate memory capabilities robustly. Experimental results with various RL agents demonstrate the necessity of adhering to this methodology, showing that violations lead to erroneous assessments and highlighting its role in enabling fair comparisons and accurate judgments of memory performance.
针对强化学习智能体中记忆概念定义模糊且评估方法不一致，阻碍客观比较的问题，本文受认知科学启发，提出了一个智能体记忆分类框架，包括长期与短期记忆、陈述性与程序性记忆等类型。方法包括建立精确定义、对记忆类别进行分类，并引入标准化的实验方法论以稳健评估记忆能力。通过对不同强化学习智能体的实验结果表明，遵循该方法论至关重要，违反会导致错误评估，并强调了其在实现公平比较和准确判断记忆性能方面的作用。
Low-Rank Contextual Reinforcement Learning from Heterogeneous Human Feedback
Authors: Seong Jin Lee, Will Wei Sun, Yufeng Liu
First: 2024-12-27T04:02:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:21:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) has become a cornerstone for aligning large language models with human preferences. However, the heterogeneity of human feedback, driven by diverse individual contexts and preferences, poses significant challenges for reward learning. To address this, we propose a Low-rank Contextual RLHF (LoCo-RLHF) framework that integrates contextual information to better model heterogeneous feedback while maintaining computational efficiency. Our approach builds on a contextual preference model, leveraging the intrinsic low-rank structure of the interaction between user contexts and query-answer pairs to mitigate the high dimensionality of feature representations. Furthermore, we address the challenge of distributional shifts in feedback through our Pessimism in Reduced Subspace (PRS) policy, inspired by pessimistic offline reinforcement learning techniques. We theoretically demonstrate that our policy achieves a tighter sub-optimality gap compared to existing methods. Extensive experiments validate the effectiveness of LoCo-RLHF, showcasing its superior performance in personalized RLHF settings and its robustness to distribution shifts.

标题：基于异构人类反馈的低秩上下文强化学习

Memory, Benchmark & Robots: A Benchmark for Solving Complex Tasks with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Egor Cherepanov, Nikita Kachaev, Alexey K. Kovalev, Aleksandr I. Panov
First: 2025-02-14T20:46:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:15:30+00:00
Comments: 57 pages, 29 figures, 11 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Memory is crucial for enabling agents to tackle complex tasks with temporal and spatial dependencies. While many reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms incorporate memory, the field lacks a universal benchmark to assess an agent's memory capabilities across diverse scenarios. This gap is particularly evident in tabletop robotic manipulation, where memory is essential for solving tasks with partial observability and ensuring robust performance, yet no standardized benchmarks exist. To address this, we introduce MIKASA (Memory-Intensive Skills Assessment Suite for Agents), a comprehensive benchmark for memory RL, with three key contributions: (1) we propose a comprehensive classification framework for memory-intensive RL tasks, (2) we collect MIKASA-Base -- a unified benchmark that enables systematic evaluation of memory-enhanced agents across diverse scenarios, and (3) we develop MIKASA-Robo (pip install mikasa-robo-suite) -- a novel benchmark of 32 carefully designed memory-intensive tasks that assess memory capabilities in tabletop robotic manipulation. Our work introduces a unified framework to advance memory RL research, enabling more robust systems for real-world use. MIKASA is available at https://tinyurl.com/membenchrobots.

IPD: Boosting Sequential Policy with Imaginary Planning Distillation in Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yihao Qin, Yuanfei Wang, Hang Zhou, Peiran Liu, Hao Dong, Yiding Ji
First: 2026-03-04T17:05:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:05:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decision transformer based sequential policies have emerged as a powerful paradigm in offline reinforcement learning (RL), yet their efficacy remains constrained by the quality of static datasets and inherent architectural limitations. Specifically, these models often struggle to effectively integrate suboptimal experiences and fail to explicitly plan for an optimal policy. To bridge this gap, we propose \textbf{Imaginary Planning Distillation (IPD)}, a novel framework that seamlessly incorporates offline planning into data generation, supervised training, and online inference. Our framework first learns a world model equipped with uncertainty measures and a quasi-optimal value function from the offline data. These components are utilized to identify suboptimal trajectories and augment them with reliable, imagined optimal rollouts generated via Model Predictive Control (MPC). A Transformer-based sequential policy is then trained on this enriched dataset, complemented by a value-guided objective that promotes the distillation of the optimal policy. By replacing the conventional, manually-tuned return-to-go with the learned quasi-optimal value function, IPD improves both decision-making stability and performance during inference. Empirical evaluations on the D4RL benchmark demonstrate that IPD significantly outperforms several state-of-the-art value-based and transformer-based offline RL methods across diverse tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：IPD：通过虚拟规划蒸馏提升离线强化学习中的序列策略
基于决策变换器的序列策略已成为离线强化学习（RL）中的重要范式，但其效果仍受限于静态数据集的质量与固有架构缺陷。具体而言，这类模型常难以有效整合次优经验，且无法显式规划最优策略。为弥补这一差距，我们提出\textbf{虚拟规划蒸馏（IPD）}——一种将离线规划无缝融入数据生成、监督训练与在线推理的新框架。该框架首先从离线数据中学习具备不确定性度量的世界模型和准最优价值函数，并利用这些组件识别次优轨迹，再通过模型预测控制（MPC）生成可靠的虚拟最优轨迹进行数据增强。随后，基于变换器的序列策略在此增强数据集上进行训练，辅以促进最优策略蒸馏的价值引导目标。通过用习得的准最优价值函数替代传统人工调整的回报目标，IPD在推理阶段同时提升了决策稳定性与性能。在D4RL基准上的实证评估表明，IPD在多样化任务中显著优于多种基于价值和基于变换器的先进离线RL方法。

Recurrent Action Transformer with Memory
Authors: Egor Cherepanov, Alexey Staroverov, Alexey K. Kovalev, Aleksandr I. Panov
First: 2023-06-15T19:29:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T17:00:23+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, 22 figures, 13 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Transformers have become increasingly popular in offline reinforcement learning (RL) due to their ability to treat agent trajectories as sequences, reframing policy learning as a sequence modeling task. However, in partially observable environments (POMDPs), effective decision-making depends on retaining information about past events -- something that standard transformers struggle with due to the quadratic complexity of self-attention, which limits their context length. One solution to this problem is to extend transformers with memory mechanisms. We propose the Recurrent Action Transformer with Memory (RATE), a novel transformer-based architecture for offline RL that incorporates a recurrent memory mechanism designed to regulate information retention. We evaluate RATE across a diverse set of environments: memory-intensive tasks (ViZDoom-Two-Colors, T-Maze, Memory Maze, Minigrid-Memory, and POPGym), as well as standard Atari and MuJoCo benchmarks. Our comprehensive experiments demonstrate that RATE significantly improves performance in memory-dependent settings while remaining competitive on standard tasks across a broad range of baselines. These findings underscore the pivotal role of integrated memory mechanisms in offline RL and establish RATE as a unified, high-capacity architecture for effective decision-making over extended horizons. Code: https://sites.google.com/view/rate-model/.

Memex(RL): Scaling Long-Horizon LLM Agents via Indexed Experience Memory
Authors: Zhenting Wang, Huancheng Chen, Jiayun Wang, Wei Wei
First: 2026-03-04T16:45:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T16:45:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents are fundamentally bottlenecked by finite context windows on long-horizon tasks. As trajectories grow, retaining tool outputs and intermediate reasoning in-context quickly becomes infeasible: the working context becomes prohibitively long, eventually exceeds the context budget, and makes distant evidence harder to use even when it is still present. Existing solutions typically shorten context through truncation or running summaries, but these methods are fundamentally lossy because they compress or discard past evidence itself. We introduce Memex, an indexed experience memory mechanism that instead compresses context without discarding evidence. Memex maintains a compact working context consisting of concise structured summaries and stable indices, while storing full-fidelity underlying interactions in an external experience database under those indices. The agent can then decide when to dereference an index and recover the exact past evidence needed for the current subgoal. We optimize both write and read behaviors with our reinforcement learning framework MemexRL, using reward shaping tailored to indexed memory usage under a context budget, so the agent learns what to summarize, what to archive, how to index it, and when to retrieve it. This yields a substantially less lossy form of long-horizon memory than summary-only approaches. We further provide a theoretical analysis showing the potential of the Memex loop to preserve decision quality with bounded dereferencing while keeping effective in-context computation bounded as history grows. Empirically, on challenging long-horizon tasks, Memex agent trained with MemexRL improves task success while using a significantly smaller working context.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Memex(RL)：通过索引化经验记忆扩展长程LLM智能体
大语言模型（LLM）智能体在长程任务中受限于有限的上下文窗口。随着任务轨迹增长，在上下文中保留工具输出和中间推理过程会迅速变得不可行：工作上下文会过度冗长，最终超出上下文预算，并使远端证据难以有效利用。现有解决方案通常通过截断或运行摘要来缩短上下文，但这些方法本质上是信息有损的，因为它们压缩或丢弃了原始证据。我们提出Memex——一种索引化经验记忆机制，它能在不丢弃证据的前提下压缩上下文。Memex维护由精炼结构化摘要和稳定索引组成的紧凑工作上下文，同时将完整保真的底层交互存储于外部经验数据库中。智能体可随时解引用索引，精确恢复当前子目标所需的过往证据。我们通过强化学习框架MemexRL优化读写行为，在上下文预算约束下采用针对索引记忆使用的奖励塑形，使智能体自主学习摘要生成、归档存储、索引构建与检索时机的策略。相比仅依赖摘要的方法，这实现了显著更低信息损耗的长程记忆形式。我们进一步提供理论分析，证明Memex循环在历史增长时能通过有限次解引用保持决策质量，同时将有效上下文计算量控制在有界范围内。实证研究表明，在复杂长程任务中，经MemexRL训练的Memex智能体能以显著更小的工作上下文实现更高的任务成功率。

The method introduces Memex, an indexed experience memory system that maintains a compact working context of structured summaries and indices while storing full interactions externally, and optimizes memory usage via a reinforcement learning framework called MemexRL to learn when to archive, index, and retrieve past evidence. The main experimental results show that the Memex agent, trained with MemexRL, achieves improved task success on challenging long-horizon tasks while using a significantly smaller working context compared to summary-only approaches.
本研究的动机在于大语言模型智能体在处理长程任务时受限于有限的上下文窗口，完整保留交互历史变得不可行，而现有的截断或摘要方法会丢失信息。方法上提出了Memex，一种索引化经验记忆机制，它维护一个包含结构化摘要和索引的紧凑工作上下文，同时将完整交互存储于外部数据库，并通过强化学习框架MemexRL优化记忆的写入和读取行为，让智能体学习何时归档、索引及检索过去证据。主要实验结果表明，在具有挑战性的长程任务上，经MemexRL训练的Memex智能体在显著减小工作上下文的同时，提高了任务成功率。
Generalization of RLVR Using Causal Reasoning as a Testbed
Authors: Brian Lu, Hongyu Zhao, Shuo Sun, Hao Peng, Rui Ding, Hongyuan Mei
First: 2025-12-23T20:45:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T16:41:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a promising paradigm for post-training large language models (LLMs) on complex reasoning tasks. Yet, the conditions under which RLVR yields robust generalization remain underexplored. This paper provides an empirical study of RLVR generalization in the setting of probabilistic inference over causal graphical models. This setting offers two natural axes along which to examine generalization: (i) the level of the probabilistic query -- associational, interventional, or counterfactual -- and (ii) the structural complexity of the query, measured by the size of its relevant subgraph. We construct a dataset of causal graphs and queries spanning these difficulty axes and fine-tune Qwen-2.5-Instruct models using RLVR or supervised fine-tuning (SFT). We vary both the model scale (3B-32B) and the query level included in training. We find that RLVR yields stronger within-level and across-level generalization than SFT, but only for specific combinations of model size and training query level. Further analysis shows that RLVR's effectiveness depends on the model's initial reasoning competence. With sufficient initial competence, RLVR improves an LLM's marginalization strategy and reduces errors in intermediate probability calculations, producing substantial accuracy gains, particularly on more complex queries. These results show that RLVR can improve specific causal reasoning subskills, with its benefits emerging only when the model has sufficient initial competence. Our code and data is available at https://github.com/zhichul/rlcausal.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于因果推理测试平台的RLVR泛化性研究
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）已成为在复杂推理任务上对大型语言模型（LLM）进行后训练的有前景范式，但其实现稳健泛化的条件尚未充分探索。本文通过因果图模型的概率推理场景，对RLVR的泛化性进行实证研究。该场景提供两个考察泛化性的自然维度：（i）概率查询的层级——关联性、干预性或反事实性；（ii）查询的结构复杂度，以其相关子图规模衡量。我们构建了覆盖这些难度维度的因果图与查询数据集，并采用RLVR或监督微调（SFT）对Qwen-2.5-Instruct模型进行微调，同时调整模型规模（3B-32B）和训练中包含的查询层级。研究发现，仅当模型规模与训练查询层级形成特定组合时，RLVR才能比SFT产生更强的层级内与跨层级泛化能力。进一步分析表明，RLVR的有效性取决于模型的初始推理能力：当初始能力足够时，RLVR能优化LLM的边缘化策略并减少中间概率计算错误，从而显著提升准确率，尤其在复杂查询上更为明显。这些结果证明RLVR可改进特定的因果推理子技能，但其优势仅在模型具备足够初始能力时显现。代码与数据公开于https://github.com/zhichul/rlcausal。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the generalization capabilities of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for enhancing large language models' performance on causal reasoning tasks, motivated by the need to understand when RLVR yields robust improvements beyond supervised fine-tuning. The method involves constructing a dataset of causal graphs and queries varying in query level and structural complexity, then fine-tuning Qwen-2.5-Instruct models of different scales using RLVR and supervised fine-tuning while controlling the training query levels. Experimental results show that RLVR outperforms supervised fine-tuning in both within-level and across-level generalization, but only for specific combinations of model size and training query level, with its effectiveness hinging on the model's initial reasoning competence; further analysis indicates RLVR improves marginalization strategies and reduces calculation errors, leading to accuracy gains on complex queries.
本文研究了基于可验证奖励的强化学习在提升大语言模型因果推理任务性能上的泛化能力，其动机在于理解RLVR何时能产生超越监督微调的稳健改进。方法包括构建一个在查询级别和结构复杂性上变化的因果图与查询数据集，然后使用RLVR和监督微调对不同规模的Qwen-2.5-Instruct模型进行微调，同时控制训练查询级别。实验结果表明，RLVR在级别内和跨级别泛化上均优于监督微调，但仅针对特定的模型规模与训练查询级别组合有效，其效果取决于模型的初始推理能力；进一步分析显示RLVR改进了边缘化策略并减少了中间概率计算错误，从而在复杂查询上获得了准确性提升。
Offline-to-Online Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning with Offline Value Function Memory and Sequential Exploration
Authors: Hai Zhong, Xun Wang, Zhuoran Li, Longbo Huang
First: 2024-10-25T10:24:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T16:33:38+00:00
Comments: Include detailed hyperparameter configurations
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning has emerged as a powerful paradigm, leveraging offline data for initialization and online fine-tuning to enhance both sample efficiency and performance. However, most existing research has focused on single-agent settings, with limited exploration of the multi-agent extension, i.e., Offline-to-Online Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (O2O MARL). In O2O MARL, two critical challenges become more prominent as the number of agents increases: (i) the risk of unlearning pre-trained Q-values due to distributional shifts during the transition from offline-to-online phases, and (ii) the difficulty of efficient exploration in the large joint state-action space. To tackle these challenges, we propose a novel O2O MARL framework called Offline Value Function Memory with Sequential Exploration (OVMSE). First, we introduce the Offline Value Function Memory (OVM) mechanism to compute target Q-values, preserving knowledge gained during offline training, ensuring smoother transitions, and enabling efficient fine-tuning. Second, we propose a decentralized Sequential Exploration (SE) strategy tailored for O2O MARL, which effectively utilizes the pre-trained offline policy for exploration, thereby significantly reducing the joint state-action space to be explored. Extensive experiments on the StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge (SMAC) demonstrate that OVMSE significantly outperforms existing baselines, achieving superior sample efficiency and overall performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于离线价值函数记忆与顺序探索的离线至在线多智能体强化学习
离线至在线强化学习已成为一种强大范式，通过利用离线数据进行初始化并在线微调，以提升样本效率与性能。然而，现有研究多集中于单智能体场景，对多智能体扩展——即离线至在线多智能体强化学习（O2O MARL）的探索有限。在O2O MARL中，随着智能体数量增加，两大挑战尤为突出：（一）因离线至在线阶段转换中的分布偏移导致预训练Q值被遗忘的风险；（二）在庞大的联合状态-动作空间中实现高效探索的困难。为应对这些挑战，我们提出一种名为“离线价值函数记忆与顺序探索”（OVMSE）的新型O2O MARL框架。首先，引入离线价值函数记忆（OVM）机制计算目标Q值，以保留离线训练中获得的知识，确保更平稳的过渡并实现高效微调。其次，提出一种专为O2O MARL设计的去中心化顺序探索（SE）策略，该策略有效利用预训练的离线策略进行探索，从而显著缩减待探索的联合状态-动作空间。在《星际争霸》多智能体挑战（SMAC）上的大量实验表明，OVMSE显著优于现有基线方法，实现了更优的样本效率与整体性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenges of Offline-to-Online Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (O2O MARL), where scaling to multiple agents exacerbates the risk of unlearning pre-trained Q-values during the online phase and complicates exploration in the vast joint action space. The proposed solution, OVMSE, introduces an Offline Value Function Memory mechanism to stabilize Q-value targets and preserve offline knowledge, combined with a decentralized Sequential Exploration strategy that leverages the pre-trained policy to reduce the exploration space efficiently. Experimental results on the StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge show that OVMSE surpasses existing baselines in both sample efficiency and overall performance.
本文针对离线到在线多智能体强化学习中的挑战展开研究，即智能体数量增加会加剧在线阶段遗忘预训练Q值的风险，并使得联合动作空间的探索更加困难。提出的OVMSE框架包含离线价值函数记忆机制，用于稳定Q值目标并保留离线知识，以及一种去中心化的顺序探索策略，利用预训练策略有效缩小探索空间。在星际争霸多智能体挑战上的实验表明，OVMSE在样本效率和整体性能上均显著优于现有基线方法。
Learning Hip Exoskeleton Control Policy via Predictive Neuromusculoskeletal Simulation
Authors: Ilseung Park, Changseob Song, Inseung Kang
First: 2026-03-04T15:23:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T15:23:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Developing exoskeleton controllers that generalize across diverse locomotor conditions typically requires extensive motion-capture data and biomechanical labeling, limiting scalability beyond instrumented laboratory settings. Here, we present a physics-based neuromusculoskeletal learning framework that trains a hip-exoskeleton control policy entirely in simulation, without motion-capture demonstrations, and deploys it on hardware via policy distillation. A reinforcement learning teacher policy is trained using a muscle-synergy action prior over a wide range of walking speeds and slopes through a two-stage curriculum, enabling direct comparison between assisted and no-exoskeleton conditions. In simulation, exoskeleton assistance reduces mean muscle activation by up to 3.4% and mean positive joint power by up to 7.0% on level ground and ramp ascent, with benefits increasing systematically with walking speed. On hardware, the assistance profiles learned in simulation are preserved across matched speed-slope conditions (r: 0.82, RMSE: 0.03 Nm/kg), providing quantitative evidence of sim-to-real transfer without additional hardware tuning. These results demonstrate that physics-based neuromusculoskeletal simulation can serve as a practical and scalable foundation for exoskeleton controller development, substantially reducing experimental burden during the design phase.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于预测性神经肌肉骨骼仿真的髋关节外骨骼控制策略学习
开发适用于多种运动条件的外骨骼控制器通常需要大量运动捕捉数据和生物力学标注，这限制了其在仪器化实验室环境外的可扩展性。本研究提出一种基于物理的神经肌肉骨骼学习框架，完全在仿真环境中训练髋关节外骨骼控制策略，无需运动捕捉演示，并通过策略蒸馏部署至硬件设备。强化学习教师策略采用肌肉协同作用先验，通过两阶段课程在多种步行速度和坡度上进行训练，实现外骨骼辅助与无外骨骼条件的直接比较。仿真结果显示：在平地与斜坡上行时，外骨骼辅助使平均肌肉激活降低达3.4%，平均正向关节功率降低达7.0%，且效益随步行速度提升系统性增强。硬件实验中，仿真习得的辅助模式在匹配的速度-坡度条件下保持稳定（相关系数：0.82，均方根误差：0.03 Nm/kg），为无需额外硬件调优的仿真到现实迁移提供了量化证据。这些结果表明，基于物理的神经肌肉骨骼仿真可作为外骨骼控制器开发实用且可扩展的基础，显著降低设计阶段的实验负担。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to develop exoskeleton controllers that generalize without extensive lab-based motion-capture data, this paper introduces a physics-based neuromusculoskeletal learning framework to train a hip-exoskeleton control policy entirely in simulation. The method employs reinforcement learning with a muscle-synergy action prior, trained over varied walking speeds and slopes via a two-stage curriculum, and transfers the policy to hardware through distillation. Experimental results in simulation show the exoskeleton reduces mean muscle activation by up to 3.4% and mean positive joint power by up to 7.0% on level ground and ramp ascent, with benefits increasing at higher speeds. On physical hardware, the learned assistance profiles transfer effectively across matched conditions (correlation 0.82, RMSE 0.03 Nm/kg), demonstrating successful sim-to-real transfer without additional tuning.
本研究旨在开发无需大量实验室运动捕捉数据即可泛化的外骨骼控制器，提出了一种基于物理的神经肌肉骨骼学习框架，完全在仿真中训练髋部外骨骼控制策略。方法采用强化学习并结合肌肉协同动作先验，通过两阶段课程在多种步行速度和坡度上进行训练，并通过策略蒸馏将策略部署到硬件。仿真实验结果表明，外骨骼在平地与上坡行走中可将平均肌肉激活降低达3.4%，平均关节正功率降低达7.0%，且效益随速度增加而提升。在硬件实验中，学习到的辅助曲线在匹配的速度-坡度条件下得到保持（相关系数0.82，均方根误差0.03 Nm/kg），实现了无需额外调参的仿真到现实迁移，证明了该框架作为外骨骼控制器开发基础的可行性与可扩展性。
InstMeter: An Instruction-Level Method to Predict Energy and Latency of DL Model Inference on MCUs
Authors: Hao Liu, Qing Wang, Marco Zuniga
First: 2026-03-04T14:48:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T14:48:29+00:00
Comments: 17 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep learning (DL) models can now run on microcontrollers (MCUs). Through neural architecture search (NAS), we can search DL models that meet the constraints of MCUs. Among various constraints, energy and latency costs of the model inference are critical metrics. To predict them, existing research relies on coarse proxies such as multiply-accumulations (MACs) and model's input parameters, often resulting in inaccurate predictions or requiring extensive data collection. In this paper, we propose InstMeter, a predictor leveraging MCUs' clock cycles to accurately estimate the energy and latency of DL models. Clock cycles are fundamental metrics reflecting MCU operations, directly determining energy and latency costs. Furthermore, a unique property of our predictor is its strong linearity, allowing it to be simple and accurate. We thoroughly evaluate InstMeter under different scenarios, MCUs, and software settings. Compared with state-of-the-art studies, InstMeter can reduce the energy and latency prediction errors by $3\times$ and $6.5\times$, respectively, while requiring $100\times$ and $10\times$ less training data. In the NAS scenario, InstMeter can fully exploit the energy budget, identifying optimal DL models with higher inference accuracy. We also evaluate InstMeter's generalization performance through various experiments on three ARM MCUs (Cortex-M4, M7, M33) and one RISC-V-based MCU (ESP32-C3), different compilation options (-Os, -O2), GCC versions (v7.3, v10.3), application scenarios (keyword spotting, image recognition), dynamic voltage and frequency scaling, temperatures (21°C, 43°C), and software settings (TFLMv2.4, TFLMvCI). We will open our source codes and the MCU-specific benchmark datasets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：InstMeter：一种基于指令级的深度学习模型在微控制器上推理能耗与延迟预测方法
深度学习模型现可在微控制器上运行。通过神经架构搜索，可寻找满足MCU约束的DL模型。在众多约束中，模型推理的能耗与延迟是关键指标。现有研究依赖乘加运算次数和模型输入参数等粗略代理进行预测，常导致结果不准确或需大量数据收集。本文提出InstMeter，一种利用MCU时钟周期精准预测DL模型能耗与延迟的方法。时钟周期是反映MCU运行的基础指标，直接决定能耗与延迟成本。该预测器具有强线性特性，兼具简洁性与准确性。我们在不同场景、MCU及软件设置下全面评估InstMeter。与前沿研究相比，InstMeter将能耗与延迟预测误差分别降低3倍和6.5倍，同时所需训练数据减少100倍和10倍。在NAS场景中，InstMeter能充分利用能耗预算，识别出具有更高推理精度的最优DL模型。我们通过在三种ARM MCU（Cortex-M4、M7、M33）和一款RISC-V架构MCU（ESP32-C3）上进行多维度实验，验证了方法的泛化性能，涵盖不同编译选项（-Os、-O2）、GCC版本（v7.3、v10.3）、应用场景（关键词检测、图像识别）、动态电压频率调节、温度条件（21°C、43°C）及软件设置（TFLMv2.4、TFLMvCI）。我们将公开源代码及MCU专用基准数据集。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for accurate energy and latency prediction for deep learning model inference on microcontrollers, which is crucial for neural architecture search but often relies on coarse proxies leading to inaccuracies, this paper introduces InstMeter, a method that leverages clock cycles as a fundamental metric to estimate these costs with high linearity and simplicity. The method involves using clock cycles to directly model energy and latency, enabling precise predictions across various hardware and software configurations. Experimental results demonstrate that InstMeter reduces energy and latency prediction errors by 3x and 6.5x respectively compared to state-of-the-art methods, while requiring significantly less training data, and it effectively identifies optimal models in NAS scenarios, with validation on multiple MCU platforms and settings.
本文的动机在于需要准确预测深度学习模型在微控制器上推理的能耗和延迟，这对神经架构搜索至关重要，但现有方法常依赖粗略代理导致预测不准确。为此，论文提出了InstMeter方法，利用时钟周期作为基本指标，通过其强线性特性来简单而准确地估计能耗和延迟。该方法基于时钟周期直接建模成本，并在不同硬件和软件配置下进行评估。实验结果表明，与现有研究相比，InstMeter将能耗和延迟预测误差分别降低了3倍和6.5倍，同时所需训练数据大幅减少，并在神经架构搜索中能充分利用能耗预算找到更优模型，其泛化性能在多种微控制器和设置下得到验证。
BeamPERL: Parameter-Efficient RL with Verifiable Rewards Specializes Compact LLMs for Structured Beam Mechanics Reasoning
Authors: Tarjei Paule Hage, Markus J. Buehler
First: 2026-03-04T14:42:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T14:42:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Can reinforcement learning with hard, verifiable rewards teach a compact language model to reason about physics, or does it primarily learn to pattern-match toward correct answers? We study this question by training a 1.5B-parameter reasoning model on beam statics, a classic engineering problem, using parameter-efficient RLVR with binary correctness rewards from symbolic solvers, without teacher-generated reasoning traces. The best BeamPERL checkpoint achieves a 66.7% improvement in Pass@1 over the base model. However, the learned competence is anisotropic: the model generalizes compositionally (more loads) but fails under topological shifts (moved supports) that require the same equilibrium equations. Intermediate checkpoints yield the strongest reasoning, while continued optimization degrades robustness while maintaining reward. These findings reveal a key limitation of outcome-level alignment: reinforcement learning with exact physics rewards induces procedural solution templates rather than internalization of governing equations. The precision of the reward signal - even when analytically exact - does not by itself guarantee transferable physical reasoning. Our results suggest that verifiable rewards may need to be paired with structured reasoning scaffolding to move beyond template matching toward robust scientific reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BeamPERL：基于可验证奖励的参数高效强化学习专用于结构化梁力学推理的紧凑型大语言模型
采用严格可验证奖励的强化学习能否教会紧凑语言模型进行物理推理，还是主要使其学会对正确答案的模式匹配？我们通过在梁静力学这一经典工程问题上训练一个15亿参数推理模型来研究该问题，使用参数高效的RLVR方法，仅依赖符号求解器提供的二元正确性奖励，无需教师生成的推理轨迹。最佳BeamPERL检查点在Pass@1指标上较基础模型提升66.7%。然而习得的能力呈现各向异性：模型能实现组合泛化（更多载荷），却在需要相同平衡方程的结构拓扑变化（支座位移）时失效。中间检查点展现出最强的推理能力，而持续优化在保持奖励的同时降低了鲁棒性。这些发现揭示了结果层面对齐的关键局限：基于精确物理奖励的强化学习仅诱导程序化解题模板，而非对控制方程的内化理解。即使奖励信号在解析意义上完全精确，其本身并不能保证可迁移的物理推理能力。我们的结果表明，可验证奖励可能需要与结构化推理框架结合，才能超越模板匹配，实现鲁棒的科学推理。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates whether reinforcement learning with verifiable, binary rewards can teach a compact language model to perform genuine physics reasoning rather than merely pattern-matching correct answers. The authors introduce BeamPERL, a parameter-efficient RL method that trains a 1.5B-parameter model on beam statics problems using only correctness rewards from symbolic solvers, without relying on human reasoning traces. Experimental results show the best checkpoint achieves a 66.7% improvement in Pass@1 over the base model, but the learned competence is anisotropic: it generalizes compositionally to more loads yet fails under topological shifts like moved supports, which require the same underlying physics. Notably, intermediate checkpoints yield the strongest reasoning, while further optimization degrades robustness despite maintaining high reward, revealing that outcome-level alignment with exact rewards induces procedural solution templates rather than an internalization of governing equations.

Learning in Markov Decision Processes with Exogenous Dynamics
Authors: Davide Maran, Davide Salaorni, Marcello Restelli
First: 2026-03-03T11:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T14:42:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning algorithms are typically designed for generic Markov Decision Processes (MDPs), where any state-action pair can lead to an arbitrary transition distribution. In many practical systems, however, only a subset of the state variables is directly influenced by the agent's actions, while the remaining components evolve according to exogenous dynamics and account for most of the stochasticity. In this work, we study a structured class of MDPs characterized by exogenous state components whose transitions are independent of the agent's actions. We show that exploiting this structure yields significantly improved learning guarantees, with only the size of the exogenous state space appearing in the leading terms of the regret bounds. We further establish a matching lower bound, showing that this dependence is information-theoretically optimal. Finally, we empirically validate our approach across classical toy settings and real-world-inspired environments, demonstrating substantial gains in sample efficiency compared to standard reinforcement learning methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：具有外生动态的马尔可夫决策过程学习
强化学习算法通常为通用马尔可夫决策过程设计，其中任意状态-动作对可导致任意转移分布。然而，在许多实际系统中，仅部分状态变量直接受智能体动作影响，其余部分则遵循外生动态演化，并构成随机性的主要来源。本研究针对一类具有外生状态分量的结构化MDP展开分析，其转移过程独立于智能体动作。我们证明利用该结构可显著提升学习保证，仅外生状态空间规模出现在遗憾边界的主导项中。进一步建立匹配下界，表明该依赖关系在信息论意义下最优。最后，通过在经典玩具场景和现实启发环境中进行实证验证，相比标准强化学习方法，本方法在样本效率上展现出显著优势。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that many real-world systems have state variables with exogenous dynamics unaffected by the agent's actions, a structure not leveraged by standard reinforcement learning methods for general Markov Decision Processes. The method involves analyzing a structured MDP class where exogenous state transitions are action-independent, leading to theoretical guarantees that exploit this separation. Main experimental results show significantly improved sample efficiency in both toy and real-world-inspired environments, with regret bounds depending primarily on the exogenous state space size, which is proven to be information-theoretically optimal via a matching lower bound.
本文的动机是观察到许多实际系统中存在不受智能体行动影响的外生状态变量，而标准的强化学习方法未利用这种一般马尔可夫决策过程之外的结构。方法涉及分析一类外生状态转移与行动无关的结构化MDP，通过利用这种分离性来推导理论保证。主要实验结果表明，在经典玩具环境和现实世界启发环境中，相比标准强化学习方法，样本效率显著提升，其遗憾边界主要取决于外生状态空间大小，并通过匹配下界证明这是信息论最优的。
Knowledge Graphs are Implicit Reward Models: Path-Derived Signals Enable Compositional Reasoning
Authors: Yuval Kansal, Niraj K. Jha
First: 2026-01-21T16:38:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T14:21:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models have achieved near-expert performance in structured reasoning domains like mathematics and programming, yet their ability to perform compositional multi-hop reasoning in specialized scientific fields remains limited. We propose a bottom-up learning paradigm in which models are grounded in axiomatic domain facts and compose them to solve complex, unseen tasks. To this end, we present a post-training pipeline, based on a combination of supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning (RL), in which knowledge graphs act as implicit reward models. By deriving novel reward signals from knowledge graph paths, we provide verifiable, scalable, and grounded supervision that encourages models to compose intermediate axioms rather than optimize only final answers during RL. We validate this approach in the medical domain, training a 14B model on short-hop reasoning paths (1-3 hops) and evaluating its zero-shot generalization to complex multi-hop queries (4-5 hops). Our experiments show that path-derived rewards act as a "compositional bridge", enabling our model to significantly outperform much larger models and frontier systems like GPT-5.2 and Gemini 3 Pro, on the most difficult reasoning tasks. Furthermore, we demonstrate the robustness of our approach to adversarial perturbations against option-shuffling stress tests. This work suggests that grounding the reasoning process in structured knowledge is a scalable and efficient path toward intelligent reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：知识图谱作为隐式奖励模型：路径衍生信号赋能组合推理
大型语言模型在数学与编程等结构化推理领域已接近专家水平，但其在专业科学领域进行组合式多跳推理的能力仍有限。我们提出一种自底向上的学习范式，使模型基于公理化领域事实进行组合以解决复杂未知任务。为此，我们提出一种结合监督微调与强化学习的后训练流程，其中知识图谱充当隐式奖励模型。通过从知识图谱路径中衍生新颖奖励信号，我们提供可验证、可扩展且具基础性的监督，促使模型在强化学习中组合中间公理而非仅优化最终答案。我们在医学领域验证该方法，使用短跳推理路径（1-3跳）训练140亿参数模型，并评估其对复杂多跳查询（4-5跳）的零样本泛化能力。实验表明，路径衍生奖励作为“组合桥梁”，使我们的模型在最困难推理任务上显著超越GPT-5.2和Gemini 3 Pro等更大规模前沿系统。此外，我们证明了该方法在选项重排压力测试中对对抗性扰动的鲁棒性。这项工作表明，将推理过程锚定于结构化知识是实现智能推理的可扩展高效路径。

SaFeR: Safety-Critical Scenario Generation for Autonomous Driving Test via Feasibility-Constrained Token Resampling
Authors: Jinlong Cui, Fenghua Liang, Guo Yang, Chengcheng Tang, Jianxun Cui
First: 2026-03-04T13:46:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T13:46:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety-critical scenario generation is crucial for evaluating autonomous driving systems. However, existing approaches often struggle to balance three conflicting objectives: adversarial criticality, physical feasibility, and behavioral realism. To bridge this gap, we propose SaFeR: safety-critical scenario generation for autonomous driving test via feasibility-constrained token resampling. We first formulate traffic generation as a discrete next token prediction problem, employing a Transformer-based model as a realism prior to capture naturalistic driving distributions. To capture complex interactions while effectively mitigating attention noise, we propose a novel differential attention mechanism within the realism prior. Building on this prior, SaFeR implements a novel resampling strategy that induces adversarial behaviors within a high-probability trust region to maintain naturalism, while enforcing a feasibility constraint derived from the Largest Feasible Region (LFR). By approximating the LFR via offline reinforcement learning, SaFeR effectively prevents the generation of theoretically inevitable collisions. Closed-loop experiments on the Waymo Open Motion Dataset and nuPlan demonstrate that SaFeR significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving a higher solution rate and superior kinematic realism while maintaining strong adversarial effectiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SaFeR：基于可行性约束令牌重采样的自动驾驶测试安全关键场景生成
安全关键场景生成对自动驾驶系统评估至关重要，但现有方法常难以平衡对抗性临界性、物理可行性与行为真实性这三个相互冲突的目标。为此，我们提出SaFeR：一种基于可行性约束令牌重采样的自动驾驶测试安全关键场景生成方法。该方法首先将交通场景生成建模为离散的下一令牌预测问题，采用基于Transformer的模型作为真实性先验以捕捉自然驾驶分布。为在捕捉复杂交互的同时有效抑制注意力噪声，我们在真实性先验中提出一种新颖的差分注意力机制。基于此先验，SaFeR实施了一种创新的重采样策略：在高概率信任区域内诱导对抗行为以保持自然性，同时强制执行源自最大可行区域（LFR）的可行性约束。通过离线强化学习近似LFR，SaFeR有效避免了理论上必然碰撞的生成。在Waymo开放运动数据集和nuPlan上的闭环实验表明，SaFeR显著优于现有基线方法，在保持强对抗有效性的同时，实现了更高的求解率和更优的运动学真实性。

Experimental results on the Waymo Open Motion Dataset and nuPlan show that SaFeR outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving higher solution rates, superior kinematic realism, and strong adversarial effectiveness.

A Review of Reward Functions for Reinforcement Learning in the context of Autonomous Driving
Authors: Ahmed Abouelazm, Jonas Michel, J. Marius Zoellner
First: 2024-04-12T08:32:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T13:43:15+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the 35th IEEE Intelligent Vehicles Symposium (IV 2024)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has emerged as an important approach for autonomous driving. A reward function is used in reinforcement learning to establish the learned skill objectives and guide the agent toward the optimal policy. Since autonomous driving is a complex domain with partly conflicting objectives with varying degrees of priority, developing a suitable reward function represents a fundamental challenge. This paper aims to highlight the gap in such function design by assessing different proposed formulations in the literature and dividing individual objectives into Safety, Comfort, Progress, and Traffic Rules compliance categories. Additionally, the limitations of the reviewed reward functions are discussed, such as objectives aggregation and indifference to driving context. Furthermore, the reward categories are frequently inadequately formulated and lack standardization. This paper concludes by proposing future research that potentially addresses the observed shortcomings in rewards, including a reward validation framework and structured rewards that are context-aware and able to resolve conflicts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自动驾驶强化学习中奖励函数综述
强化学习已成为自动驾驶领域的重要方法。奖励函数在强化学习中用于设定学习技能目标并引导智能体获得最优策略。由于自动驾驶是一个复杂领域，其目标部分冲突且优先级各异，设计合适的奖励函数构成了一项根本性挑战。本文通过评估文献中提出的不同奖励函数形式，将具体目标划分为安全性、舒适性、行驶效率与交通规则遵守四大类别，旨在揭示该领域函数设计的不足。同时，本文讨论了现有奖励函数的局限性，如目标聚合方式单一、对驾驶情境缺乏敏感性等问题。此外，现有奖励类别常存在定义不充分且缺乏标准化的问题。最后，本文提出未来研究方向，包括建立奖励函数验证框架、设计具有情境感知能力并能解决目标冲突的结构化奖励函数，以弥补当前研究的不足。

Self-adapting Robotic Agents through Online Continual Reinforcement Learning with World Model Feedback
Authors: Fabian Domberg, Georg Schildbach
Venue: IROS 2026
First: 2026-03-04T13:07:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T13:07:42+00:00
Comments: submitted to IROS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As learning-based robotic controllers are typically trained offline and deployed with fixed parameters, their ability to cope with unforeseen changes during operation is limited. Biologically inspired, this work presents a framework for online Continual Reinforcement Learning that enables automated adaptation during deployment. Building on DreamerV3, a model-based Reinforcement Learning algorithm, the proposed method leverages world model prediction residuals to detect out-of-distribution events and automatically trigger finetuning. Adaptation progress is monitored using both task-level performance signals and internal training metrics, allowing convergence to be assessed without external supervision and domain knowledge. The approach is validated on a variety of contemporary continuous control problems, including a quadruped robot in high-fidelity simulation, and a real-world model vehicle. Relevant metrics and their interpretation are presented and discussed, as well as resulting trade-offs described. The results sketch out how autonomous robotic agents could once move beyond static training regimes toward adaptive systems capable of self-reflection and -improvement during operation, just like their biological counterparts.

Discriminative Perception via Anchored Description for Reasoning Segmentation
Authors: Tao Yang, Qing Zhou, Yanliang Li, Qi Wang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-04T12:46:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T12:46:27+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reasoning segmentation increasingly employs reinforcement learning to generate explanatory reasoning chains that guide Multimodal Large Language Models. While these geometric rewards are primarily confined to guiding the final localization, they are incapable of discriminating whether the reasoning process remains anchored on the referred region or strays into irrelevant context. Lacking this discriminative guidance, the model's reasoning often devolves into unfocused and verbose chains that ultimately fail to disambiguate and perceive the target in complex scenes. This suggests a need to complement the RL objective with Discriminative Perception, an ability to actively distinguish a target from its context. To realize this, we propose DPAD to compel the model to generate a descriptive caption of the referred object, which is then used to explicitly discriminate by contrasting the caption's semantic relevance to the referred object against the wider context. By optimizing for this discriminative capability, the model is forced to focus on the unique attributes of the target, leading to a more converged and efficient reasoning chain. The descriptive caption also serves as an interpretability rationale that aligns with the segmentation. Experiments on the benchmarks confirm the validity of our approach, delivering substantial performance gains, with the cIoU on ReasonSeg increasing by 3.09% and the reasoning chain length decreasing by approximately 42%. Code is available at https://github.com/mrazhou/DPAD
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于锚定描述的判别感知用于推理分割
推理分割领域日益采用强化学习生成解释性推理链以指导多模态大语言模型。然而，这类几何奖励主要局限于指导最终定位，无法判别推理过程是否始终锚定于所指区域或偏离至无关上下文。缺乏此类判别性引导，模型推理常退化为散漫冗长的链条，最终难以在复杂场景中消歧并感知目标。这表明需要为强化学习目标补充判别感知能力——即主动区分目标与其上下文的能力。为实现此目标，我们提出DPAD方法，强制模型生成所指对象的描述性标题，随后通过对比该标题与所指对象及更广上下文的语义相关性进行显式判别。通过优化此判别能力，模型被迫聚焦于目标的独特属性，从而产生更收敛高效的推理链。描述性标题同时可作为与分割结果对齐的可解释性依据。基准测试实验证实了本方法的有效性：ReasonSeg数据集上的cIoU指标提升3.09%，推理链长度减少约42%。代码发布于https://github.com/mrazhou/DPAD

The paper addresses a limitation in reasoning segmentation where reinforcement learning rewards focus on final localization but fail to ensure the reasoning process stays anchored to the target region, leading to verbose and unfocused chains. To tackle this, the authors propose DPAD, a method that compels the model to generate a descriptive caption of the referred object and then uses it to discriminate the target from its context by contrasting semantic relevance. This approach forces the model to focus on unique attributes, resulting in more converged and efficient reasoning. Experimental results on benchmarks show substantial gains, including a 3.09% increase in cIoU on ReasonSeg and a 42% reduction in reasoning chain length.
本文针对推理分割中的局限性提出改进，现有强化学习奖励主要关注最终定位，但无法确保推理过程始终锚定目标区域，导致冗长且不聚焦的推理链。为此，作者提出DPAD方法，强制模型生成被指代对象的描述性标题，并通过对比其与目标及背景的语义相关性来明确区分目标。这种方法迫使模型关注目标的独特属性，从而产生更收敛和高效的推理。在基准测试上的实验证实了该方法的有效性，在ReasonSeg上cIoU提升了3.09%，同时推理链长度减少了约42%。
Training High-Level Schedulers with Execution-Feedback Reinforcement Learning for Long-Horizon GUI Automation
Authors: Zehao Deng, Tianjie Ju, Zheng Wu, Zhuosheng Zhang, Gongshen Liu
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-11-27T09:01:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T12:15:06+00:00
Comments: Accepted to CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The rapid development of large vision-language model (VLM) has greatly promoted the research of GUI agent. However, GUI agents still face significant challenges in handling long-horizon tasks. First, single-agent models struggle to balance high-level capabilities and low-level execution capability, facing prevalent issues of responsibility coupling and capability conflicts. Second, agents lack awareness of the task state, leading to progress loss in long-horizon tasks. To address these challenges, we propose a staged execution-feedback reinforcement learning algorithm. Unlike training a unified policy model, we focus on training high-level scheduling models. Specifically, we propose and train two agents: a Coordinator, responsible for the strategic planning and task decomposition; and a State Tracker, responsible for context compression and information management to maintain the task's state and coherence. Based on this, we built the Coordinator-Executor-State Tracker (CES) multi-agent framework, which can be integrated with any low-level Executor model, assisting the Executor in solving long-horizon tasks through task scheduling and state management. Experiments on long-horizon task benchmarks demonstrate that CES significantly enhances the system's planning and state management capabilities. Furthermore, analysis confirms that our trained high-level scheduling module is a generalizable, plug-and-play module that significantly enhances the long-horizon capabilities of various Executors. Code can be available at https://github.com/hehehahi4/CES.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于执行反馈强化学习训练高层调度器实现长程GUI自动化
大规模视觉语言模型（VLM）的快速发展极大推动了GUI智能体的研究。然而，GUI智能体在处理长程任务时仍面临重大挑战：其一，单智能体模型难以平衡高层规划能力与底层执行能力，普遍存在职责耦合与能力冲突问题；其二，智能体缺乏任务状态感知能力，导致长程任务中的进度丢失。为应对这些挑战，我们提出一种分阶段的执行反馈强化学习算法。区别于训练统一策略模型，我们专注于训练高层调度模型。具体而言，我们提出并训练两种智能体：负责战略规划与任务分解的协调器（Coordinator），以及负责上下文压缩与信息管理以维持任务状态与连贯性的状态追踪器（State Tracker）。在此基础上，我们构建了协调器-执行器-状态追踪器（CES）多智能体框架，该框架可与任意底层执行器模型集成，通过任务调度与状态管理协助执行器解决长程任务。在长程任务基准测试上的实验表明，CES显著提升了系统的规划与状态管理能力。进一步分析证实，我们训练的高层调度模块具有通用性，可作为即插即用模块显著增强各类执行器的长程任务处理能力。代码发布于https://github.com/hehehahi4/CES。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenges that GUI agents face in long-horizon tasks, such as balancing high-level planning with low-level execution and lacking task state awareness, this paper introduces a staged execution-feedback reinforcement learning method to train high-level scheduling models. The method proposes a multi-agent framework called Coordinator-Executor-State Tracker (CES), which includes a Coordinator for strategic planning and task decomposition and a State Tracker for context compression and information management to maintain task coherence, both designed to work with any low-level Executor. Experimental results on long-horizon benchmarks show that CES significantly improves planning and state management capabilities, and analysis confirms that the trained high-level scheduling module is a generalizable, plug-and-play component that enhances the long-horizon performance of various Executors.
针对GUI智能体在长周期任务中面临高、低层能力难以平衡且缺乏任务状态感知的挑战，本文提出了一种分阶段的执行反馈强化学习方法来训练高层调度模型。该方法构建了一个名为协调器-执行器-状态跟踪器（CES）的多智能体框架，其中协调器负责战略规划与任务分解，状态跟踪器负责上下文压缩与信息管理以维持任务连贯性，两者均可与任意低层执行器模型集成。在长周期任务基准测试上的实验结果表明，CES显著提升了系统的规划与状态管理能力，且分析证实训练得到的高层调度模块是一个通用、即插即用的组件，能有效增强不同执行器的长周期任务处理性能。
Black Box Meta-Learning Intrinsic Rewards
Authors: Octavio Pappalardo, Rodrigo Ramele, Juan Miguel Santos
First: 2024-07-31T12:09:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T11:49:12+00:00
Comments: Improved exposition; no technical changes to content
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The broader application of reinforcement learning (RL) is limited by challenges including data efficiency, generalization capability, and ability to learn in sparse-reward environments. Meta-learning has emerged as a promising approach to address these issues by optimizing components of the learning algorithm to meet desired characteristics. Additionally, a different line of work has extensively studied the use of intrinsic rewards to enhance the exploration capabilities of algorithms. This work investigates how meta-learning can improve the training signal received by RL agents. We introduce a method to learn intrinsic rewards within a reinforcement learning framework that bypasses the typical computation of meta-gradients through an optimization process by treating policy updates as black boxes. We validate our approach against training with extrinsic rewards, demonstrating its effectiveness, and additionally compare it to the use of a meta-learned advantage function. Experiments are carried out on distributions of continuous control tasks with both parametric and non-parametric variations. Furthermore, only sparse rewards are used during evaluation. Code is available at: https: //github.com/Octavio-Pappalardo/Meta-learning-rewards
中文标题/摘要
标题：黑盒元学习内在奖励机制
强化学习（RL）的广泛应用受限于数据效率、泛化能力及稀疏奖励环境下的学习能力等挑战。元学习通过优化学习算法的组件以满足期望特性，已成为解决这些问题的有效途径。与此同时，另一研究方向深入探索了利用内在奖励增强算法探索能力的方法。本研究探讨元学习如何改进RL智能体接收的训练信号，提出一种在强化学习框架内学习内在奖励的方法：将策略更新视为黑盒，通过优化过程规避元梯度的典型计算流程。实验通过对比外在奖励训练验证了该方法的有效性，并与元学习优势函数的使用进行了比较。研究在参数化与非参数化变体的连续控制任务分布上进行测试，且评估阶段仅使用稀疏奖励。代码已开源：https://github.com/Octavio-Pappalardo/Meta-learning-rewards
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of reinforcement learning in data efficiency, generalization, and sparse-reward environments, this paper proposes a meta-learning method to enhance training signals by learning intrinsic rewards. The method treats policy updates as black boxes, bypassing explicit meta-gradient computation, to optimize intrinsic rewards within an RL framework. Experimental results on continuous control task distributions, using only sparse rewards during evaluation, demonstrate the approach's effectiveness over extrinsic reward training and a meta-learned advantage function baseline.
针对强化学习在数据效率、泛化能力和稀疏奖励环境中的局限性，本文提出一种元学习方法，通过学习内在奖励来增强训练信号。该方法将策略更新视为黑箱，绕过显式的元梯度计算，在强化学习框架内优化内在奖励。在连续控制任务分布上的实验结果表明，该方法在仅使用稀疏奖励进行评估时，优于外在奖励训练和元学习优势函数基线，验证了其有效性。
GIPO: Gaussian Importance Sampling Policy Optimization
Authors: Chengxuan Lu, Zhenquan Zhang, Shukuan Wang, Qunzhi Lin, Baigui Sun, Yang Liu
First: 2026-03-04T11:34:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T11:34:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Post-training with reinforcement learning (RL) has recently shown strong promise for advancing multimodal agents beyond supervised imitation. However, RL remains limited by poor data efficiency, particularly in settings where interaction data are scarce and quickly become outdated. To address this challenge, GIPO (Gaussian Importance sampling Policy Optimization) is proposed as a policy optimization objective based on truncated importance sampling, replacing hard clipping with a log-ratio-based Gaussian trust weight to softly damp extreme importance ratios while maintaining non-zero gradients. Theoretical analysis shows that GIPO introduces an implicit, tunable constraint on the update magnitude, while concentration bounds guarantee robustness and stability under finite-sample estimation. Experimental results show that GIPO achieves state-of-the-art performance among clipping-based baselines across a wide range of replay buffer sizes, from near on-policy to highly stale data, while exhibiting superior bias--variance trade-off, high training stability and improved sample efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GIPO：高斯重要性采样策略优化
强化学习（RL）的后训练近期展现出推动多模态智能体超越监督式模仿学习的巨大潜力。然而，RL仍受限于数据效率低下，尤其在交互数据稀缺且快速过时的场景中。为应对这一挑战，本文提出GIPO（高斯重要性采样策略优化），这是一种基于截断重要性采样的策略优化目标，通过基于对数比的高斯信任权重替代硬截断，以柔和地抑制极端重要性比率，同时保持非零梯度。理论分析表明，GIPO对更新幅度引入了隐式可调约束，而集中性界限保证了有限样本估计下的鲁棒性与稳定性。实验结果显示，GIPO在基于截断的基线方法中实现了最优性能，适用于从近同策略到高度陈旧数据的广泛经验回放缓冲区规模，同时展现出更优的偏差-方差权衡、高训练稳定性及改进的样本效率。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the data inefficiency of reinforcement learning in post-training for multimodal agents, particularly when interaction data is scarce and quickly outdated. It proposes GIPO, a policy optimization method that uses truncated importance sampling with a log-ratio-based Gaussian trust weight to softly damp extreme importance ratios while preserving non-zero gradients, theoretically ensuring robust and stable updates via implicit constraints. Experiments demonstrate that GIPO achieves state-of-the-art performance across varying replay buffer sizes, from near on-policy to stale data, with superior bias-variance trade-off, high training stability, and improved sample efficiency compared to clipping-based baselines.
该论文针对强化学习在多模态智能体后训练中的数据效率低下问题，特别是在交互数据稀缺且快速过时的场景下，提出了GIPO方法。该方法基于截断重要性采样，采用对数比高斯信任权重来柔和抑制极端重要性比率，同时保持非零梯度，理论分析表明其引入了可调隐式约束以确保有限样本估计下的鲁棒性和稳定性。实验结果显示，GIPO在从近在线到高度陈旧数据的不同回放缓冲区大小下，均优于基于剪裁的基线方法，实现了最佳的偏差-方差权衡、高训练稳定性和更高的样本效率。
RVN-Bench: A Benchmark for Reactive Visual Navigation
Authors: Jaewon Lee, Jaeseok Heo, Gunmin Lee, Howoong Jun, Jeongwoo Oh, Songhwai Oh
First: 2026-03-04T11:26:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T11:26:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Safe visual navigation is critical for indoor mobile robots operating in cluttered environments. Existing benchmarks, however, often neglect collisions or are designed for outdoor scenarios, making them unsuitable for indoor visual navigation. To address this limitation, we introduce the reactive visual navigation benchmark (RVN-Bench), a collision-aware benchmark for indoor mobile robots. In RVN-Bench, an agent must reach sequential goal positions in previously unseen environments using only visual observations and no prior map, while avoiding collisions. Built on the Habitat 2.0 simulator and leveraging high-fidelity HM3D scenes, RVN-Bench provides large-scale, diverse indoor environments, defines a collision-aware navigation task and evaluation metrics, and offers tools for standardized training and benchmarking. RVN-Bench supports both online and offline learning by offering an environment for online reinforcement learning, a trajectory image dataset generator, and tools for producing negative trajectory image datasets that capture collision events. Experiments show that policies trained on RVN-Bench generalize effectively to unseen environments, demonstrating its value as a standardized benchmark for safe and robust visual navigation. Code and additional materials are available at: https://rvn-bench.github.io/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RVN-Bench：反应式视觉导航基准测试

Dynamic Adversarial Reinforcement Learning for Robust Multimodal Large Language Models
Authors: Yicheng Bao, Xuhong Wang, Qiaosheng Zhang, Chaochao Lu, Xia Hu, Xin Tan
First: 2026-01-24T03:47:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T11:04:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite their impressive capabilities, Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) exhibit perceptual fragility when confronted with visually complex scenes. This weakness stems from a reliance on finite training datasets, which are prohibitively expensive to scale and impose a ceiling on model robustness. We introduce \textbf{AOT-SFT}, a large-scale adversarial dataset for bootstrapping MLLM robustness. Building on this, we propose \textbf{AOT (Adversarial Opponent Training)}, a self-play framework that forges MLLM robustness by creating its own training data. Our method orchestrates a co-evolution between an image-editing Attacker and a Defender MLLM, where the Attacker generates a diverse and dynamic curriculum of image manipulations, forcing the Defender to adapt and improve. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AOT enhances the Defender's perceptual robustness and reduces hallucinations, establishing a scalable paradigm for training more reliable MLLMs.

Selecting Offline Reinforcement Learning Algorithms for Stochastic Network Control
Authors: Nicolas Helson, Pegah Alizadeh, Anastasios Giovanidis
First: 2026-03-04T10:41:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T10:41:10+00:00
Comments: Long version 12 pages, double column including Appendix. Short version accepted at NOMS2026-IPSN, Rome, Italy
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline Reinforcement Learning (RL) is a promising approach for next-generation wireless networks, where online exploration is unsafe and large amounts of operational data can be reused across the model lifecycle. However, the behavior of offline RL algorithms under genuinely stochastic dynamics -- inherent to wireless systems due to fading, noise, and traffic mobility -- remains insufficiently understood. We address this gap by evaluating Bellman-based (Conservative Q-Learning), sequence-based (Decision Transformers), and hybrid (Critic-Guided Decision Transformers) offline RL methods in an open-access stochastic telecom environment (mobile-env). Our results show that Conservative Q-Learning consistently produces more robust policies across different sources of stochasticity, making it a reliable default choice in lifecycle-driven AI management frameworks. Sequence-based methods remain competitive and can outperform Bellman-based approaches when sufficient high-return trajectories are available. These findings provide practical guidance for offline RL algorithm selection in AI-driven network control pipelines, such as O-RAN and future 6G functions, where robustness and data availability are key operational constraints.
中文标题/摘要
标题：随机网络控制中离线强化学习算法的选择
离线强化学习是下一代无线网络的一种有前景的方法，其中在线探索不安全，且大量运营数据可在模型生命周期中重复使用。然而，对于离线强化学习算法在真实随机动态下的行为——由于衰落、噪声和流量移动性而成为无线系统固有特性——仍缺乏充分理解。我们通过在开放随机电信环境（mobile-env）中评估基于贝尔曼的（保守Q学习）、基于序列的（决策变换器）和混合（评论家引导决策变换器）离线强化学习方法来解决这一空白。结果表明，保守Q学习在不同随机性来源下始终产生更稳健的策略，使其成为生命周期驱动的AI管理框架中可靠的默认选择。当可获得足够高回报轨迹时，基于序列的方法仍具竞争力，并能超越基于贝尔曼的方法。这些发现为AI驱动的网络控制流程（如O-RAN和未来6G功能）中的离线强化学习算法选择提供了实用指导，其中稳健性和数据可用性是关键运营约束。

Joint Hardware-Workload Co-Optimization for In-Memory Computing Accelerators
Authors: Olga Krestinskaya, Mohammed E. Fouda, Ahmed Eltawil, Khaled N. Salama
First: 2026-03-04T09:32:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T09:32:06+00:00
Comments: Accepted to IEEE Access
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Software-hardware co-design is essential for optimizing in-memory computing (IMC) hardware accelerators for neural networks. However, most existing optimization frameworks target a single workload, leading to highly specialized hardware designs that do not generalize well across models and applications. In contrast, practical deployment scenarios require a single IMC platform that can efficiently support multiple neural network workloads. This work presents a joint hardware-workload co-optimization framework based on an optimized evolutionary algorithm for designing generalized IMC accelerator architectures. By explicitly capturing cross-workload trade-offs rather than optimizing for a single model, the proposed approach significantly reduces the performance gap between workload-specific and generalized IMC designs. The framework is evaluated on both RRAM- and SRAM-based IMC architectures, demonstrating strong robustness and adaptability across diverse design scenarios. Compared to baseline methods, the optimized designs achieve energy-delay-area product (EDAP) reductions of up to 76.2% and 95.5% when optimizing across a small set (4 workloads) and a large set (9 workloads), respectively. The source code of the framework is available at https://github.com/OlgaKrestinskaya/JointHardwareWorkloadOptimizationIMC.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向存内计算加速器的硬件-负载联合协同优化
软硬件协同设计对于优化面向神经网络的存内计算硬件加速器至关重要。然而，现有优化框架大多针对单一负载，导致硬件设计高度专用化，难以在不同模型与应用间泛化。实际部署场景则要求单一存内计算平台能高效支持多种神经网络负载。本研究提出一种基于优化进化算法的硬件-负载联合协同优化框架，用于设计通用化存内计算加速器架构。该方法通过显式捕获跨负载权衡而非针对单一模型优化，显著缩小了专用化与通用化存内计算设计间的性能差距。该框架在基于RRAM和SRAM的存内计算架构上均得到验证，展现出跨多样设计场景的强大鲁棒性与适应性。相较于基线方法，在小型负载集（4种负载）和大型负载集（9种负载）的优化中，所得设计分别实现了高达76.2%和95.5%的能耗-延迟-面积积降低。框架源代码发布于https://github.com/OlgaKrestinskaya/JointHardwareWorkloadOptimizationIMC。

QFlowNet: Fast, Diverse, and Efficient Unitary Synthesis with Generative Flow Networks
Authors: Inhoe Koo, Hyunho Cha, Jungwoo Lee
First: 2026-03-03T14:38:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T09:29:40+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 6 figures, IEEE International Conference on Quantum Communications, Networking, and Computing (QCNC 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unitary Synthesis, the decomposition of a unitary matrix into a sequence of quantum gates, is a fundamental challenge in quantum compilation. Prevailing reinforcement learning (RL) approaches are often hampered by sparse reward signals, which necessitate complex reward shaping or long training times, and typically converge to a single policy, lacking solution diversity. In this work, we propose QFlowNet, a novel framework that learns efficiently from sparse signals by pairing a Generative Flow Network (GFlowNet) with Transformers. Our approach addresses two key challenges. First, the GFlowNet framework is fundamentally designed to learn a diverse policy that samples solutions proportional to their reward, overcoming the single-solution limitation of RL while offering faster inference than other generative models like diffusion. Second, the Transformers act as a powerful encoder, capturing the non-local structure of unitary matrices and compressing a high-dimensional state into a dense latent representation for the policy network. Our agent achieves an overall success rate of 99.7% on a 3-qubit benchmark(lengths 1-12) and discovers a diverse set of compact circuits, establishing QFlowNet as an efficient and diverse paradigm for unitary synthesis.
中文标题/摘要
标题：QFlowNet：基于生成流网络实现快速、多样且高效的酉矩阵合成
酉矩阵合成——将酉矩阵分解为量子门序列——是量子编译领域的核心挑战。主流强化学习方法常受稀疏奖励信号制约，需复杂奖励塑形或长时训练，且通常收敛至单一策略，缺乏解多样性。本研究提出QFlowNet框架，通过将生成流网络与Transformer结合，实现从稀疏信号的高效学习。该方案解决两大关键问题：其一，生成流网络框架本质设计为学习按奖励比例采样解的多样化策略，克服强化学习的单解局限，同时比扩散模型等生成方法具有更快推理速度；其二，Transformer作为强大编码器，捕捉酉矩阵的非局部结构，将高维状态压缩为策略网络的稠密隐表示。智能体在3量子比特基准测试（长度1-12）中达成99.7%总成功率，并发现多样化紧凑电路，确立QFlowNet作为高效且多样化的酉矩阵合成范式。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of unitary synthesis in quantum compilation, where existing reinforcement learning methods suffer from sparse rewards and limited solution diversity. The proposed QFlowNet method combines a Generative Flow Network (GFlowNet) with Transformers to efficiently learn from sparse signals, enabling diverse sampling of solutions proportional to reward and leveraging Transformers to encode the non-local structure of unitary matrices into dense latent representations. Experimental results show a 99.7% success rate on a 3-qubit benchmark with circuit lengths from 1 to 12, producing compact and diverse circuits, thus establishing QFlowNet as an efficient and diverse paradigm for unitary synthesis.
