Generative Recommendation for Large-Scale Advertising
Authors: Ben Xue, Dan Liu, Lixiang Wang, Mingjie Sun, Peng Wang, Pengfei Zhang, Shaoyun Shi, Tianyu Xu, Yunhao Sha, Zhiqiang Liu, Bo Kong, Bo Wang, Hang Yang, Jieting Xue, Junhao Wang, Shengyu Wang, Shuping Hui, Wencai Ye, Xiao Lin, Yongzhi Li, Yuhang Chen, Zhihui Yin, Quan Chen, Shiyang Wen, Wenjin Wu, Han Li, Guorui Zhou, Changcheng Li, Peng Jiang
First: 2026-02-26T08:15:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T09:28:17+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 6 figures, under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative recommendation has recently attracted widespread attention in industry due to its potential for scaling and stronger model capacity. However, deploying real-time generative recommendation in large-scale advertising requires designs beyond large-language-model (LLM)-style training and serving recipes. We present a production-oriented generative recommender co-designed across architecture, learning, and serving, named GR4AD (Generative Recommendation for ADdvertising). As for tokenization, GR4AD proposes UA-SID (Unified Advertisement Semantic ID) to capture complicated business information. Furthermore, GR4AD introduces LazyAR, a lazy autoregressive decoder that relaxes layer-wise dependencies for short, multi-candidate generation, preserving effectiveness while reducing inference cost, which facilitates scaling under fixed serving budgets. To align optimization with business value, GR4AD employs VSL (Value-Aware Supervised Learning) and proposes RSPO (Ranking-Guided Softmax Preference Optimization), a ranking-aware, list-wise reinforcement learning algorithm that optimizes value-based rewards under list-level metrics for continual online updates. For online inference, we further propose dynamic beam serving, which adapts beam width across generation levels and online load to control compute. Large-scale online A/B tests show up to 4.2% ad revenue improvement over an existing DLRM-based stack, with consistent gains from both model scaling and inference-time scaling. GR4AD has been fully deployed in Kuaishou advertising system with over 400 million users and achieves high-throughput real-time serving.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大规模广告的生成式推荐
生成式推荐因其可扩展性和更强的模型能力，近期在工业界受到广泛关注。然而，在大规模广告中部署实时生成式推荐需要超越大语言模型（LLM）式训练与服务方案的设计。我们提出了一种面向生产的生成式推荐系统GR4AD（面向广告的生成式推荐），在架构、学习与服务层面进行协同设计。在标记化方面，GR4AD提出UA-SID（统一广告语义标识）以捕捉复杂的业务信息。此外，GR4AD引入LazyAR，一种惰性自回归解码器，通过放松层间依赖关系来支持短序列多候选生成，在保持效果的同时降低推理成本，从而在固定服务预算下促进扩展。为使优化与业务价值对齐，GR4AD采用VSL（价值感知监督学习），并提出RSPO（排序引导的Softmax偏好优化）——一种排序感知的列表式强化学习算法，可在列表级指标下优化基于价值的奖励，支持持续在线更新。对于在线推理，我们进一步提出动态束搜索服务，通过在不同生成层级和在线负载间自适应调整束宽来控制计算量。大规模在线A/B测试显示，相较于现有基于DLRM的架构，广告收入提升最高达4.2%，模型扩展和推理时扩展均带来持续收益。GR4AD已在拥有超4亿用户的快手广告系统全面部署，实现了高吞吐实时服务。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to deploy real-time generative recommendation in large-scale advertising beyond standard LLM approaches, this paper introduces GR4AD, a production-oriented system co-designed across architecture, learning, and serving. The method employs a Unified Advertisement Semantic ID (UA-SID) for tokenization, a Lazy Autoregressive (LazyAR) decoder for efficient multi-candidate generation, and a ranking-aware reinforcement learning algorithm called RSPO for value-aligned optimization. Main experimental results from large-scale online A/B tests demonstrate up to a 4.2% improvement in ad revenue compared to a DLRM-based baseline, with consistent gains from model and inference scaling, and the system has been fully deployed serving over 400 million users.
本文旨在解决大规模广告中实时生成式推荐部署的挑战，提出了一个面向生产的系统GR4AD，其在架构、学习和服务端协同设计。方法上采用统一广告语义ID进行表征，引入惰性自回归解码器以降低推理成本，并提出了基于排序的强化学习算法RSPO进行价值对齐优化。主要实验结果表明，通过大规模在线A/B测试，相比基于DLRM的现有系统，广告收入提升最高达4.2%，且模型和推理扩展均带来稳定收益，该系统已全面部署于拥有超过4亿用户的快手广告平台。
Fairness Begins with State: Purifying Latent Preferences for Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning in Interactive Recommendation
Authors: Yun Lu, Xiaoyu Shi, Hong Xie, Xiangyu Zhao, Mingsheng Shang
First: 2026-03-04T08:14:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T08:14:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Interactive recommender systems (IRS) are increasingly optimized with Reinforcement Learning (RL) to capture the sequential nature of user-system dynamics. However, existing fairness-aware methods often suffer from a fundamental oversight: they assume the observed user state is a faithful representation of true preferences. In reality, implicit feedback is contaminated by popularity-driven noise and exposure bias, creating a distorted state that misleads the RL agent. We argue that the persistent conflict between accuracy and fairness is not merely a reward-shaping issue, but a state estimation failure. In this work, we propose \textbf{DSRM-HRL}, a framework that reformulates fairness-aware recommendation as a latent state purification problem followed by decoupled hierarchical decision-making. We introduce a Denoising State Representation Module (DSRM) based on diffusion models to recover the low-entropy latent preference manifold from high-entropy, noisy interaction histories. Built upon this purified state, a Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning (HRL) agent is employed to decouple conflicting objectives: a high-level policy regulates long-term fairness trajectories, while a low-level policy optimizes short-term engagement under these dynamic constraints. Extensive experiments on high-fidelity simulators (KuaiRec, KuaiRand) demonstrate that DSRM-HRL effectively breaks the "rich-get-richer" feedback loop, achieving a superior Pareto frontier between recommendation utility and exposure equity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：公平始于状态：交互式推荐中层次强化学习的潜在偏好净化
交互式推荐系统（IRS）日益采用强化学习（RL）进行优化，以捕捉用户-系统动态的序列特性。然而，现有公平性方法常存在根本性疏忽：它们假设观测到的用户状态能真实反映其偏好。实际上，隐式反馈受流行度噪声和曝光偏差污染，形成误导RL智能体的失真状态。我们认为，准确性与公平性间的持续冲突不仅是奖励塑造问题，更是状态估计失效。本文提出\textbf{DSRM-HRL}框架，将公平性推荐重构为潜在状态净化问题，并采用解耦的层次化决策。我们基于扩散模型设计去噪状态表示模块（DSRM），从高熵噪声交互历史中恢复低熵潜在偏好流形。在此净化状态基础上，采用层次强化学习（HRL）智能体解耦冲突目标：高层策略调控长期公平性轨迹，低层策略在动态约束下优化短期参与度。在高保真模拟器（KuaiRec、KuaiRand）上的大量实验表明，DSRM-HRL能有效打破“富者愈富”反馈循环，在推荐效用与曝光公平性间实现更优的帕累托前沿。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the persistent accuracy-fairness trade-off in interactive recommender systems by arguing that the conflict stems from biased state estimation, not just reward shaping. The proposed DSRM-HRL framework first purifies latent user preferences from noisy interaction data using a diffusion-based denoising module, then employs a hierarchical RL agent where a high-level policy manages long-term fairness and a low-level policy optimizes short-term engagement. Experiments on simulators show the method breaks the "rich-get-richer" loop and achieves a better Pareto frontier between utility and exposure equity.
本文针对交互式推荐系统中长期存在的准确性与公平性权衡问题，提出冲突源于有偏的状态估计而非仅是奖励塑造。所提出的DSRM-HRL框架首先使用基于扩散模型的去噪模块从噪声交互数据中净化潜在用户偏好，然后采用分层强化学习代理，其中高层策略管理长期公平性，低层策略在动态约束下优化短期参与度。在模拟器上的实验表明，该方法打破了“富者愈富”的反馈循环，并在推荐效用和曝光公平性之间实现了更优的帕累托前沿。
ToolRLA: Multiplicative Reward Decomposition for Tool-Integrated Agents
Authors: Pengbo Liu
First: 2026-03-02T08:52:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T07:26:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-integrated agents that interleave reasoning with API calls are promising for complex tasks, yet aligning them for high-stakes, domain-specific deployment remains challenging: existing reinforcement learning approaches rely on coarse binary rewards that cannot distinguish tool selection errors from malformed parameters. We present ToolRLA, a three-stage post-training pipeline (SFT $\rightarrow$ GRPO $\rightarrow$ DPO) for domain-specific tool agents. The core contribution is a fine-grained reward function with multiplicative correctness decomposition spanning four dimensions -- format validity, tool selection, parameter accuracy, and regulatory compliance -- that encodes domain priority orderings as inductive biases in the reward landscape. Deployed on a financial advisory copilot (80+ advisors, 1,200+ daily queries), ToolRLA achieves over three months: a 47\% improvement in task completion rate ($62\%\rightarrow91\%$), a 63\% reduction in tool invocation errors ($38\%\rightarrow14\%$), and a 93\% reduction in regulatory violations ($12\%\rightarrow0.8\%$), within sub-2-second latency. Ablation studies show the multiplicative reward design accounts for 7 percentage points of improvement over additive alternatives. Generalization is further validated on ToolBench and API-Bank.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ToolRLA：面向工具集成智能体的乘性奖励分解方法
交替进行推理与API调用的工具集成智能体在处理复杂任务方面前景广阔，但针对高风险领域特定场景的对齐部署仍具挑战：现有强化学习方法依赖粗粒度的二元奖励机制，无法区分工具选择错误与参数格式错误。本文提出ToolRLA——面向领域特定工具智能体的三阶段后训练流程（监督微调→分组相对策略优化→直接偏好优化）。核心贡献在于构建了具有乘性正确性分解特性的细粒度奖励函数，涵盖格式有效性、工具选择、参数准确性和合规性四个维度，通过将领域优先级顺序编码为奖励空间的归纳偏置。在金融顾问协理系统（覆盖80+顾问，日均1200+查询）的部署实践中，ToolRLA在三个月内实现：任务完成率提升47%（62%→91%），工具调用错误减少63%（38%→14%），违规操作降低93%（12%→0.8%），且响应延迟低于2秒。消融实验表明乘性奖励设计较加性方案带来7个百分点的性能提升。该方法在ToolBench和API-Bank基准测试中进一步验证了泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of aligning tool-integrated agents for high-stakes, domain-specific tasks, where existing reinforcement learning methods rely on coarse binary rewards that fail to distinguish between different error types. The authors propose ToolRLA, a three-stage post-training pipeline (SFT → GRPO → DPO) featuring a fine-grained reward function with multiplicative decomposition across four dimensions: format validity, tool selection, parameter accuracy, and regulatory compliance, which encodes domain priorities as inductive biases. Experimental results from deployment on a financial advisory copilot show significant improvements over three months, including a 47% increase in task completion rate (62% to 91%), a 63% reduction in tool invocation errors (38% to 14%), and a 93% reduction in regulatory violations (12% to 0.8%), with sub-2-second latency, while ablation studies confirm the superiority of multiplicative rewards over additive alternatives, and generalization is validated on benchmarks like ToolBench and API-Bank.
本文针对高风险、特定领域任务中工具集成智能体的对齐挑战，现有强化学习方法依赖粗糙的二元奖励，无法区分工具选择错误与参数格式错误。作者提出了ToolRLA，一个包含三阶段后训练流程（SFT → GRPO → DPO）的方法，其核心是细粒度奖励函数，通过乘法分解覆盖四个维度：格式有效性、工具选择、参数准确性和合规性，将领域优先级作为归纳偏置编码到奖励中。在金融顾问助手的实际部署中，三个月内的实验结果显示任务完成率提升47%（从62%到91%），工具调用错误减少63%（从38%到14%），违规行为降低93%（从12%到0.8%），且延迟低于2秒；消融研究表明乘法奖励设计比加法替代方案带来7个百分点的改进，并在ToolBench和API-Bank等基准上验证了泛化能力。
When Silence Is Golden: Can LLMs Learn to Abstain in Temporal QA and Beyond?
Authors: Xinyu Zhou, Chang Jin, Carsten Eickhoff, Zhijiang Guo, Seyed Ali Bahrainian
First: 2026-02-04T16:54:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T06:39:07+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) rarely admit uncertainty, often producing fluent but misleading answers, rather than abstaining (i.e., refusing to answer). This weakness is even evident in temporal question answering, where models frequently ignore time-sensitive evidence and conflate facts across different time-periods. In this paper, we present the first empirical study of training LLMs with an abstention ability while reasoning about temporal QA. Existing approaches such as calibration might be unreliable in capturing uncertainty in complex reasoning. We instead frame abstention as a teachable skill and introduce a pipeline that couples Chain-of-Thought (CoT) supervision with Reinforcement Learning (RL) guided by abstention-aware rewards. Our goal is to systematically analyze how different information types and training techniques affect temporal reasoning with abstention behavior in LLMs. Through extensive experiments studying various methods, we find that RL yields strong empirical gains on reasoning: a model initialized by Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct surpasses GPT-4o by $3.46\%$ and $5.80\%$ in Exact Match on TimeQA-Easy and Hard, respectively. Moreover, it improves the True Positive rate on unanswerable questions by $20\%$ over a pure supervised fine-tuned (SFT) variant. Beyond performance, our analysis shows that SFT induces overconfidence and harms reliability, while RL improves prediction accuracy but exhibits similar risks. Finally, by comparing implicit reasoning cues (e.g., original context, temporal sub-context, knowledge graphs) with explicit CoT supervision, we find that implicit information provides limited benefit for reasoning with abstention. Our study provides new insights into how abstention and reasoning can be jointly optimized, providing a foundation for building more reliable LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：沉默是金：大语言模型能否在时序问答及其他任务中学会弃答？
大语言模型（LLMs）很少承认不确定性，常生成流畅但误导性的答案而非选择弃答（即拒绝回答）。这一缺陷在时序问答中尤为明显：模型常忽略时效性证据，混淆不同时期的事实。本文首次实证研究了在时序问答推理中训练LLMs弃答能力的方法。现有方法（如校准）在捕捉复杂推理的不确定性时可能不可靠。我们将弃答构建为可教授技能，提出一种结合思维链监督与弃答感知奖励强化学习的训练框架。旨在系统分析不同信息类型与训练技术如何影响LLMs的时序推理弃答行为。通过多方法实验发现：强化学习显著提升推理性能——基于Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct初始化的模型在TimeQA-Easy/Hard数据集上的精确匹配率分别超越GPT-4o达3.46%和5.80%；对不可答问题的真阳性率较纯监督微调基线提升20%。分析表明：监督微调易引发过度自信损害可靠性，强化学习虽提升预测精度但存在类似风险。通过对比隐式推理线索（原始上下文、时序子语境、知识图谱）与显式思维链监督，发现隐式信息对弃答推理的助益有限。本研究为联合优化弃答与推理机制提供了新见解，为构建更可靠的LLMs奠定基础。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the problem that large language models (LLMs) often produce confidently wrong answers instead of abstaining when uncertain, particularly in temporal question answering where they conflate facts across time periods. The authors frame abstention as a teachable skill and introduce a training pipeline combining Chain-of-Thought supervision with Reinforcement Learning using abstention-aware rewards to jointly optimize reasoning and abstention behavior. Experimental results show that their RL-trained model, based on Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct, outperforms GPT-4o on TimeQA benchmarks and improves the true positive rate on unanswerable questions by 20% compared to supervised fine-tuning alone, though analysis reveals that both SFT and RL can induce overconfidence, and implicit reasoning cues provide limited benefit for abstention.
本文针对大语言模型在不确定时经常产生自信但错误的答案而非选择弃答的问题展开研究，特别是在时序问答中，模型容易混淆不同时期的事实。作者将弃答能力构建为一种可学习的技能，提出了一种结合思维链监督和基于弃答感知奖励的强化学习的训练流程，以联合优化推理和弃答行为。实验结果表明，基于Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct的强化学习训练模型在TimeQA基准上超越了GPT-4o，并在不可回答问题上的真阳性率比纯监督微调模型提高了20%，不过分析也表明监督微调和强化学习都可能引发过度自信，且隐式推理线索对弃答能力的提升有限。
Learning Approximate Nash Equilibria in Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning via Mean-Field Subsampling
Authors: Emile Anand, Ishani Karmarkar
First: 2026-03-04T06:14:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T06:14:24+00:00
Comments: 48 pages, 4 figures, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many large-scale platforms and networked control systems have a centralized decision maker interacting with a massive population of agents under strict observability constraints. Motivated by such applications, we study a cooperative Markov game with a global agent and $n$ homogeneous local agents in a communication-constrained regime, where the global agent only observes a subset of $k$ local agent states per time step. We propose an alternating learning framework $(\texttt{ALTERNATING-MARL})$, where the global agent performs subsampled mean-field $Q$-learning against a fixed local policy, and local agents update by optimizing in an induced MDP. We prove that these approximate best-response dynamics converge to an $\widetilde{O}(1/\sqrt{k})$-approximate Nash Equilibrium, while yielding a separation in the sample complexities between the joint state space and action space. Finally, we validate our results in numerical simulations for multi-robot control and federated optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过均值场子采样在合作多智能体强化学习中学习近似纳什均衡
许多大规模平台和网络控制系统存在集中决策者与海量智能体在严格可观测性约束下交互的场景。受此类应用驱动，本研究在通信受限机制下探讨包含全局智能体与$n$个同质局部智能体的合作马尔可夫博弈，其中全局智能体每时间步仅能观测$k$个局部智能体状态的子集。我们提出交替学习框架$(\texttt{ALTERNATING-MARL})$：全局智能体针对固定局部策略执行子采样均值场$Q$学习，局部智能体通过在诱导MDP中优化进行更新。理论证明该近似最优响应动态可收敛至$\widetilde{O}(1/\sqrt{k})$近似纳什均衡，同时在联合状态空间与动作空间之间产生样本复杂度分离。最后通过多机器人控制与联邦优化的数值仿真验证了理论结果。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by large-scale systems with centralized control and limited observability, this paper studies cooperative Markov games where a global agent can only observe a subset of many homogeneous local agents. The method introduces an alternating learning framework (ALTERNATING-MARL), where the global agent uses subsampled mean-field Q-learning against a fixed local policy, and local agents optimize within an induced MDP. Experimental results demonstrate convergence to an approximate Nash equilibrium with error scaling as O~(1/√k), showing a separation in sample complexity between state and action spaces, and the approach is validated in multi-robot control and federated optimization simulations.
本文针对具有集中控制但可观测性受限的大规模系统，研究了一个全局智能体仅能观测部分同质局部智能体的合作马尔可夫博弈。方法提出了一种交替学习框架（ALTERNATING-MARL），其中全局智能体使用子采样均值场Q学习来应对固定的局部策略，而局部智能体则在诱导的MDP中进行优化。实验结果表明，该方法能收敛到一个误差为O~(1/√k)的近似纳什均衡，显示了状态空间与动作空间在样本复杂度上的分离，并在多机器人控制和联邦优化仿真中得到了验证。
Confidence-Calibrated Small-Large Language Model Collaboration for Cost-Efficient Reasoning
Authors: Chuang Zhang, Zizhen Zhu, Yihao Wei, Bing Tian, Junyi Liu, Henan Wang, Xavier Wang, Yaxiao Liu
First: 2026-03-04T05:55:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:55:20+00:00
Comments: Accepted to EACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate superior reasoning capabilities compared to small language models (SLMs), but incur substantially higher costs. We propose COllaborative REAsoner (COREA), a system that cascades an SLM with an LLM to achieve a balance between accuracy and cost in complex reasoning tasks. COREA first attempts to answer questions using the SLM, which outputs both an answer and a verbalized confidence score. Questions with confidence below a predefined threshold are deferred to the LLM for more accurate resolution. We introduce a reinforcement learning-based training algorithm that aligns the SLM's confidence through an additional confidence calibration reward. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method jointly improves the SLM's reasoning ability and confidence calibration across diverse datasets and model backbones. Compared to using the LLM alone, COREA reduces cost by 21.5% and 16.8% on out-of-domain math and non-math datasets, respectively, with only an absolute pass@1 drop within 2%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于置信度校准的大小语言模型协作实现高性价比推理
大语言模型（LLM）相比小语言模型（SLM）具有更优的推理能力，但成本显著更高。我们提出协作推理器（COREA），该系统通过级联SLM与LLM，在复杂推理任务中实现准确性与成本的平衡。COREA首先尝试用SLM回答问题，SLM会同时输出答案和语言化置信度分数。置信度低于预设阈值的问题将交由LLM进行更精确求解。我们引入基于强化学习的训练算法，通过额外的置信度校准奖励来对齐SLM的置信度。大量实验表明，该方法能协同提升SLM在不同数据集和模型架构下的推理能力与置信度校准效果。与单独使用LLM相比，COREA在域外数学和非数学数据集上分别降低21.5%和16.8%的成本，而绝对pass@1指标下降幅度控制在2%以内。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high cost of large language models (LLMs) despite their superior reasoning, this paper introduces COREA, a collaborative system that cascades a small language model (SLM) with an LLM to balance accuracy and expense. The method involves the SLM first attempting to answer questions while outputting a verbalized confidence score; questions with confidence below a threshold are deferred to the LLM, and a reinforcement learning algorithm is used to calibrate the SLM's confidence via an additional reward. Experimental results show that COREA improves both the SLM's reasoning and confidence calibration across diverse datasets, reducing costs by 21.5% and 16.8% on out-of-domain math and non-math tasks respectively with only a minimal drop in accuracy.
本文的动机在于大型语言模型（LLM）虽然推理能力强但成本高昂，因此提出了COREA系统，通过级联小型语言模型（SLM）和LLM来平衡准确性与开销。方法上，SLM首先尝试回答问题并输出言语化的置信度分数，置信度低于阈值的问题则交由LLM处理，同时采用基于强化学习的训练算法，通过额外的置信度校准奖励来对齐SLM的置信度。主要实验结果表明，COREA在不同数据集和模型骨干上提升了SLM的推理能力和置信度校准，在域外数学和非数学数据集上分别降低了21.5%和16.8%的成本，而准确率仅略有下降。
Interaction-Aware Whole-Body Control for Compliant Object Transport
Authors: Hao Zhang, Yves Tseng, Ding Zhao, H. Eric Tseng
First: 2026-03-04T05:50:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:50:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Cooperative object transport in unstructured environments remains challenging for assistive humanoids because strong, time-varying interaction forces can make tracking-centric whole-body control unreliable, especially in close-contact support tasks. This paper proposes a bio-inspired, interaction-oriented whole-body control (IO-WBC) that functions as an artificial cerebellum - an adaptive motor agent that translates upstream (skill-level) commands into stable, physically consistent whole-body behavior under contact. This work structurally separates upper-body interaction execution from lower-body support control, enabling the robot to maintain balance while shaping force exchange in a tightly coupled robot-object system. A trajectory-optimized reference generator (RG) provides a kinematic prior, while a reinforcement learning (RL) policy governs body responses under heavy-load interactions and disturbances. The policy is trained in simulation with randomized payload mass/inertia and external perturbations, and deployed via asymmetric teacher-student distillation so that the student relies only on proprioceptive histories at runtime. Extensive experiments demonstrate that IO-WBC maintains stable whole-body behavior and physical interaction even when precise velocity tracking becomes infeasible, enabling compliant object transport across a wide range of scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向顺应性物体搬运的交互感知全身控制
在非结构化环境中进行协作式物体搬运对辅助型人形机器人仍具挑战性，因为强烈且时变的交互力会使以轨迹跟踪为核心的全身控制变得不可靠，尤其在紧密接触的支撑任务中。本文提出一种受生物启发的交互导向全身控制（IO-WBC），其功能类似于人工小脑——一个自适应运动代理，能将上游（技能层）指令转化为接触状态下稳定且物理一致的全身行为。该工作在结构上将上半身交互执行与下半身支撑控制分离，使机器人在紧密耦合的机器人-物体系统中保持平衡的同时调控力交换。轨迹优化的参考生成器提供运动学先验，而强化学习策略则主导重载交互与扰动下的身体响应。该策略在仿真环境中通过随机化负载质量/惯量和外部扰动进行训练，并通过非对称师生蒸馏进行部署，使学生策略在运行时仅依赖本体感知历史数据。大量实验表明，即使在精确速度跟踪无法实现时，IO-WBC仍能保持稳定的全身行为与物理交互，从而在广泛场景中实现顺应性物体搬运。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of reliable cooperative object transport by humanoid robots in unstructured environments, where strong, time-varying interaction forces can destabilize traditional tracking-centric whole-body controllers. The proposed method, Interaction-Oriented Whole-Body Control (IO-WBC), is a bio-inspired framework that structurally separates upper-body interaction execution from lower-body support, functioning like an artificial cerebellum to translate high-level commands into stable, physically consistent behavior under contact. It combines a trajectory-optimized reference generator with a reinforcement learning policy trained in simulation under randomized payloads and disturbances, which is then distilled into a student network using only proprioceptive history for deployment. Experimental results show that IO-WBC maintains stable whole-body behavior and compliant physical interaction even when precise velocity tracking is infeasible, enabling robust object transport across diverse scenarios.
本文针对人形机器人在非结构化环境中进行协作物体搬运的挑战，即强时变交互力易使传统以跟踪为核心的整体控制失稳的问题，提出了一种受生物启发的交互导向整体控制方法。该方法在结构上将上半身的交互执行与下半身的支撑控制分离，如同人工小脑般将上游技能指令转化为接触下的稳定、物理一致的整体行为，其结合了轨迹优化的参考生成器与在模拟中通过随机化负载和扰动训练得到的强化学习策略，并通过师生蒸馏部署为仅依赖本体感知历史的网络。大量实验表明，该方法在精确速度跟踪不可行时仍能保持稳定的整体行为与柔顺的物理交互，实现了广泛场景下的顺应性物体搬运。
HALyPO: Heterogeneous-Agent Lyapunov Policy Optimization for Human-Robot Collaboration
Authors: Hao Zhang, Yaru Niu, Yikai Wang, Ding Zhao, H. Eric Tseng
First: 2026-03-04T05:26:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:26:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
To improve generalization and resilience in human-robot collaboration (HRC), robots must handle the combinatorial diversity of human behaviors and contexts, motivating multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). However, inherent heterogeneity between robots and humans creates a rationality gap (RG) in the learning process-a variational mismatch between decentralized best-response dynamics and centralized cooperative ascent. The resulting learning problem is a general-sum differentiable game, so independent policy-gradient updates can oscillate or diverge without added structure. We propose heterogeneous-agent Lyapunov policy optimization (HALyPO), which establishes formal stability directly in the policy-parameter space by enforcing a per-step Lyapunov decrease condition on a parameter-space disagreement metric. Unlike Lyapunov-based safe RL, which targets state/trajectory constraints in constrained Markov decision processes, HALyPO uses Lyapunov certification to stabilize decentralized policy learning. HALyPO rectifies decentralized gradients via optimal quadratic projections, ensuring monotonic contraction of RG and enabling effective exploration of open-ended interaction spaces. Extensive simulations and real-world humanoid-robot experiments show that this certified stability improves generalization and robustness in collaborative corner cases.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HALyPO：面向人机协作的异构智能体李雅普诺夫策略优化
为提升人机协作的泛化性与鲁棒性，机器人需应对人类行为与情境的组合多样性，这推动了多智能体强化学习的应用。然而，机器人与人类间的内在异质性会在学习过程中产生理性鸿沟——即分散式最优响应动态与集中式协同上升间的变分失配。该学习问题本质上是广义和可微博弈，若无额外结构约束，独立策略梯度更新易出现振荡或发散。本文提出异构智能体李雅普诺夫策略优化方法，通过在参数空间分歧度量上强制实施步进式李雅普诺夫递减条件，直接在策略参数空间建立形式化稳定性。与基于李雅普诺夫的安全强化学习（针对约束马尔可夫决策过程的状态/轨迹约束）不同，HALyPO运用李雅普诺夫证明来稳定分散式策略学习。该方法通过最优二次投影修正分散式梯度，确保理性鸿沟的单调收缩，并支持对开放式交互空间的有效探索。大量仿真与真实人形机器人实验表明，这种经证明的稳定性显著提升了协作边缘场景中的泛化能力与鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need for robots to generalize and remain resilient in human-robot collaboration (HRC) despite the combinatorial diversity of human behaviors, which leads to a rationality gap (RG) due to heterogeneity between agents in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). To address this, the authors propose Heterogeneous-Agent Lyapunov Policy Optimization (HALyPO), a method that enforces a per-step Lyapunov decrease condition on a parameter-space disagreement metric to stabilize decentralized policy learning by rectifying gradients via optimal quadratic projections, ensuring monotonic contraction of RG. Experimental results from simulations and real-world humanoid-robot experiments demonstrate that this certified stability enhances generalization and robustness in collaborative corner cases.
本文的动机是，在人机协作（HRC）中，机器人需要泛化并保持韧性以应对人类行为的组合多样性，这导致多智能体强化学习（MARL）中因智能体异质性产生理性差距（RG）。为解决此问题，作者提出了异构智能体李雅普诺夫策略优化（HALyPO），该方法通过在参数空间分歧度量上强制每步李雅普诺夫递减条件，通过最优二次投影校正梯度，以稳定去中心化策略学习，确保RG单调收缩。仿真和真实世界人形机器人实验结果表明，这种经认证的稳定性提高了协作边缘案例中的泛化能力和鲁棒性。
AutoQD: Automatic Discovery of Diverse Behaviors with Quality-Diversity Optimization
Authors: Saeed Hedayatian, Stefanos Nikolaidis
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-05T23:34:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:24:53+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Quality-Diversity (QD) algorithms have shown remarkable success in discovering diverse, high-performing solutions, but rely heavily on hand-crafted behavioral descriptors that constrain exploration to predefined notions of diversity. Leveraging the equivalence between policies and occupancy measures, we present a theoretically grounded approach to automatically generate behavioral descriptors by embedding the occupancy measures of policies in Markov Decision Processes. Our method, AutoQD, leverages random Fourier features to approximate the Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD) between policy occupancy measures, creating embeddings whose distances reflect meaningful behavioral differences. A low-dimensional projection of these embeddings that captures the most behaviorally significant dimensions can then be used as behavioral descriptors for CMA-MAE, a state of the art blackbox QD method, to discover diverse policies. We prove that our embeddings converge to true MMD distances between occupancy measures as the number of sampled trajectories and embedding dimensions increase. Through experiments in multiple continuous control tasks we demonstrate AutoQD's ability in discovering diverse policies without predefined behavioral descriptors, presenting a well-motivated alternative to prior methods in unsupervised Reinforcement Learning and QD optimization. Our approach opens new possibilities for open-ended learning and automated behavior discovery in sequential decision making settings without requiring domain-specific knowledge. Source code is available at https://github.com/conflictednerd/autoqd-code.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AutoQD：基于质量多样性优化的多样化行为自动发现方法
质量多样性算法在发现多样化高性能解决方案方面成效显著，但严重依赖人工设计的行为描述符，将探索范围限制在预设的多样性概念中。基于策略与占用测度的等价性，我们提出一种理论完备的方法，通过嵌入马尔可夫决策过程中策略的占用测度来自动生成行为描述符。我们的方法AutoQD利用随机傅里叶特征逼近策略占用测度间的最大均值差异，构建能反映行为差异的嵌入表示。通过捕捉最具行为显著性的低维投影，这些嵌入可作为前沿黑箱QD方法CMA-MAE的行为描述符，用于发现多样化策略。我们证明随着轨迹采样数和嵌入维度的增加，该嵌入会收敛至占用测度的真实MMD距离。在多个连续控制任务中的实验表明，AutoQD无需预定义行为描述符即可发现多样化策略，为无监督强化学习和QD优化提供了理论完备的替代方案。该方法为序列决策场景中的开放式学习和自动化行为发现开辟了新途径，且无需领域先验知识。源代码发布于https://github.com/conflictednerd/autoqd-code。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of Quality-Diversity (QD) algorithms, which depend on hand-crafted behavioral descriptors that restrict exploration to predefined diversity notions. The method, AutoQD, automatically generates behavioral descriptors by embedding policy occupancy measures in Markov Decision Processes using random Fourier features to approximate Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD), creating embeddings whose distances reflect meaningful behavioral differences; these are then projected into a low-dimensional space for use with the CMA-MAE QD algorithm. Experimental results in continuous control tasks demonstrate AutoQD's ability to discover diverse policies without predefined descriptors, offering a theoretically grounded alternative for unsupervised reinforcement learning and QD optimization, thereby enabling open-ended learning without domain-specific knowledge.
本文针对质量多样性（QD）算法依赖手工设计行为描述符、限制探索预定义多样性概念的局限性，提出了一种自动生成行为描述符的方法。该方法名为AutoQD，通过嵌入马尔可夫决策过程中策略的占用测度，利用随机傅里叶特征近似最大均值差异（MMD），创建能反映行为差异的嵌入表示，并将其投影到低维空间以用于CMA-MAE QD算法。在连续控制任务中的实验结果表明，AutoQD能够在无需预定义描述符的情况下发现多样化的策略，为无监督强化学习和QD优化提供了理论依据充分的替代方案，从而实现了无需领域知识的开放式学习。
SHE: Stepwise Hybrid Examination Reinforcement Learning Framework for E-commerce Search Relevance
Authors: Pengkun Jiao, Yiming Jin, Jianhui Yang, Chenhe Dong, Zerui Huang, Shaowei Yao, Xiaojiang Zhou, Dan Ou, Haihong Tang
First: 2025-10-09T09:03:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T05:15:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Query-product relevance prediction is a foundational technology in e-commerce search engines and has become increasingly important in AI-driven e-commerce. The recent emergence of LLMs, particularly their CoT reasoning capabilities, offers promising opportunities for developing relevance systems that are both more interpretable and more robust. However, existing training paradigms have notable limitations: SFT and DPO suffer from poor generalization on long-tail queries and from a lack of fine-grained, stepwise supervision to enforce rule-aligned reasoning. In contrast, reinforcement learning with verification rewards (RLVR) suffers from sparse feedback, which provides insufficient signal to correct erroneous intermediate steps, thereby undermining logical consistency and limiting performance in complex inference scenarios. To address these challenges, we introduce the Stepwise Hybrid Examination Reinforcement Learning framework for search relevance (SHE). At its core is Stepwise Reward Policy Optimization (SRPO), a reinforcement learning algorithm that leverages step-level rewards generated by a hybrid of a high-quality generative stepwise reward model and a human-annotated offline verifier, prioritizing learning from critical correct and incorrect reasoning steps. To bolster robustness and generalization, SHE further integrates a dual-strategy optimization: diversified data filtering, which broadens the exploration of reasoning trajectories to preempt policy entropy collapse, and a multi-stage curriculum learning protocol that systematically orchestrates progressive capability acquisition. Extensive experiments on real-world search benchmarks show that SHE improves both reasoning quality and relevance-prediction accuracy in large-scale e-commerce settings, outperforming SFT, DPO, GRPO, and other baselines, while also enhancing interpretability and robustness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SHE：面向电商搜索相关性的逐步混合检验强化学习框架
查询-商品相关性预测是电商搜索引擎的基础技术，在AI驱动的电商领域日益重要。近期大语言模型（LLM）的出现，特别是其思维链推理能力，为开发更具可解释性和鲁棒性的相关性系统提供了新机遇。然而，现有训练范式存在明显局限：监督微调（SFT）和直接偏好优化（DPO）对长尾查询泛化能力不足，且缺乏细粒度、逐步的监督来确保规则对齐的推理；而基于验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）则受限于稀疏反馈，难以纠正错误的中间步骤，损害逻辑一致性并限制复杂推理场景的性能。为应对这些挑战，我们提出面向搜索相关性的逐步混合检验强化学习框架（SHE）。其核心是逐步奖励策略优化（SRPO）算法，该强化学习算法通过融合高质量生成式逐步奖励模型与人工标注离线验证器产生的步骤级奖励，优先从关键正误推理步骤中学习。为增强鲁棒性与泛化能力，SHE进一步集成双策略优化：多样化数据过滤通过扩展推理轨迹探索防止策略熵崩溃，多阶段课程学习协议系统化协调渐进能力习得。在真实搜索基准上的大量实验表明，SHE在大规模电商环境中同时提升推理质量与相关性预测准确率，优于SFT、DPO、GRPO等基线方法，并增强可解释性与鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing training paradigms like SFT, DPO, and RLVR for query-product relevance prediction—which suffer from poor generalization, lack of stepwise supervision, and sparse feedback—this paper introduces the Stepwise Hybrid Examination Reinforcement Learning framework (SHE). The method centers on Stepwise Reward Policy Optimization (SRPO), which uses step-level rewards from a hybrid generative model and human-annotated verifier to prioritize critical reasoning steps, combined with diversified data filtering and multi-stage curriculum learning for robustness. Experimental results on real-world e-commerce benchmarks demonstrate that SHE outperforms SFT, DPO, GRPO, and other baselines in both reasoning quality and relevance-prediction accuracy, while also improving interpretability and robustness.

OASI: Objective-Aware Surrogate Initialization for Multi-Objective Bayesian Optimization in TinyML Keyword Spotting
Authors: Soumen Garai, Danilo Pau, Suman Samui
First: 2025-12-17T17:32:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T04:50:18+00:00
Comments: Updated version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Voice-triggered interfaces rely on keyword spotting (KWS) models that must operate continuously under strict memory, latency, and energy constraints on microcontroller-class hardware. Designing such models therefore requires not only high recognition accuracy but also predictable deployability within limited Flash and SRAM budgets. Bayesian optimization is known to handle accuracy-efficiency trade-offs effectively in multi-objective optimization; however, it is highly sensitive to initialization, particularly in the low-budget regimes of TinyML model optimization. We propose Objective-Aware Surrogate Initialization (OASI), which seeds surrogate optimization with Pareto-biased solutions generated via multi-objective simulated annealing. Unlike space-filling or heuristic warm-start methods, OASI initializes the surrogate conditioning process with a bias toward feasible accuracy-memory trade-offs, thus avoiding SRAM-violating configurations. OASI improves hypervolume and convergence robustness over Latin hypercube, Sobol, and random initializations under the same budget constraints on a TinyML KWS problem. Hardware-in-the-loop experiments on STM32 microcontrollers verify the existence of deployable and memory-feasible models without incurring extra optimization costs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OASI：面向TinyML关键词检测中多目标贝叶斯优化的目标感知代理初始化方法
语音触发接口依赖关键词检测模型，此类模型必须在微控制器级硬件上严格的内存、延迟和能耗约束下持续运行。因此设计这类模型不仅需要高识别准确率，还需确保在有限的Flash和SRAM资源内具备可预测的部署能力。贝叶斯优化虽能有效处理多目标优化中的精度-效率权衡，但其对初始化极为敏感，在TinyML模型优化的低预算场景中尤为突出。本文提出目标感知代理初始化方法，通过多目标模拟退火生成的帕累托偏置解来初始化代理优化。与空间填充或启发式热启动方法不同，OASI在初始化代理条件化过程时偏向可行的精度-内存权衡方案，从而避免违反SRAM约束的配置。在相同预算约束下，OASI在TinyML关键词检测问题上相较于拉丁超立方、Sobol序列及随机初始化方法，显著提升了超体积指标与收敛鲁棒性。基于STM32微控制器的硬件在环实验验证了该方法可在不增加额外优化成本的前提下，获得可部署且内存可行的模型。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of designing keyword spotting models for microcontroller hardware, which must balance high accuracy with strict memory and latency constraints. The authors propose Objective-Aware Surrogate Initialization (OASI), a method that seeds Bayesian optimization with Pareto-optimal solutions generated via multi-objective simulated annealing to bias the search toward feasible accuracy-memory trade-offs. Experimental results show that OASI improves hypervolume and convergence robustness over standard initialization methods under limited budgets, and hardware-in-the-loop tests on STM32 microcontrollers confirm it identifies deployable models without extra optimization cost.
本文针对微控制器硬件上关键词识别模型的设计挑战，需在保证高精度的同时满足严格的内存和延迟限制。作者提出了目标感知代理初始化方法，通过多目标模拟退火生成帕累托最优解来初始化贝叶斯优化，从而偏向于可行的精度-内存权衡。实验结果表明，在有限预算下，该方法相比拉丁超立方、Sobol和随机初始化，提高了超体积和收敛鲁棒性；在STM32微控制器上的硬件在环测试验证了其能识别出可部署且内存可行的模型，且无需额外优化成本。
Subsampling Factorization Machine Annealing
Authors: Yusuke Hama, Tadashi Kadowaki
Venue: Phys. Rev. Research 8, 013187 (2026)
First: 2025-08-12T09:25:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T04:09:43+00:00
Comments: 29 pages and 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantum computing and machine learning are state-of-the-art technologies that have been investigated intensively in both academia and industry. The hybrid technology of these two ingredients is expected to be a powerful tool to solve complex problems in many branches of science and engineering such as combinatorial optimization problems and accelerate the creation of next-generation technologies. In this work, we develop an algorithm to solve a black-box optimization problem by improving Factorization Machine Annealing (FMA) such that the training of a machine learning model called Factorization Machine is performed not by a full dataset but by a subdataset that is sampled from a full dataset: Subsampling Factorization Machine Annealing (SFMA). According to such a probabilistic training process, the performance of FMA on exploring a solution space gets enhanced. As a result, SFMA exhibits balanced performance of exploration and exploitation, which we call exploitation-exploration functionality. We conduct numerical benchmarking tests to compare the performance of SFMA with that of FMA. Consequently, SFMA certainly exhibits the exploration-exploitation functionality and outperforms FMA in speed and accuracy. In addition, the performance of SFMA can be further improved by sequentially using two subsampling datasets with different sizes such that the size of the latter dataset is substantially smaller than the former. Such a substantial reduction not only enhances the exploration performance of SFMA but also enables us to run it with correspondingly low computational cost even for a large-scale problem. These results indicate the effectiveness of SFMA in a certain class of black-box optimization problems of significant size: the potential scalability of SFMA in solving large-scale problems with correspondingly low computational cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：子采样因子分解机退火算法
量子计算与机器学习是学术界和工业界广泛研究的前沿技术。两者的融合技术有望成为解决组合优化等科学与工程领域复杂问题的强大工具，并加速下一代技术的创新。本研究通过改进因子分解机退火算法，提出一种解决黑盒优化问题的新算法：子采样因子分解机退火算法。该算法采用概率性训练策略，仅从全数据集中采样子数据集训练因子分解机模型，而非使用完整数据集。这种机制增强了算法在解空间的探索能力，实现了探索与利用的平衡功能。通过数值基准测试对比发现，SFMA在探索-利用功能、求解速度与精度上均优于原始FMA。此外，通过先后使用两个规模递减的子采样数据集（后者规模显著小于前者），不仅能进一步提升SFMA的探索性能，还能大幅降低大规模问题的计算成本。这些结果表明SFMA在特定类型的大规模黑盒优化问题中具有显著有效性，展现出以较低计算成本解决大规模问题的潜在可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance the performance of quantum-inspired optimization algorithms for large-scale black-box problems, this work introduces Subsampling Factorization Machine Annealing (SFMA), an improved variant of Factorization Machine Annealing (FMA). The method trains a Factorization Machine model using probabilistically sampled subsets of the full dataset rather than the entire dataset, which enhances exploration of the solution space and achieves a balanced exploitation-exploration functionality. Experimental benchmarking shows that SFMA outperforms FMA in both speed and accuracy, and further performance gains are achieved by sequentially using two subsampling datasets of different sizes, with the latter substantially smaller, enabling effective scaling to large problems with reduced computational cost.
本研究旨在提升量子启发优化算法处理大规模黑盒问题的性能，提出了子采样因子机退火（SFMA），这是对因子机退火（FMA）的改进。该方法通过概率性地从全数据集中采样子数据集来训练因子机模型，而非使用完整数据集，从而增强了对解空间的探索能力，实现了利用与探索的平衡功能。数值基准测试表明，SFMA在速度和精度上均优于FMA，且通过顺序使用两个不同大小的子采样数据集（后者规模显著更小）可进一步提升性能，这不仅增强了探索效果，还降低了计算成本，使SFMA能够有效扩展到大规模问题中。
UrbanHuRo: A Two-Layer Human-Robot Collaboration Framework for the Joint Optimization of Heterogeneous Urban Services
Authors: Tonmoy Dey, Lin Jiang, Zheng Dong, Guang Wang
Venue: ICRA
First: 2026-03-04T04:02:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T04:02:28+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 15 figures. This paper has been accepted by ICRA'26 as a regular paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In the vision of smart cities, technologies are being developed to enhance the efficiency of urban services and improve residents' quality of life. However, most existing research focuses on optimizing individual services in isolation, without adequately considering reciprocal interactions among heterogeneous urban services that could yield higher efficiency and improved resource utilization. For example, human couriers could collect traffic and air quality data along their delivery routes, while sensing robots could assist with on-demand delivery during peak hours, enhancing both sensing coverage and delivery efficiency. However, the joint optimization of different urban services is challenging due to potentially conflicting objectives and the need for real-time coordination in dynamic environments. In this paper, we propose UrbanHuRo, a two-layer human-robot collaboration framework for joint optimization of heterogeneous urban services, demonstrated through crowdsourced delivery and urban sensing. UrbanHuRo includes two key designs: (i) a scalable distributed MapReduce-based K-submodular maximization module for efficient order dispatch, and (ii) a deep submodular reward reinforcement learning algorithm for sensing route planning. Experimental evaluations on real-world datasets from a food delivery platform demonstrate that UrbanHuRo improves sensing coverage by 29.7% and courier income by 39.2% on average in most settings, while also significantly reducing the number of overdue orders.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UrbanHuRo：面向异构城市服务联合优化的双层人机协作框架
在智慧城市的愿景中，技术发展旨在提升城市服务效率并改善居民生活质量。然而，现有研究多集中于孤立优化单一服务，未能充分考虑异构城市服务间的相互协同作用——这种协同可带来更高效率与更优资源利用。例如，人类配送员可在配送途中收集交通与空气质量数据，而传感机器人可在高峰时段协助按需配送，从而同时提升传感覆盖与配送效率。但不同城市服务的联合优化面临挑战，因其目标可能存在冲突，且需在动态环境中实现实时协调。本文提出UrbanHuRo，一个用于异构城市服务联合优化的双层人机协作框架，并以众包配送与城市感知为例进行验证。UrbanHuRo包含两项核心设计：（一）基于可扩展分布式MapReduce的K-子模最大化模块，用于高效订单调度；（二）基于深度子模奖励的强化学习算法，用于传感路径规划。基于真实外卖平台数据集的实验表明，在多数场景下UrbanHuRo平均提升29.7%的传感覆盖率与39.2%的配送员收入，同时显著减少超时订单数量。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to move beyond isolated optimization of individual urban services in smart cities, recognizing that synergistic human-robot collaboration across heterogeneous services like delivery and sensing can yield greater overall efficiency and resource utilization. The proposed method, UrbanHuRo, is a two-layer framework featuring a scalable distributed module for order dispatch based on K-submodular maximization and a deep submodular reward reinforcement learning algorithm for sensing route planning. Experimental results on real-world food delivery data show that the framework improves urban sensing coverage by 29.7% and courier income by 39.2% on average, while also significantly reducing overdue orders.
本文的动机是认识到在智慧城市中，需要超越对单个城市服务的孤立优化，通过跨异构服务（如配送与感知）的协同人机协作可以实现更高的整体效率和资源利用率。所提出的方法UrbanHuRo是一个双层框架，包含一个基于K-子模最大化的可扩展分布式订单调度模块，以及一个用于感知路线规划的深度子模奖励强化学习算法。在真实世界外卖平台数据上的实验结果表明，该框架平均将城市感知覆盖率提高了29.7%，将配送员收入提高了39.2%，同时显著减少了超时订单数量。
Vision-Zero: Scalable VLM Self-Improvement via Strategic Gamified Self-Play
Authors: Qinsi Wang, Bo Liu, Tianyi Zhou, Jing Shi, Yueqian Lin, Yiran Chen, Hai Helen Li, Kun Wan, Wentian Zhao
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-29T21:55:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T03:35:17+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Although reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a promising approach for improving vision-language models (VLMs) and multimodal large language models (MLLMs), current methods rely heavily on manually curated datasets and costly human verification, which limits scalable self-improvement in multimodal systems. To address this challenge, we propose Vision-Zero, a label-free, domain-agnostic multi-agent self-play framework for self-evolving VLMs through competitive visual games generated from arbitrary image inputs. Specifically, Vision-Zero encompasses three main attributes: (1) Strategic Self-Play Framework: Vision-Zero trains VLMs in "Who Is the Spy"-style games, where the models engage in strategic reasoning and actions across multiple roles. Through interactive gameplay, models autonomously generate their training data without human annotation. (2) Gameplay from Arbitrary Images: Unlike existing gamified frameworks, Vision-Zero can generate games from arbitrary images, thereby enhancing the model's reasoning ability across diverse domains and showing strong generalization to different tasks. We demonstrate this versatility using three distinct types of image datasets: CLEVR-based synthetic scenes, charts, and real-world images. (3) Sustainable Performance Gain: We introduce Iterative Self-Play Policy Optimization (Iterative-SPO), a novel training algorithm that alternates between Self-Play and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), mitigating the performance plateau often seen in self-play-only training and achieving sustained long-term improvements. Despite using label-free data, Vision-Zero achieves state-of-the-art performance on reasoning, chart question answering, and vision-centric understanding tasks, surpassing other annotation-based methods. Models and code have been released at https://github.com/wangqinsi1/Vision-Zero.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Vision-Zero：通过策略性游戏化自我对弈实现可扩展的视觉语言模型自我改进
尽管强化学习已成为改进视觉语言模型和多模态大语言模型的有前景方法，但现有方法严重依赖人工标注数据集和昂贵的人工验证，限制了多模态系统的可扩展自我改进。为应对这一挑战，我们提出Vision-Zero——一种无需标注、领域无关的多智能体自我对弈框架，通过任意图像输入生成的竞争性视觉游戏实现视觉语言模型的自主进化。该框架具备三大特性：（1）策略性自我对弈框架：通过“谁是卧底”式游戏训练模型进行跨角色策略推理与行动，在交互式游戏中自主生成训练数据；（2）任意图像生成游戏：突破现有游戏化框架限制，可从任意图像生成游戏，增强模型跨领域推理能力，在合成场景、图表和真实图像三类数据集上均展现卓越泛化性；（3）可持续性能增益：提出迭代式自我对弈策略优化算法，交替进行自我对弈与可验证奖励的强化学习，突破纯自我对弈的性能瓶颈，实现长期持续改进。在无需标注数据的情况下，Vision-Zero在推理、图表问答和视觉中心理解任务上达到最先进性能，超越基于标注的方法。模型与代码已开源。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the scalability limitations of current reinforcement learning methods for vision-language models, which depend on costly human-curated data, by introducing Vision-Zero, a label-free, domain-agnostic framework that enables self-improvement through strategic multi-agent self-play. The method involves training models in competitive visual games, such as a "Who Is the Spy"-style setup, where models generate their own training data from arbitrary images without human annotation, and employs Iterative Self-Play Policy Optimization to combine self-play with reinforcement learning for sustained performance gains. Experimental results on synthetic scenes, charts, and real-world images demonstrate state-of-the-art performance in reasoning, chart question answering, and vision-centric understanding tasks, outperforming annotation-based approaches.
本文针对当前基于强化学习的视觉语言模型改进方法依赖人工标注数据且可扩展性有限的问题，提出了Vision-Zero框架，这是一种无需标注、领域无关的多智能体自博弈方法，通过从任意图像生成竞争性视觉游戏来实现模型自我进化。该方法的核心包括：设计战略自博弈框架，让模型在类似“谁是卧底”的游戏中自主生成训练数据；支持从任意图像生成游戏，提升跨领域推理能力；并采用迭代自博弈策略优化算法，结合自博弈和强化学习以避免性能瓶颈。实验在合成场景、图表和真实世界图像上验证了该框架的有效性，在推理、图表问答和视觉理解任务中取得了领先性能，超越了基于标注的方法。
MAGE: Meta-Reinforcement Learning for Language Agents toward Strategic Exploration and Exploitation
Authors: Lu Yang, Zelai Xu, Minyang Xie, Jiaxuan Gao, Zhao Shok, Yu Wang, Yi Wu
First: 2026-03-04T03:14:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T03:14:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM) agents have demonstrated remarkable proficiency in learned tasks, yet they often struggle to adapt to non-stationary environments with feedback. While In-Context Learning and external memory offer some flexibility, they fail to internalize the adaptive ability required for long-term improvement. Meta-Reinforcement Learning (meta-RL) provides an alternative by embedding the learning process directly within the model. However, existing meta-RL approaches for LLMs focus primarily on exploration in single-agent settings, neglecting the strategic exploitation necessary for multi-agent environments. We propose MAGE, a meta-RL framework that empowers LLM agents for strategic exploration and exploitation. MAGE utilizes a multi-episode training regime where interaction histories and reflections are integrated into the context window. By using the final episode reward as the objective, MAGE incentivizes the agent to refine its strategy based on past experiences. We further combine population-based training with an agent-specific advantage normalization technique to enrich agent diversity and ensure stable learning. Experiment results show that MAGE outperforms existing baselines in both exploration and exploitation tasks. Furthermore, MAGE exhibits strong generalization to unseen opponents, suggesting it has internalized the ability for strategic exploration and exploitation. Code is available at https://github.com/Lu-Yang666/MAGE.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MAGE：面向语言智能体的元强化学习框架，实现策略性探索与利用
大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在已学习任务中展现出卓越能力，但在适应具有反馈的非稳态环境时仍面临挑战。尽管上下文学习和外部记忆提供了一定灵活性，它们未能内化长期改进所需的适应能力。元强化学习（meta-RL）通过将学习过程直接嵌入模型提供了替代方案，但现有面向LLM的元强化学习方法主要关注单智能体环境中的探索，忽视了多智能体环境所需的策略性利用。本文提出MAGE框架，通过元强化学习赋能LLM智能体实现策略性探索与利用。该框架采用多轮次训练机制，将交互历史与反思整合至上下文窗口，并以最终轮次奖励为目标激励智能体基于历史经验优化策略。通过结合群体训练与智能体特定优势归一化技术，MAGE增强了智能体多样性并确保稳定学习。实验表明，MAGE在探索与利用任务中均优于现有基线方法，且对未见过的对手表现出强泛化能力，表明其已内化策略性探索与利用的能力。代码发布于https://github.com/Lu-Yang666/MAGE。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of Large Language Model (LLM) agents in adapting to non-stationary environments, as existing methods like In-Context Learning lack internalized adaptive capabilities for long-term improvement. To overcome this, the authors propose MAGE, a meta-reinforcement learning framework that trains LLM agents through a multi-episode regime, integrating interaction histories and reflections into the context window and using final episode rewards to refine strategies, while employing population-based training and advantage normalization for diversity and stability. Experimental results demonstrate that MAGE outperforms baselines in both exploration and exploitation tasks and shows strong generalization to unseen opponents, indicating successful internalization of strategic adaptation.
本文针对大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在非平稳环境中适应能力不足的问题，指出现有方法如上下文学习缺乏长期改进所需的内化适应能力。为此，作者提出了MAGE，一个元强化学习框架，通过多轮次训练机制，将交互历史和反思整合到上下文窗口中，并利用最终轮次奖励优化策略，同时结合基于种群的训练和智能体特定的优势归一化技术以增强多样性和稳定性。实验结果表明，MAGE在探索和利用任务上均优于现有基线，并对未见过的对手表现出强大的泛化能力，表明其成功内化了战略探索与利用的能力。
MIND: Unified Inquiry and Diagnosis RL with Criteria Grounded Clinical Supports for Psychiatric Consultation
Authors: Guoyi Li, Shihao Xu, Jiatong Ma, Yunyun Han, Jianhua Chen, Yafeng Deng
First: 2026-03-04T03:05:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T03:05:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have advanced medical dialogue systems, yet psychiatric consultation poses substantially higher demands due to subjective ambiguity and comorbidity complexity: an agent must continuously extract psychopathological cues from incomplete and inconsistent patient reports in multi-turn interactions and perform rigorous differential diagnostic reasoning. However, existing methods face two fundamental challenges. First, without criteria-grounded clinical supports, they are prone to unsupported clinical assertions when symptoms are atypical or underspecified. Second, in multi-turn interactions, they struggle to mitigate inquiry drift (off-topic or low-yield questioning) and optimize questioning strategies. To address these challenges, we propose MIND, a unified inquiry--diagnosis reinforcement learning framework for psychiatric consultation. Specifically, we build a Criteria-Grounded Psychiatric Reasoning Bank (PRB) that summarizes dialogue context into clinical retrieval states, retrieves semantically similar reference consultations, and distills reusable criteria-grounded clinical supports to guide criteria-aligned inquiry and reasoning. Building on this foundation, MIND enforces explicit clinical reasoning with rubric-based process rewards to provide fine-grained supervision over intermediate decision steps, and incorporates a value-aware trajectory rectification mechanism to jointly improve information acquisition and diagnostic decision-making across turns. Extensive experiments demonstrate that MIND consistently outperforms strong baselines in diagnostic accuracy, empathetic interaction quality, interpretability, and generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MIND：基于标准锚定临床支持的精神科会诊统一问诊与诊断强化学习框架
大语言模型虽推动了医疗对话系统发展，但精神科会诊因主观模糊性与共病复杂性面临更高要求：智能体需在多轮交互中持续从不完整、不一致的患者陈述中提取精神病理线索，并进行严谨的鉴别诊断推理。现有方法存在两大根本挑战：其一，缺乏标准锚定的临床支持，易在症状非典型或描述不明确时做出无依据的临床断言；其二，在多轮交互中难以抑制问诊偏移（偏离主题或低效提问）并优化提问策略。为此，我们提出MIND——面向精神科会诊的统一问诊-诊断强化学习框架。具体而言，我们构建了标准锚定精神科推理库，将对话语境归纳为临床检索状态，检索语义相似的参考会诊记录，并提炼可复用的标准锚定临床支持，以指导符合诊断标准的问诊推理。在此基础上，MIND通过基于量规的过程奖励机制强化显式临床推理，对中间决策步骤实施细粒度监督，并引入价值感知轨迹校正机制，协同优化多轮交互中的信息获取与诊断决策。大量实验表明，MIND在诊断准确性、共情交互质量、可解释性及泛化能力上均持续优于现有基线模型。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the heightened challenges in psychiatric consultation, where large language models must navigate subjective ambiguity and complex comorbidities by extracting psychopathological cues from inconsistent patient reports and performing differential diagnosis. To overcome issues of unsupported clinical assertions and inquiry drift in multi-turn interactions, the authors propose MIND, a unified inquiry-diagnosis reinforcement learning framework that incorporates a Criteria-Grounded Psychiatric Reasoning Bank to distill clinical supports from reference consultations, guiding criteria-aligned inquiry. The method enforces explicit clinical reasoning with rubric-based process rewards and uses value-aware trajectory rectification to jointly optimize questioning and diagnosis. Experimental results show that MIND outperforms baselines in diagnostic accuracy, empathetic interaction quality, interpretability, and generalization.
本文针对精神科会诊中主观模糊性和共病复杂性带来的挑战，旨在解决现有方法因缺乏标准依据的临床支持而产生无根据断言，以及在多轮交互中难以避免询问偏离和优化策略的问题。作者提出了MIND，一个统一的询问-诊断强化学习框架，通过构建标准依据的精神科推理库，从参考会诊中提炼可重用的临床支持，以指导符合标准的询问和推理。该方法采用基于量规的过程奖励来强化显式临床推理，并结合价值感知的轨迹校正机制，共同优化信息获取和诊断决策。大量实验表明，MIND在诊断准确性、共情交互质量、可解释性和泛化能力上均优于现有基线方法。
Rewards as Labels: Revisiting RLVR from a Classification Perspective
Authors: Zepeng Zhai, Meilin Chen, Jiaxuan Zhao, Junlang Qian, Lei Shen, Yuan Lu
First: 2026-02-05T13:11:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T03:01:17+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 5 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards has recently advanced the capabilities of Large Language Models in complex reasoning tasks by providing explicit rule-based supervision. Among RLVR methods, GRPO and its variants have achieved strong empirical performance. Despite their success, we identify that they suffer from Gradient Misassignment in Positives and Gradient Domination in Negatives, which lead to inefficient and suboptimal policy updates. To address these issues, we propose Rewards as Labels (REAL), a novel framework that revisits verifiable rewards as categorical labels rather than scalar weights, thereby reformulating policy optimization as a classification problem. Building on this, we further introduce anchor logits to enhance policy learning. Our analysis reveals that REAL induces a monotonic and bounded gradient weighting, enabling balanced gradient allocation across rollouts and effectively mitigating the identified mismatches. Extensive experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that REAL improves training stability and consistently outperforms GRPO and strong variants such as DAPO. On the 1.5B model, REAL improves average Pass@1 over DAPO by 6.7%. These gains further scale to 7B model, REAL continues to outperform DAPO and GSPO by 6.2% and 1.7%, respectively. Notably, even with a vanilla binary cross-entropy, REAL remains stable and exceeds DAPO by 4.5% on average.
中文标题/摘要
标题：奖励作为标签：从分类视角重审可验证奖励强化学习
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）近期通过提供明确的规则监督，显著提升了大型语言模型在复杂推理任务中的能力。在RLVR方法中，GRPO及其变体取得了优异的实证性能。尽管成果显著，我们发现这些方法存在正样本梯度错配与负样本梯度主导问题，导致策略更新效率低下且非最优。为解决这些问题，我们提出“奖励作为标签”（REAL）框架，将可验证奖励重新定义为分类标签而非标量权重，从而将策略优化重构为分类问题。在此基础上，我们进一步引入锚定逻辑值以增强策略学习。分析表明，REAL能产生单调有界的梯度加权机制，实现回合间梯度分配的平衡，有效缓解上述错配问题。在数学推理基准上的大量实验显示，REAL提升了训练稳定性，并持续超越GRPO及DAPO等强效变体。在15亿参数模型中，REAL的Pass@1平均指标较DAPO提升6.7%。该优势在70亿参数模型中进一步扩大，REAL分别超越DAPO和GSPO达6.2%和1.7%。值得注意的是，即使采用基础二元交叉熵损失，REAL仍保持稳定，平均性能超过DAPO达4.5%。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses inefficiencies in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods like GRPO, identifying issues of Gradient Misassignment in Positives and Gradient Domination in Negatives that lead to suboptimal policy updates. The authors propose Rewards as Labels (REAL), a novel framework that reinterprets verifiable rewards as categorical labels instead of scalar weights, thereby reformulating policy optimization as a classification problem and introducing anchor logits to enhance learning. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that REAL improves training stability and outperforms strong baselines, achieving average Pass@1 improvements of 6.7% over DAPO on a 1.5B model, with gains scaling to larger 7B models.
本文针对可验证奖励强化学习方法中的低效问题，指出GRPO等方法存在正样本梯度错配和负样本梯度主导的缺陷，导致策略更新次优。作者提出了Rewards as Labels（REAL）框架，将可验证奖励重新定义为分类标签而非标量权重，从而将策略优化重构为分类问题，并引入锚定逻辑值以增强学习。在数学推理基准上的实验结果表明，REAL提高了训练稳定性并超越了现有基线，在1.5B模型上平均Pass@1比DAPO提升6.7%，且在7B模型上仍保持显著优势。
CaRe-BN: Precise Moving Statistics for Stabilizing Spiking Neural Networks in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zijie Xu, Xinyu Shi, Yiting Dong, Zihan Huang, Zhaofei Yu
First: 2025-09-28T10:21:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T02:40:03+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) offer low-latency and energy-efficient decision-making on neuromorphic hardware by mimicking the event-driven dynamics of biological neurons. However, the discrete and non-differentiable nature of spikes leads to unstable gradient propagation in directly trained SNNs, making Batch Normalization (BN) an important component for stabilizing training. In online Reinforcement Learning (RL), imprecise BN statistics hinder exploitation, resulting in slower convergence and suboptimal policies. While Artificial Neural Networks (ANNs) can often omit BN, SNNs critically depend on it, limiting the adoption of SNNs for energy-efficient control on resource-constrained devices. To overcome this, we propose Confidence-adaptive and Re-calibration Batch Normalization (CaRe-BN), which introduces (i) a confidence-guided adaptive update strategy for BN statistics and (ii) a re-calibration mechanism to align distributions. By providing more accurate normalization, CaRe-BN stabilizes SNN optimization without disrupting the RL training process. Importantly, CaRe-BN does not alter inference, thus preserving the energy efficiency of SNNs in deployment. Extensive experiments on both discrete and continuous control benchmarks demonstrate that CaRe-BN improves SNN performance by up to $22.6\%$ across different spiking neuron models and RL algorithms. Remarkably, SNNs equipped with CaRe-BN even surpass their ANN counterparts by $5.9\%$. These results highlight a new direction for BN techniques tailored to RL, paving the way for neuromorphic agents that are both efficient and high-performing. Code is available at https://github.com/xuzijie32/CaRe-BN.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CaRe-BN：通过精确移动统计稳定强化学习中脉冲神经网络的训练
脉冲神经网络（SNN）通过模拟生物神经元的事件驱动特性，在神经形态硬件上实现了低延迟、高能效的决策。然而，脉冲的离散性和不可微性导致直接训练的SNN梯度传播不稳定，使得批归一化（BN）成为稳定训练的关键组件。在在线强化学习（RL）中，不精确的BN统计会阻碍策略利用，导致收敛速度慢和策略性能下降。虽然人工神经网络（ANN）常可省略BN，但SNN对其依赖性强，这限制了SNN在资源受限设备上实现高能效控制的应用。为此，我们提出置信度自适应与重校准批归一化（CaRe-BN），其引入（i）基于置信度的BN统计自适应更新策略，以及（ii）分布对齐的重校准机制。通过提供更精确的归一化，CaRe-BN在不干扰RL训练过程的前提下稳定了SNN优化。重要的是，CaRe-BN不改变推理过程，从而保持了SNN在部署时的能效优势。在离散和连续控制基准上的大量实验表明，CaRe-BN在不同脉冲神经元模型和RL算法中将SNN性能提升最高达22.6%。值得注意的是，配备CaRe-BN的SNN甚至比对应ANN性能高出5.9%。这些结果为面向RL的BN技术指明了新方向，为构建高效且高性能的神经形态智能体铺平了道路。代码发布于：https://github.com/xuzijie32/CaRe-BN。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of unstable gradient propagation in directly trained Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) for online Reinforcement Learning (RL), where imprecise Batch Normalization (BN) statistics hinder exploitation and slow convergence. To overcome this, the authors propose CaRe-BN, a method featuring a confidence-guided adaptive update strategy for BN statistics and a re-calibration mechanism to align distributions, which stabilizes SNN optimization without altering inference. Experimental results on discrete and continuous control benchmarks show that CaRe-BN improves SNN performance by up to 22.6% across various spiking neuron models and RL algorithms, even surpassing Artificial Neural Network counterparts by 5.9%, highlighting its potential for efficient neuromorphic agents.
本文针对脉冲神经网络在在线强化学习中直接训练时梯度传播不稳定的问题，其中不精确的批归一化统计会阻碍利用并减缓收敛。为解决此问题，作者提出了CaRe-BN方法，该方法引入了置信度引导的自适应更新策略和分布对齐的重新校准机制，以稳定SNN优化而不改变推理过程。在离散和连续控制基准上的实验结果表明，CaRe-BN在不同脉冲神经元模型和强化学习算法中将SNN性能提升高达22.6%，甚至超过人工神经网络5.9%，为高效高性能的神经形态智能体指明了新方向。
Principled Learning-to-Communicate with Quasi-Classical Information Structures
Authors: Xiangyu Liu, Haoyi You, Kaiqing Zhang
First: 2026-03-04T02:36:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T02:36:18+00:00
Comments: Preliminary version appeared at IEEE CDC 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning-to-communicate (LTC) in partially observable environments has received increasing attention in deep multi-agent reinforcement learning, where the control and communication strategies are jointly learned. Meanwhile, the impact of communication on decision-making has been extensively studied in control theory. In this paper, we seek to formalize and better understand LTC by bridging these two lines of work, through the lens of information structures (ISs). To this end, we formalize LTC in decentralized partially observable Markov decision processes (Dec-POMDPs) under the common-information-based framework from decentralized stochastic control, and classify LTC problems based on the ISs before (additional) information sharing. We first show that non-classical LTCs are computationally intractable in general, and thus focus on quasi-classical (QC) LTCs. We then propose a series of conditions for QC LTCs, under which LTCs preserve the QC IS after information sharing, whereas violating which can cause computational hardness in general. Further, we develop provable planning and learning algorithms for QC LTCs, and establish quasi-polynomial time and sample complexities for several QC LTC examples that satisfy the above conditions. Along the way, we also establish results on the relationship between (strictly) QC IS and the condition of having strategy-independent common-information-based beliefs (SI-CIBs), as well as on solving Dec-POMDPs without computationally intractable oracles but beyond those with SI-CIBs, which may be of independent interest.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于准经典信息结构的原理性通信学习
在部分可观测环境中的通信学习（LTC）在深度多智能体强化学习中日益受到关注，其控制与通信策略被联合学习。与此同时，通信对决策的影响在控制理论中已得到广泛研究。本文通过信息结构（IS）的视角，试图通过连接这两条研究路径来形式化并更好地理解LTC。为此，我们在基于公共信息的分散随机控制框架下，将LTC形式化为分散部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（Dec-POMDP），并根据（额外）信息共享前的信息结构对LTC问题进行分类。我们首先证明非经典LTC在计算上通常是难解的，因此聚焦于准经典（QC）LTC。随后提出一系列QC LTC的充分条件，在这些条件下信息共享后LTC能保持QC信息结构，而违反这些条件通常会导致计算困难。进一步，我们为QC LTC开发了可证明的规划与学习算法，并对满足上述条件的若干QC LTC实例建立了拟多项式时间与样本复杂度。在此过程中，我们还建立了（严格）QC信息结构与具有策略无关的公共信息信念（SI-CIB）条件之间的关系，并提出了在无需计算难解预言机的情况下求解超出SI-CIB范围的Dec-POMDP的方法，这些成果可能具有独立的研究价值。
Summary / 总结
This paper aims to formalize learning-to-communicate (LTC) in multi-agent systems by bridging deep reinforcement learning and control theory through the lens of information structures. The motivation is to understand when and how communication can be learned effectively in decentralized partially observable Markov decision processes (Dec-POMDPs). The method involves classifying LTC problems based on their information structures, focusing on quasi-classical (QC) cases, and establishing conditions under which LTC remains tractable. The main experimental results show that the proposed provable planning and learning algorithms achieve quasi-polynomial time and sample complexities for several QC LTC examples that satisfy the identified conditions, while also demonstrating the general computational intractability of non-classical LTC problems.
本文旨在通过信息结构的视角，连接深度强化学习与控制理论，以形式化多智能体系统中的学习通信问题。其动机是为了理解在去中心化部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程中，何时以及如何能有效学习通信。方法包括基于信息结构对学习通信问题进行分类，聚焦于准经典情况，并建立确保学习通信问题可高效求解的条件。主要实验结果表明，所提出的可证明规划与学习算法在多个满足条件的准经典学习通信示例上实现了准多项式时间和样本复杂度，同时证明了非经典学习通信问题通常具有计算上的难解性。
Freezing of Gait Prediction using Proactive Agent that Learns from Selected Experience and DDQN Algorithm
Authors: Septian Enggar Sukmana, Sang Won Bae, Tomohiro Shibata
First: 2026-03-04T02:16:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T02:16:46+00:00
Comments: Accepted on Activity and Behavior Computing (ABC) 2026 Conference (https://autocare.ai/abc2026) and will be published on International Journal of Activity and Behavior Computing (IJABC) (International Journal of Activity and Behavior Computing)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Freezing of Gait (FOG) is a debilitating motor symptom commonly experienced by individuals with Parkinson's Disease (PD) which often leads to falls and reduced mobility. Timely and accurate prediction of FOG episodes is essential for enabling proactive interventions through assistive technologies. This study presents a reinforcement learning-based framework designed to identify optimal pre-FOG onset points, thereby extending the prediction horizon for anticipatory cueing systems. The model implements a Double Deep Q-Network (DDQN) architecture enhanced with Prioritized Experience Replay (PER) allowing the agent to focus learning on high-impact experiences and refine its policy. Trained over 9000 episodes with a reward shaping strategy that promotes cautious decision-making, the agent demonstrated robust performance in both subject-dependent and subject-independent evaluations. The model achieved a prediction horizon of up to 8.72 seconds prior to FOG onset in subject-independent scenarios and 7.89 seconds in subject-dependent settings. These results highlight the model's potential for integration into wearable assistive devices, offering timely and personalized interventions to mitigate FOG in PD patients.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于选择性经验学习与DDQN算法的步态冻结预测主动智能体
步态冻结（FOG）是帕金森病患者常见的致残性运动症状，常导致跌倒和行动能力下降。及时准确预测FOG发作对于通过辅助技术实施主动干预至关重要。本研究提出一种基于强化学习的框架，旨在识别最优的FOG发作前起始点，从而扩展预警提示系统的预测时间窗。该模型采用双深度Q网络（DDQN）架构，并结合优先经验回放（PER）机制，使智能体能聚焦于高价值经验以优化决策策略。通过9000轮训练及鼓励谨慎决策的奖励塑形策略，该智能体在受试者依赖与独立评估中均表现出稳健性能。在受试者独立场景下，模型实现了FOG发作前8.72秒的预测时间窗；在受试者依赖场景下为7.89秒。这些结果表明该模型具备集成至可穿戴辅助设备的潜力，能为帕金森病患者提供及时个性化的FOG干预方案。

SafeDPO: A Simple Approach to Direct Preference Optimization with Enhanced Safety
Authors: Geon-Hyeong Kim, Yu Jin Kim, Byoungjip Kim, Honglak Lee, Kyunghoon Bae, Youngsoo Jang, Moontae Lee
Venue: ICLR
First: 2025-05-26T14:50:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T02:11:26+00:00
Comments: 40 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in real-world applications, balancing helpfulness and safety has become a central challenge. A natural approach is to incorporate safety constraints into Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF), where recent studies have shown promising progress. However, these methods often rely on auxiliary networks or multi-stage pipelines, thereby increasing complexity. In this work, we revisit the original safety alignment objective and show that, under mild assumptions, it admits a closed-form optimal policy. We further derive a provably equivalent and tractable objective, enabling direct optimization. Building on this insight, we propose SafeDPO, a lightweight method that preserves the optimal solution of the underlying safety-constrained objective while requiring only one additional hyperparameter and minimal modifications to existing preference-based training methods. SafeDPO eliminates the need for reward models, cost models, and online sampling, relying only on preference data and safety indicators. Despite its simplicity, SafeDPO achieves competitive safety-helpfulness trade-offs compared to existing safety alignment methods. Experiments on the PKU-SafeRLHF-30K benchmark demonstrate that SafeDPO substantially improves safety while maintaining competitive helpfulness. Ablation studies further show that the additional hyperparameter provides a flexible mechanism to enhance safety while preserving the theoretical optimum, and confirm that SafeDPO scales reliably to LLMs with up to 13B parameters. Overall, our results highlight that a simple, theory-driven objective can provide a lightweight yet effective solution for safety alignment in practice.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SafeDPO：一种增强安全性的直接偏好优化简易方法
随着大语言模型（LLM）在现实应用中的日益普及，平衡有用性与安全性已成为核心挑战。一种自然的方法是将安全约束纳入基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）中，近期研究已展现出良好进展。然而，这些方法通常依赖辅助网络或多阶段流程，从而增加了复杂性。本研究重新审视了原始的安全对齐目标，并证明在温和假设下，该目标存在闭式最优策略。我们进一步推导出一个可证明等价且易处理的目标，实现了直接优化。基于此洞见，我们提出了SafeDPO——一种轻量级方法，在仅需一个额外超参数、对现有基于偏好的训练方法改动极小的前提下，保留了底层安全约束目标的最优解。SafeDPO无需奖励模型、成本模型或在线采样，仅依赖偏好数据与安全指示器。尽管设计简洁，SafeDPO在安全性与有用性的权衡方面与现有安全对齐方法相比具有竞争力。在PKU-SafeRLHF-30K基准测试上的实验表明，SafeDPO在保持竞争力有用性的同时显著提升了安全性。消融研究进一步证实，额外超参数提供了增强安全性同时保持理论最优解的灵活机制，并验证了SafeDPO可稳定扩展至130亿参数的LLM。总体而言，我们的结果表明，这种简洁的理论驱动目标能为实际安全对齐提供轻量而有效的解决方案。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the challenge of balancing helpfulness and safety in Large Language Models (LLMs) by simplifying existing safety alignment methods, which often involve complex multi-stage pipelines or auxiliary networks. The method introduces SafeDPO, a lightweight approach derived from a closed-form optimal policy under mild assumptions, requiring only one additional hyperparameter and minimal modifications to existing preference-based training methods, eliminating the need for reward models, cost models, or online sampling. Experimental results on the PKU-SafeRLHF-30K benchmark show that SafeDPO substantially improves safety while maintaining competitive helpfulness, with ablation studies confirming its scalability to LLMs up to 13B parameters and the effectiveness of its hyperparameter in enhancing safety without compromising theoretical optimality.
本研究的动机是通过简化现有安全对齐方法来解决大型语言模型（LLM）中平衡有用性与安全性的挑战，这些方法通常涉及复杂的多阶段流程或辅助网络。方法上提出了SafeDPO，这是一种轻量级方法，基于温和假设下的闭式最优策略推导而来，仅需一个额外超参数和对现有偏好训练方法的最小修改，无需奖励模型、成本模型或在线采样。在PKU-SafeRLHF-30K基准上的实验结果表明，SafeDPO显著提升了安全性，同时保持了有竞争力的有用性，消融研究进一步证实了其可扩展至130亿参数规模的LLM，且超参数能有效增强安全性而不损害理论最优性。
Online Robust Reinforcement Learning with General Function Approximation
Authors: Debamita Ghosh, George K. Atia, Yue Wang
First: 2025-12-22T02:12:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T02:00:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In many real-world settings, reinforcement learning systems suffer performance degradation when the environment encountered at deployment differs from that observed during training. Distributionally robust reinforcement learning (DR-RL) mitigates this issue by seeking policies that maximize performance under the most adverse transition dynamics within a prescribed uncertainty set. Most existing DR-RL approaches, however, rely on strong data availability assumptions, such as access to a generative model or large offline datasets, and are largely restricted to tabular settings. In this work, we propose a fully online DR-RL algorithm with general function approximation that learns robust policies solely through interaction, without requiring prior knowledge or pre-collected data. Our approach is based on a dual-driven fitted robust Bellman procedure that simultaneously estimates the value function and the corresponding worst-case backup operator. We establish regret guarantees for online DR-RL characterized by an intrinsic complexity notion, the robust Bellman-Eluder dimension, covering a broad class of phi-divergence uncertainty sets. The resulting regret bounds are sublinear, do not scale with the size of the state or action spaces, and specialize to tight rates in structured problem classes, demonstrating the practicality and scalability of our framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于通用函数逼近的在线鲁棒强化学习
在许多实际场景中，当部署环境与训练环境存在差异时，强化学习系统的性能会下降。分布鲁棒强化学习通过寻找在预设不确定性集合内最差转移动态下仍能最大化性能的策略来缓解此问题。然而，现有方法大多依赖强数据可获性假设（如生成模型或大规模离线数据集），且主要局限于表格化设置。本研究提出一种完全在线的分布鲁棒强化学习算法，该算法通过通用函数逼近实现，仅需交互即可学习鲁棒策略，无需先验知识或预收集数据。该方法基于双驱动拟合鲁棒贝尔曼过程，同步估计值函数及对应最差情况回溯算子。我们建立了以鲁棒贝尔曼-埃尔德维度这一内在复杂性概念为特征的在线分布鲁棒强化学习遗憾保证，覆盖广泛的φ-散度不确定性集合。所得遗憾界具有次线性特性，不随状态或动作空间规模增长，在结构化问题类别中可收敛至紧致速率，证明了本框架的实用性与可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the performance degradation of reinforcement learning systems in real-world deployment due to environmental shifts by proposing an online distributionally robust reinforcement learning (DR-RL) algorithm. The motivation stems from the limitations of existing DR-RL methods, which often rely on strong data assumptions like generative models or large offline datasets and are confined to tabular settings. Hybrid Belief Reinforcement Learning for Efficient Coordinated Spatial Exploration
Authors: Danish Rizvi, David Boyle
First: 2026-03-04T00:00:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-04T00:00:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Coordinating multiple autonomous agents to explore and serve spatially heterogeneous demand requires jointly learning unknown spatial patterns and planning trajectories that maximize task performance. Pure model-based approaches provide structured uncertainty estimates but lack adaptive policy learning, while deep reinforcement learning often suffers from poor sample efficiency when spatial priors are absent. This paper presents a hybrid belief-reinforcement learning (HBRL) framework to address this gap. In the first phase, agents construct spatial beliefs using a Log-Gaussian Cox Process (LGCP) and execute information-driven trajectories guided by a Pathwise Mutual Information (PathMI) planner with multi-step lookahead. In the second phase, trajectory control is transferred to a Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) agent, warm-started through dual-channel knowledge transfer: belief state initialization supplies spatial uncertainty, and replay buffer seeding provides demonstration trajectories generated during LGCP exploration. A variance-normalized overlap penalty enables coordinated coverage through shared belief state, permitting cooperative sensing in high-uncertainty regions while discouraging redundant coverage in well-explored areas. The framework is evaluated on a multi-UAV wireless service provisioning task. Results show 10.8% higher cumulative reward and 38% faster convergence over baselines, with ablation studies confirming that dual-channel transfer outperforms either channel alone.
中文标题/摘要
标题：混合信念强化学习在高效协同空间探索中的应用
协调多个自主智能体探索并服务空间异质性需求，需联合学习未知空间模式并规划最大化任务性能的轨迹。纯模型方法提供结构化不确定性估计但缺乏自适应策略学习，而深度强化学习在缺乏空间先验时常面临样本效率低下的问题。本文提出混合信念强化学习框架以解决这一局限。第一阶段，智能体采用对数高斯考克斯过程构建空间信念，并通过具有多步前瞻的路径互信息规划器执行信息驱动的轨迹。第二阶段，轨迹控制转移至软演员-评论家智能体，通过双通道知识迁移实现热启动：信念状态初始化提供空间不确定性，回放缓冲区预置提供LGCP探索阶段生成的示范轨迹。方差归一化重叠惩罚机制通过共享信念状态实现协同覆盖，允许在高不确定性区域进行协作感知，同时避免在已充分探索区域的冗余覆盖。该框架在多无人机无线服务供给任务中验证，结果显示其累计奖励较基线提升10.8%，收敛速度加快38%，消融实验证实双通道迁移策略优于任一单通道方案。

This paper addresses the challenge of coordinating multiple autonomous agents for spatial exploration and service tasks, where purely model-based methods lack adaptive policy learning and deep reinforcement learning suffers from poor sample efficiency without spatial priors. The authors propose a hybrid belief-reinforcement learning (HBRL) framework that first uses a Log-Gaussian Cox Process (LGCP) to build spatial beliefs and guide exploration with a Pathwise Mutual Information planner, then transfers control to a Soft Actor-Critic agent warm-started via dual-channel knowledge transfer of belief states and demonstration trajectories. Experimental results on a multi-UAV wireless service task show the framework achieves 10.8% higher cumulative reward and 38% faster convergence compared to baselines, with ablation studies confirming the effectiveness of the dual-channel transfer approach.
本文针对多智能体在空间探索与服务任务中的协调问题，指出纯模型方法缺乏自适应策略学习，而深度强化学习在缺乏空间先验时样本效率低下。作者提出了一种混合信念强化学习框架，首先利用对数高斯柯克斯过程构建空间信念并通过路径互信息规划器指导探索，随后将控制权转移至通过双通道知识转移热启动的软演员-评论家智能体，转移内容包括信念状态和演示轨迹。在多无人机无线服务任务上的实验结果表明，该框架相比基线方法累计奖励提高10.8%、收敛速度加快38%，消融研究验证了双通道转移策略的有效性。
R1-Code-Interpreter: LLMs Reason with Code via Supervised and Multi-stage Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yongchao Chen, Yueying Liu, Junwei Zhou, Yilun Hao, Jingquan Wang, Yang Zhang, Na Li, Chuchu Fan
First: 2025-05-27T18:47:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T22:06:19+00:00
Comments: 29 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Practical guidance on training Large Language Models (LLMs) to leverage Code Interpreter across diverse tasks remains lacking. We present R1-Code-Interpreter, an extension of a text-only LLM trained via multi-turn supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL) to autonomously generate multiple code queries during step-by-step reasoning. Unlike prior RL + tool-use efforts focused on narrow domains such as math or retrieval, we curate 144 diverse reasoning and planning tasks and show that training a general-purpose Code Interpreter across them presents significant challenges due to task heterogeneity and scarcity of effective samples. To address this, we introduce a multi-stage curriculum learning approach that partitions training samples by measured improvement potential. The RL training prioritizes samples with higher potential and gradually shifts to lower-potential ones, increasing the average RL gains from merely +3.4% to +9.3% across Qwen-2.5 models (3/7/14B). Our final model, R1-CI-14B, improves average accuracy on the 37 test tasks from 44.1% to 72.4%, outperforming text-only GPT-4o (58.6%) and GPT-4o with Code Interpreter (70.9%). Notably, R1-CI-14B also exhibits emergent self-checking behavior through code generation. Datasets, Codes, and Models are available at https://github.com/yongchao98/R1-Code-Interpreter and https://huggingface.co/yongchao98.
