本研究的动机在于缺乏训练大语言模型（LLM）跨多样化任务有效使用代码解释器的实用指南。方法上提出了R1-Code-Interpreter，通过对纯文本LLM进行多轮监督微调，并采用一种新颖的多阶段强化学习课程，该课程根据样本的改进潜力高低来优先训练。主要实验结果表明，该方法显著提升了性能，在37个测试任务上，14B模型的平均准确率从44.1%提高到72.4%，超越了纯文本的GPT-4o以及使用代码解释器的GPT-4o，同时通过代码生成展现了新兴的自我检查行为。
CNFP: Optimizing Cloud-Native Network Function Placement with Diffusion Models on the Cloud Continuum
Authors: Álvaro Vázquez Rodríguez, Manuel Fernández-Veiga, Carlos Giraldo-Rodríguez
First: 2025-11-03T08:47:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T21:23:44+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 11 figures, 4 tables, Submitted to Computer Networks
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The placement of Cloud-Native Network Functions across the Cloud-Continuum represents a core challenge in the orchestration of current 5G and future 6G networks. The process entails the implementation of interdependent computing tasks, which are structured as Service Function Chains, over distributed cloud infrastructures. This is achieved while satisfying strict resource, bandwidth, connectivity, and end-to-end latency constraints. It is widely acknowledged that classical approaches, including mixed-integer (non)linear programming, heuristics, and reinforcement learning, face practical limitations in terms of scalability, robust constraint handling, and generalization to unseen network conditions. In this study, a diffusion-based theoretical and algorithmic framework for CNF placement is proposed, based on Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Models. The placement process is reconceptualised as a conditional graph-to-assignment generation task. Each scenario is encoded as a heterogeneous graph, capturing infrastructure and service-chain structure. A Graph Neural Network denoiser is trained to iteratively refine noisy CNF-to-cloud assignment matrices. In order to bias the generation process towards valid deployments, the model incorporates constraint-aware penalties during training. At inference, a multitude of candidate placements are sampled, and the best suboptimal, feasible solution is selected. Extensive experimentation on diverse topologies, incorporating out-of-distribution evaluations with larger instances and shifted constraint regimes, demonstrates that the proposed approach consistently generates feasible solutions with considerably accelerated inference compared to other solvers. The findings of this study demonstrate the potential of diffusion-based generative modelling as a scalable tool for constrained network placement and embedding in cloud-continuum orchestration.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CNFP：基于扩散模型的云连续体上云原生网络功能优化部署
云原生网络功能在云连续体上的部署是当前5G及未来6G网络编排的核心挑战。该过程需要在分布式云基础设施上实现相互依赖的计算任务（以服务功能链形式组织），同时满足严格的资源、带宽、连通性和端到端时延约束。传统方法（包括混合整数（非）线性规划、启发式算法和强化学习）在可扩展性、鲁棒约束处理及对未知网络条件的泛化能力方面存在明显局限。本研究提出基于去噪扩散概率模型的扩散式理论与算法框架，将部署过程重新定义为条件图到分配生成的图生成任务。每个场景被编码为异质图以捕获基础设施与服务链结构，通过图神经网络去噪器迭代优化带噪声的CNF-云分配矩阵。为引导生成过程趋向有效部署，模型在训练中引入约束感知惩罚机制。推理阶段通过采样生成多组候选部署方案，并选择最优的可行次优解。在多样化拓扑结构上的实验（包含更大规模实例和偏移约束机制的分布外评估）表明，该方法能持续生成可行解，且推理速度显著优于其他求解器。本研究证实了基于扩散的生成模型可作为云连续体编排中约束网络部署与嵌入的可扩展工具。

Q-Measure-Learning for Continuous State RL: Efficient Implementation and Convergence
Authors: Shengbo Wang
First: 2026-03-03T21:15:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T21:15:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study reinforcement learning in infinite-horizon discounted Markov decision processes with continuous state spaces, where data are generated online from a single trajectory under a Markovian behavior policy. To avoid maintaining an infinite-dimensional, function-valued estimate, we propose the novel Q-Measure-Learning, which learns a signed empirical measure supported on visited state-action pairs and reconstructs an action-value estimate via kernel integration. The method jointly estimates the stationary distribution of the behavior chain and the Q-measure through coupled stochastic approximation, leading to an efficient weight-based implementation with $O(n)$ memory and $O(n)$ computation cost per iteration. Under uniform ergodicity of the behavior chain, we prove almost sure sup-norm convergence of the induced Q-function to the fixed point of a kernel-smoothed Bellman operator. We also bound the approximation error between this limit and the optimal $Q^*$ as a function of the kernel bandwidth. To assess the performance of our proposed algorithm, we conduct RL experiments in a two-item inventory control setting.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续状态强化学习的Q测度学习：高效实现与收敛性分析
本研究针对具有连续状态空间的无限时域折扣马尔可夫决策过程，探索在马尔可夫行为策略下通过单轨迹在线生成数据的强化学习。为避免维护无限维函数值估计，我们提出创新的Q测度学习方法：通过学习访问过的状态-动作对上的符号经验测度，并通过核积分重构动作值估计。该方法通过耦合随机逼近联合估计行为链的平稳分布与Q测度，实现了基于权重的高效实现——每次迭代仅需O(n)内存和O(n)计算成本。在行为链满足均匀遍历性的条件下，我们证明了诱导Q函数几乎必然以一致范数收敛至核平滑贝尔曼算子的不动点，并量化了该极限与最优Q*函数之间随核带宽变化的近似误差界限。为评估算法性能，我们在双物品库存控制场景中进行了强化学习实验。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of reinforcement learning in continuous state spaces, where traditional methods struggle with infinite-dimensional function estimation. The authors propose Q-Measure-Learning, a method that learns a signed empirical measure over visited state-action pairs and reconstructs action-value estimates via kernel integration, using coupled stochastic approximation to jointly estimate the behavior policy's stationary distribution and the Q-measure, achieving efficient O(n) memory and computation per iteration. Experimental results in a two-item inventory control setting demonstrate the method's practical viability, while theoretical analysis under uniform ergodicity shows almost sure sup-norm convergence to a kernel-smoothed Bellman operator fixed point, with approximation error to the optimal Q* bounded by kernel bandwidth.

Value Flows
Authors: Perry Dong, Chongyi Zheng, Chelsea Finn, Dorsa Sadigh, Benjamin Eysenbach
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-09T00:57:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T20:53:27+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3 · Project1
Abstract
While most reinforcement learning methods today flatten the distribution of future returns to a single scalar value, distributional RL methods exploit the return distribution to provide stronger learning signals and to enable applications in exploration and safe RL. While the predominant method for estimating the return distribution is by modeling it as a categorical distribution over discrete bins or estimating a finite number of quantiles, such approaches leave unanswered questions about the fine-grained structure of the return distribution and about how to distinguish states with high return uncertainty for decision-making. The key idea in this paper is to use modern, flexible flow-based models to estimate the full future return distributions and identify those states with high return variance. We do so by formulating a new flow-matching objective that generates probability density paths satisfying the distributional Bellman equation. Building upon the learned flow models, we estimate the return uncertainty of distinct states using a new flow derivative ODE. We additionally use this uncertainty information to prioritize learning a more accurate return estimation on certain transitions. We compare our method (Value Flows) with prior methods in the offline and online-to-online settings. Experiments on $37$ state-based and $25$ image-based benchmark tasks demonstrate that Value Flows achieves a $1.3\times$ improvement on average in success rates. Website: https://pd-perry.github.io/value-flows Code: https://github.com/chongyi-zheng/value-flows
中文标题/摘要
标题：价值流
当前多数强化学习方法将未来回报分布简化为单一标量值，而分布强化学习方法则利用回报分布提供更强的学习信号，并支持探索与安全强化学习的应用。主流方法通过离散区间分类分布或有限分位数估计来建模回报分布，但此类方法未能揭示回报分布的细粒度结构，亦未解决如何区分高回报不确定状态以辅助决策的问题。本文核心思想是采用现代灵活的流式模型估计完整未来回报分布，并识别高回报方差的状态。我们通过构建新的流匹配目标实现这一目标，该目标生成的概率密度路径满足分布贝尔曼方程。基于习得的流模型，我们通过新的流导数常微分方程估计不同状态的回报不确定性。此外，我们利用该不确定性信息优先学习特定状态转移的精确回报估计。我们将本方法（价值流）与离线及在线至在线场景的既有方法进行比较。在37个基于状态和25个基于图像的基准任务实验中，价值流平均实现1.3倍的成功率提升。网站：https://pd-perry.github.io/value-flows 代码：https://github.com/chongyi-zheng/value-flows
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitations of existing distributional reinforcement learning methods, which often model return distributions using discrete bins or quantiles, thereby obscuring fine-grained structural details and hindering the identification of states with high return uncertainty for decision-making. To address this, the authors propose Value Flows, a method that employs flexible flow-based models to estimate full future return distributions, introducing a flow-matching objective that satisfies the distributional Bellman equation and a flow derivative ODE to quantify return uncertainty, which is then used to prioritize learning on uncertain transitions. Experimental results across 37 state-based and 25 image-based benchmark tasks show that Value Flows achieves an average 1.3× improvement in success rates compared to prior methods in offline and online-to-online settings.
本文的动机在于现有分布强化学习方法通常使用离散区间或分位数建模回报分布，这掩盖了分布的细粒度结构细节，并阻碍了识别高回报不确定性状态以辅助决策。为此，作者提出了Value Flows方法，采用灵活的基于流的模型来估计完整的未来回报分布，通过引入满足分布贝尔曼方程的流匹配目标和一个用于量化回报不确定性的流导数常微分方程，并利用该不确定性信息优先学习不确定的转移。在37个基于状态和25个基于图像的基准任务上的实验结果表明，与先前方法相比，Value Flows在离线和在线到在线设置中平均实现了1.3倍的成功率提升。
PhyPrompt: RL-based Prompt Refinement for Physically Plausible Text-to-Video Generation
Authors: Shang Wu, Chenwei Xu, Zhuofan Xia, Weijian Li, Lie Lu, Pranav Maneriker, Fan Du, Manling Li, Han Liu
First: 2026-03-03T20:26:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T20:26:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
State-of-the-art text-to-video (T2V) generators frequently violate physical laws despite high visual quality. We show this stems from insufficient physical constraints in prompts rather than model limitations: manually adding physics details reliably produces physically plausible videos, but requires expertise and does not scale. We present PhyPrompt, a two-stage reinforcement learning framework that automatically refines prompts for physically realistic generation. First, we fine-tune a large language model on a physics-focused Chain-of-Thought dataset to integrate principles like object motion and force interactions while preserving user intent. Second, we apply Group Relative Policy Optimization with a dynamic reward curriculum that initially prioritizes semantic fidelity, then progressively shifts toward physical commonsense. This curriculum achieves synergistic optimization: PhyPrompt-7B reaches 40.8\% joint success on VideoPhy2 (8.6pp gain), improving physical commonsense by 11pp (55.8\% to 66.8\%) while simultaneously increasing semantic adherence by 4.4pp (43.4\% to 47.8\%). Remarkably, our curriculum exceeds single-objective training on both metrics, demonstrating compositional prompt discovery beyond conventional multi-objective trade-offs. PhyPrompt outperforms GPT-4o (+3.8\% joint) and DeepSeek-V3 (+2.2\%, 100$\times$ larger) using only 7B parameters. The approach transfers zero-shot across diverse T2V architectures (Lavie, VideoCrafter2, CogVideoX-5B) with up to 16.8\% improvement, establishing that domain-specialized reinforcement learning with compositional curricula surpasses general-purpose scaling for physics-aware generation.

标题：PhyPrompt：基于强化学习的物理合理文本到视频生成提示词优化框架
当前最先进的文本到视频生成器虽具备高视觉质量，却常违背物理定律。研究表明这源于提示词中物理约束的不足而非模型局限：人工添加物理细节虽能可靠生成物理合理的视频，但需专业知识且难以规模化。本文提出PhyPrompt——一个两阶段强化学习框架，可自动优化提示词以实现物理真实的生成。首先，我们在专注物理的思维链数据集上微调大语言模型，使其在保持用户意图的同时整合物体运动与力相互作用等原理。其次，采用动态奖励课程的组相对策略优化：初期优先语义保真度，随后逐步转向物理常识。该课程实现协同优化：PhyPrompt-7B在VideoPhy2数据集上达到40.8%的联合成功率（提升8.6个百分点），物理常识得分提升11个百分点（55.8%→66.8%），同时语义遵循度提升4.4个百分点（43.4%→47.8%）。值得注意的是，该课程在两项指标上均超越单目标训练，证明了超越传统多目标权衡的组合式提示词发现能力。PhyPrompt仅用70亿参数即超越GPT-4o（联合成功率+3.8%）和参数量百倍于己的DeepSeek-V3（+2.2%）。该方法在多种T2V架构（Lavie、VideoCrafter2、CogVideoX-5B）上实现零样本迁移，最高提升16.8%，证实了组合课程与领域专业化强化学习在物理感知生成任务上优于通用规模化扩展。

Agile Flight Emerges from Multi-Agent Competitive Racing
Authors: Vineet Pasumarti, Lorenzo Bianchi, Antonio Loquercio
First: 2025-12-12T18:48:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T20:25:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Through multi-agent competition and the sparse high-level objective of winning a race, we find that both agile flight (e.g., high-speed motion pushing the platform to its physical limits) and strategy (e.g., overtaking or blocking) emerge from agents trained with reinforcement learning. We provide evidence in both simulation and the real world that this approach outperforms the common paradigm of training agents in isolation with rewards that prescribe behavior, e.g., progress on the raceline, in particular when the complexity of the environment increases, e.g., in the presence of obstacles. Moreover, we find that multi-agent competition yields policies that transfer more reliably to the real world than policies trained with a single-agent progress-based reward, despite the two methods using the same simulation environment, randomization strategy, and hardware. In addition to improved sim-to-real transfer, the multi-agent policies also exhibit some degree of generalization to opponents unseen at training time. Overall, our work, following in the tradition of multi-agent competitive game-play in digital domains, shows that sparse task-level rewards are sufficient for training agents capable of advanced low-level control in the physical world. Code: https://github.com/Jirl-upenn/AgileFlight_MultiAgent

Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of developing agile robotic flight and strategic behaviors without prescribing detailed rewards, this paper employs multi-agent competitive reinforcement learning, where agents are trained solely with the sparse objective of winning a race. The method involves training agents against each other in simulation, which leads to the emergence of both high-speed, limit-pushing flight maneuvers and strategic actions like overtaking and blocking. Experimental results in simulation and real-world tests demonstrate that this competitive approach outperforms single-agent training with progress-based rewards, especially in complex environments with obstacles, and shows superior sim-to-real transfer and some generalization to unseen opponents.
本研究旨在无需预设详细奖励的情况下，开发敏捷的机器人飞行和策略行为，其方法采用多智能体竞争性强化学习，仅以赢得比赛这一稀疏目标训练智能体。通过在模拟环境中让智能体相互竞争，该方法自发涌现出高速、逼近物理极限的飞行动作以及超车、阻挡等策略。实验结果表明，在模拟和真实世界中，这种竞争方法优于基于进度奖励的单智能体训练，尤其在存在障碍的复杂环境中表现更佳，并展现出更好的仿真到现实迁移能力以及对未见过对手的一定泛化性。
Phys4D: Fine-Grained Physics-Consistent 4D Modeling from Video Diffusion
Authors: Haoran Lu, Shang Wu, Jianshu Zhang, Maojiang Su, Guo Ye, Chenwei Xu, Lie Lu, Pranav Maneriker, Fan Du, Manling Li, Zhaoran Wang, Han Liu
First: 2026-03-03T20:01:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T20:01:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent video diffusion models have achieved impressive capabilities as large-scale generative world models. However, these models often struggle with fine-grained physical consistency, exhibiting physically implausible dynamics over time. In this work, we present \textbf{Phys4D}, a pipeline for learning physics-consistent 4D world representations from video diffusion models. Phys4D adopts \textbf{a three-stage training paradigm} that progressively lifts appearance-driven video diffusion models into physics-consistent 4D world representations. We first bootstrap robust geometry and motion representations through large-scale pseudo-supervised pretraining, establishing a foundation for 4D scene modeling. We then perform physics-grounded supervised fine-tuning using simulation-generated data, enforcing temporally consistent 4D dynamics. Finally, we apply simulation-grounded reinforcement learning to correct residual physical violations that are difficult to capture through explicit supervision. To evaluate fine-grained physical consistency beyond appearance-based metrics, we introduce a set of \textbf{4D world consistency evaluation} that probe geometric coherence, motion stability, and long-horizon physical plausibility. Experimental results demonstrate that Phys4D substantially improves fine-grained spatiotemporal and physical consistency compared to appearance-driven baselines, while maintaining strong generative performance. Our project page is available at https://sensational-brioche-7657e7.netlify.app/

Optimal trajectory-guided stochastic co-optimization for e-fuel system design and real-time operation
Authors: Jeongdong Kim, Minsu Kim, Jonggeol Na, Junghwan Kim
First: 2026-03-03T20:00:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T20:00:39+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, 6 figures. Supplementary Information included
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
E-fuels are promising long-term energy carriers supporting the net-zero transition. However, the large combinatorial design-operation spaces under renewable uncertainty make the use of mathematical programming impractical for co-optimizing e-fuel production systems. Here, we present MasCOR, a machine-learning-assisted co-optimization framework that learns from global operational trajectories. By encoding system design and renewable trends, a single MasCOR agent generalizes dynamic operation across diverse configurations and scenarios, substantially simplifying design-operation co-optimization under uncertainty. Benchmark comparisons against state-of-the-art reinforcement learning baselines demonstrate near-optimal performance, while computational costs are substantially lower than those of mathematical programming, enabling rapid parallel evaluation of designs within the co-optimization loop. This framework enables rapid screening of feasible design spaces together with corresponding operational policies. When applied to four potential European sites targeting e-methanol production, MasCOR shows that most locations benefit from reducing system load below 50 MW to achieve carbon-neutral methanol production, with production costs of 1.0-1.2 USD per kg. In contrast, Dunkirk (France), with limited renewable availability and high grid prices, favors system loads above 200 MW and expanded storage to exploit dynamic grid exchange and hydrogen sales to the market. These results underscore the value of the MasCOR framework for site-specific guidance from system design to real-time operation.

Minimax Optimal Strategy for Delayed Observations in Online Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Harin Lee, Kevin Jamieson
First: 2026-03-03T19:52:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T19:52:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study reinforcement learning with delayed state observation, where the agent observes the current state after some random number of time steps. We propose an algorithm that combines the augmentation method and the upper confidence bound approach. For tabular Markov decision processes (MDPs), we derive a regret bound of $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(H \sqrt{D_{\max} SAK})$, where $S$ and $A$ are the cardinalities of the state and action spaces, $H$ is the time horizon, $K$ is the number of episodes, and $D_{\max}$ is the maximum length of the delay. We also provide a matching lower bound up to logarithmic factors, showing the optimality of our approach. Our analytical framework formulates this problem as a special case of a broader class of MDPs, where their transition dynamics decompose into a known component and an unknown but structured component. We establish general results for this abstract setting, which may be of independent interest.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在线强化学习中延迟观测的极小极大最优策略
我们研究了状态观测存在延迟的强化学习问题，其中智能体需经过随机时间步后才能观测当前状态。我们提出了一种结合状态增广方法与置信上界方法的算法。针对表格型马尔可夫决策过程，推导出遗憾上界为$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(H \sqrt{D_{\max} SAK})$，其中$S$和$A$分别表示状态空间与动作空间的基数，$H$为时间跨度，$K$为回合数，$D_{\max}$为最大延迟长度。同时给出了对数因子范围内的匹配下界，证明了方法的渐进最优性。我们的分析框架将该问题建模为一类广义MDP的特例，其转移动力学可分解为已知分量与具有结构特性的未知分量。针对这一抽象设定建立的理论结果可能具有独立的研究价值。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of delayed state observations in online reinforcement learning, where agents receive state information after random delays, complicating real-time decision-making. The authors propose an algorithm that integrates state augmentation with an upper confidence bound (UCB) approach to manage uncertainty from delays. For tabular Markov decision processes, they derive a regret bound of ˜O(H√(D_max SAK)), which is shown to be minimax optimal via a matching lower bound, confirming the algorithm's efficiency in handling delayed feedback. Their framework generalizes the problem to MDPs with decomposable transition dynamics, offering analytical tools that may benefit broader RL research.
本文研究了在线强化学习中状态观测延迟的问题，即智能体在随机延迟后接收到状态信息，这给实时决策带来了困难。作者提出了一种算法，结合状态增广和上置信界方法，以处理延迟带来的不确定性。针对表格型马尔可夫决策过程，他们推导出˜O(H√(D_max SAK))的遗憾界，并通过匹配的下界证明该界是最小化最优的，从而验证了算法在处理延迟反馈时的有效性。该框架将问题推广到具有可分解转移动态的MDP中，提供了可能对更广泛强化学习研究有价值的分析工具。
[Re] FairDICE: A Gap Between Theory And Practice
Authors: Peter Adema, Karim Galliamov, Aleksey Evstratovskiy, Ross Geurts
First: 2026-03-03T19:12:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T19:12:06+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 8 figures in main text. Code at https://github.com/p-adema/re-fairdice
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Offline Reinforcement Learning (RL) is an emerging field of RL in which policies are learned solely from demonstrations. Within offline RL, some environments involve balancing multiple objectives, but existing multi-objective offline RL algorithms do not provide an efficient way to find a fair compromise. FairDICE (see arXiv:2506.08062v2) seeks to fill this gap by adapting OptiDICE (an offline RL algorithm) to automatically learn weights for multiple objectives to e.g.\ incentivise fairness among objectives. As this would be a valuable contribution, this replication study examines the replicability of claims made regarding FairDICE. We find that many theoretical claims hold, but an error in the code reduces FairDICE to standard behaviour cloning in continuous environments, and many important hyperparameters were originally underspecified. After rectifying this, we show in experiments extending the original paper that FairDICE can scale to complex environments and high-dimensional rewards, though it can be reliant on (online) hyperparameter tuning. We conclude that FairDICE is a theoretically interesting method, but the experimental justification requires significant revision.
中文标题/摘要
标题：[复现] FairDICE：理论与实践之间的差距
离线强化学习是强化学习的新兴领域，其策略仅从演示数据中学习。在离线强化学习中，部分环境涉及多目标平衡，但现有算法未提供寻找公平折衷的有效方法。FairDICE（参见arXiv:2506.08062v2）通过改进OptiDICE算法，实现了多目标权重的自动学习以促进目标间公平性。本研究检验了FairDICE声明的可复现性，发现其理论主张基本成立，但代码错误导致连续环境中算法退化为标准行为克隆，且关键超参数原定义模糊。修正后，扩展实验表明FairDICE可扩展至复杂环境与高维奖励空间，但对（在线）超参数调优存在依赖。结论认为该方法理论价值显著，但实验论证需重大修订。
Summary / 总结
This replication study investigates FairDICE, a method proposed to address fairness in multi-objective offline reinforcement learning by automatically learning objective weights. The authors find that while the theoretical claims largely hold, a coding error in the original implementation reduces the algorithm to standard behavior cloning in continuous environments, and key hyperparameters were underspecified. After correcting these issues, extended experiments demonstrate that FairDICE can scale to complex environments and high-dimensional rewards, though its performance often depends on online hyperparameter tuning, indicating that the experimental justification requires significant revision despite the method's theoretical interest.
这项复制研究考察了FairDICE方法，该方法旨在通过自动学习目标权重来解决多目标离线强化学习中的公平性问题。研究发现，尽管其理论主张基本成立，但原始代码中的一个错误导致该算法在连续环境中退化为标准的行为克隆，且关键超参数最初未明确指定。修正这些问题后，扩展实验表明FairDICE能够扩展到复杂环境和高维奖励，但其性能常依赖于在线超参数调优，因此尽管方法具有理论价值，其实验论证仍需重大修订。
Geometry-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Multi-view Consistent 3D Scene Editing
Authors: Jiyuan Wang, Chunyu Lin, Lei Sun, Zhi Cao, Yuyang Yin, Lang Nie, Zhenlong Yuan, Xiangxiang Chu, Yunchao Wei, Kang Liao, Guosheng Lin
First: 2026-03-03T16:31:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T16:31:10+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Leveraging the priors of 2D diffusion models for 3D editing has emerged as a promising paradigm. However, maintaining multi-view consistency in edited results remains challenging, and the extreme scarcity of 3D-consistent editing paired data renders supervised fine-tuning (SFT), the most effective training strategy for editing tasks, infeasible. In this paper, we observe that, while generating multi-view consistent 3D content is highly challenging, verifying 3D consistency is tractable, naturally positioning reinforcement learning (RL) as a feasible solution. Motivated by this, we propose \textbf{RL3DEdit}, a single-pass framework driven by RL optimization with novel rewards derived from the 3D foundation model, VGGT. Specifically, we leverage VGGT's robust priors learned from massive real-world data, feed the edited images, and utilize the output confidence maps and pose estimation errors as reward signals, effectively anchoring the 2D editing priors onto a 3D-consistent manifold via RL. Extensive experiments demonstrate that RL3DEdit achieves stable multi-view consistency and outperforms state-of-the-art methods in editing quality with high efficiency. To promote the development of 3D editing, we will release the code and model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：几何引导的强化学习实现多视角一致的3D场景编辑
利用二维扩散模型先验进行三维编辑已成为前景广阔的研究范式。然而，保持编辑结果的多视角一致性仍具挑战性，且三维一致性编辑配对数据的极度稀缺使得监督微调——编辑任务最有效的训练策略——难以实施。本文发现，虽然生成多视角一致的三维内容极具挑战性，但验证三维一致性是可行的，这自然使强化学习成为可行的解决方案。基于此，我们提出\textbf{RL3DEdit}，这是一个由强化学习优化的单次处理框架，其创新奖励信号源自三维基础模型VGGT。具体而言，我们利用VGGT从海量真实数据中学到的鲁棒先验，输入编辑后的图像，并将输出的置信度图与姿态估计误差作为奖励信号，通过强化学习将二维编辑先验有效锚定在三维一致性流形上。大量实验表明，RL3DEdit在实现稳定多视角一致性的同时，以高效性在编辑质量上超越现有最优方法。为促进三维编辑领域发展，我们将公开代码与模型。

The method uses novel reward signals derived from a 3D foundation model (VGGT), specifically its confidence maps and pose estimation errors, to guide the RL optimization and anchor 2D editing priors onto a 3D-consistent manifold. Experimental results show that RL3DEdit achieves stable multi-view consistency, outperforms state-of-the-art methods in editing quality, and operates efficiently.

Proactive Guiding Strategy for Item-side Fairness in Interactive Recommendation
Authors: Chongjun Xia, Xiaoyu Shi, Hong Xie, Xianzhi Wang, yun lu, Mingsheng Shang
First: 2026-03-03T15:32:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T15:32:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Item-side fairness is crucial for ensuring the fair exposure of long-tail items in interactive recommender systems. Existing approaches promote the exposure of long-tail items by directly incorporating them into recommended results. This causes misalignment between user preferences and the recommended long-tail items, which hinders long-term user engagement and reduces the effectiveness of recommendations. We aim for a proactive fairness-guiding strategy, which actively guides user preferences toward long-tail items while preserving user satisfaction during the interactive recommendation process. To this end, we propose HRL4PFG, an interactive recommendation framework that leverages hierarchical reinforcement learning to guide user preferences toward long-tail items progressively. HRL4PFG operates through a macro-level process that generates fairness-guided targets based on multi-step feedback, and a micro-level process that fine-tunes recommendations in real time according to both these targets and evolving user preferences. Extensive experiments show that HRL4PFG improves cumulative interaction rewards and maximum user interaction length by a larger margin when compared with state-of-the-art methods in interactive recommendation environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：交互式推荐中面向项目侧公平性的主动引导策略
项目侧公平性对于确保交互式推荐系统中长尾项目的公平曝光至关重要。现有方法通过直接将长尾项目纳入推荐结果来促进其曝光，但这会导致用户偏好与推荐的长尾项目之间不匹配，从而阻碍长期用户参与度并降低推荐效果。我们提出一种主动公平引导策略，在交互推荐过程中积极引导用户偏好向长尾项目倾斜，同时保持用户满意度。为此，我们提出HRL4PFG框架，该框架利用分层强化学习逐步引导用户偏好转向长尾项目。HRL4PFG通过宏观层面（基于多步反馈生成公平引导目标）和微观层面（根据这些目标及动态用户偏好实时微调推荐）协同运作。大量实验表明，在交互推荐环境中，与前沿方法相比，HRL4PFG能更大程度提升累积交互奖励和最大用户交互长度。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to ensure fair exposure for long-tail items in interactive recommender systems without compromising user satisfaction, this paper introduces HRL4PFG, a proactive fairness-guiding strategy using hierarchical reinforcement learning. The method employs a macro-level process to set fairness targets based on multi-step feedback and a micro-level process to adjust recommendations in real time, aligning user preferences with long-tail items gradually. Experimental results demonstrate that HRL4PFG outperforms state-of-the-art methods by significantly enhancing cumulative interaction rewards and extending maximum user interaction length in interactive recommendation environments.

RAPO: Expanding Exploration for LLM Agents via Retrieval-Augmented Policy Optimization
Authors: Siwei Zhang, Yun Xiong, Xi Chen, Zi'an Jia, Renhong Huang, Jiarong Xu, Jiawei Zhang
Venue: KDD 2026
First: 2026-03-03T15:23:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T15:23:42+00:00
Comments: Submit to KDD 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic Reinforcement Learning (Agentic RL) has shown remarkable potential in large language model-based (LLM) agents. These works can empower LLM agents to tackle complex tasks via multi-step, tool-integrated reasoning. However, an inherent limitation of existing Agentic RL methods is their reliance on a pure on-policy paradigm for exploration, restricting exploration to the agent's self-generated outputs and preventing the discovery of new reasoning perspectives for further improvement. While recent efforts incorporate auxiliary off-policy signals to enhance exploration, they typically utilize full off-policy trajectories for trajectory-level policy estimation, overlooking the necessity for the fine-grained, step-level exploratory dynamics within agentic rollout. In this paper, we revisit exploration in Agentic RL and propose Retrieval-Augmented Policy Optimization (RAPO), a novel RL framework that introduces retrieval to explicitly expand exploration during training. To achieve this, we decompose the Agentic RL training process into two phases: (i) Hybrid-policy Agentic Rollout, and (ii) Retrieval-aware Policy Optimization. Specifically, we propose a Hybrid-policy Agentic Rollout strategy, which allows the agents to continuously reason over the retrieved off-policy step-level traces. It dynamically extends the reasoning receptive field of agents, enabling broader exploration conditioned on external behaviors. Subsequently, we introduce the Retrieval-aware Policy Optimization mechanism, which calibrates the policy gradient estimation with retrieval reward and importance shaping, stabilizing training and prioritizing retrieval-illuminating exploration. Extensive experiments show that RAPO achieves an +5.0% average gain on fourteen datasets across three agentic reasoning tasks, while delivering 1.2x faster training efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RAPO：基于检索增强策略优化的LLM智能体探索扩展方法
智能体强化学习在基于大语言模型的智能体中展现出显著潜力，能通过多步骤工具集成推理处理复杂任务。然而现有方法依赖纯在线策略探索范式，将探索局限在智能体自身生成的结果中，难以发现新的推理视角以实现改进。虽然近期研究引入辅助离线策略信号增强探索，但通常采用完整轨迹进行策略估计，忽略了智能体推演过程中细粒度步骤级探索动态的必要性。本文重新审视智能体强化学习的探索机制，提出检索增强策略优化框架，通过显式引入检索扩展训练期间的探索空间。具体实现分为两个阶段：（1）混合策略智能体推演：设计混合策略推演策略，使智能体能持续基于检索的离线策略步骤级轨迹进行推理，动态扩展智能体的推理感知域，实现基于外部行为的广谱探索；（2）检索感知策略优化：通过检索奖励与重要性加权校准策略梯度估计，稳定训练过程并优先促进具有检索启发性的探索。在三个智能体推理任务的十四组数据集上的实验表明，RAPO平均性能提升达5.0%，同时训练效率提升1.2倍。

To overcome this, the authors propose Retrieval-Augmented Policy Optimization (RAPO), a novel RL framework that introduces retrieval to explicitly expand exploration during training through a two-phase process: Hybrid-policy Agentic Rollout, which allows agents to reason over retrieved off-policy step-level traces to broaden exploration, and Retrieval-aware Policy Optimization, which calibrates policy gradient estimation with retrieval reward and importance shaping to stabilize training. Experimental results demonstrate that RAPO achieves an average performance gain of +5.0% across fourteen datasets in three agentic reasoning tasks while improving training efficiency by 1.2 times.
本文针对现有智能体强化学习方法依赖纯在线策略探索的局限性，即智能体仅能基于自身生成输出进行探索，难以发现新的推理视角。为此，作者提出了检索增强策略优化（RAPO），这是一种新颖的强化学习框架，通过引入检索在训练中显式扩展探索，包含两个阶段：混合策略智能体推演，允许智能体基于检索的离线策略步骤级轨迹进行推理以拓宽探索；以及检索感知策略优化，通过检索奖励和重要性调整来校准策略梯度估计，从而稳定训练。实验结果表明，RAPO在三个智能体推理任务的十四个数据集上平均性能提升5.0%，同时训练效率提高1.2倍。
TikZilla: Scaling Text-to-TikZ with High-Quality Data and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Christian Greisinger, Steffen Eger
First: 2026-03-03T15:17:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T15:17:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to assist scientists across diverse workflows. A key challenge is generating high-quality figures from textual descriptions, often represented as TikZ programs that can be rendered as scientific images. Prior research has proposed a variety of datasets and modeling approaches for this task. However, existing datasets for Text-to-TikZ are too small and noisy to capture the complexity of TikZ, causing mismatches between text and rendered figures. Moreover, prior approaches rely solely on supervised fine-tuning (SFT), which does not expose the model to the rendered semantics of the figure, often resulting in errors such as looping, irrelevant content, and incorrect spatial relations. To address these issues, we construct DaTikZ-V4, a dataset more than four times larger and substantially higher in quality than DaTikZ-V3, enriched with LLM-generated figure descriptions. Using this dataset, we train TikZilla, a family of small open-source Qwen models (3B and 8B) with a two-stage pipeline of SFT followed by reinforcement learning (RL). For RL, we leverage an image encoder trained via inverse graphics to provide semantically faithful reward signals. Extensive human evaluations with over 1,000 judgments show that TikZilla improves by 1.5-2 points over its base models on a 5-point scale, surpasses GPT-4o by 0.5 points, and matches GPT-5 in the image-based evaluation, while operating at much smaller model sizes. Code, data, and models will be made available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TikZilla：通过高质量数据与强化学习实现文本到TikZ的规模化生成
大语言模型（LLMs）正日益广泛地辅助科学家完成多样化工作流程。其中关键挑战在于从文本描述生成高质量图表，这类描述常以可渲染为科学图像的TikZ程序表示。先前研究已为此任务提出了多种数据集与建模方法。然而，现有文本到TikZ的数据集规模过小且噪声较多，难以捕捉TikZ的复杂性，导致文本与渲染图像间存在偏差。此外，现有方法仅依赖监督微调（SFT），未让模型接触图像的渲染语义，常产生循环结构、无关内容及错误空间关系等问题。为解决这些缺陷，我们构建了DaTikZ-V4数据集，其规模超DaTikZ-V3四倍以上，质量显著提升，并融合了LLM生成的图表描述。基于此数据集，我们训练了TikZilla系列模型——采用3B与8B参数量的小型开源Qwen模型，通过监督微调与强化学习（RL）两阶段流程实现。在强化学习阶段，我们利用通过逆向图形训练的图像编码器提供语义保真的奖励信号。超过1000次人工评估表明：在5分量表中，TikZilla较其基础模型提升1.5-2分，超越GPT-4o 0.5分，在基于图像的评估中与GPT-5表现相当，而模型规模显著更小。代码、数据与模型将公开提供。

Experimental results from human evaluations with over 1,000 judgments show that TikZilla improves by 1.5-2 points over base models on a 5-point scale, surpasses GPT-4o by 0.5 points, and matches GPT-5 in image-based evaluation, despite operating at much smaller model sizes.
该论文针对从文本描述生成高质量科学图表（使用TikZ代码）的挑战，指出现有数据集规模过小且噪声多，仅依赖监督微调无法捕捉渲染语义，导致循环、无关内容和空间关系错误等问题。为解决这些问题，作者构建了DaTikZ-V4数据集，其规模和质量均超过前代版本四倍以上，并利用大语言模型生成的描述进行增强，随后采用两阶段流程训练TikZilla模型（3B和8B Qwen）：先进行监督微调，再通过强化学习结合基于逆向图形训练的图像编码器提供奖励信号。实验结果表明，在超过1000次人工评估中，TikZilla在5分制上比基础模型提升1.5-2分，超越GPT-4o 0.5分，并在基于图像的评估中与GPT-5持平，同时模型规模更小。
Reinforcement Learning with Symbolic Reward Machines
Authors: Thomas Krug, Daniel Neider
First: 2026-03-03T15:11:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T15:11:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward Machines (RMs) are an established mechanism in Reinforcement Learning (RL) to represent and learn sparse, temporally extended tasks with non-Markovian rewards. RMs rely on high-level information in the form of labels that are emitted by the environment alongside the observation. However, this concept requires manual user input for each environment and task. The user has to create a suitable labeling function that computes the labels. These limitations lead to poor applicability in widely adopted RL frameworks. We propose Symbolic Reward Machines (SRMs) together with the learning algorithms QSRM and LSRM to overcome the limitations of RMs. SRMs consume only the standard output of the environment and process the observation directly through guards that are represented by symbolic formulas. In our evaluation, our SRM methods outperform the baseline RL approaches and generate the same results as the existing RM methods. At the same time, our methods adhere to the widely used environment definition and provide interpretable representations of the task to the user.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于符号奖励机制的强化学习
奖励机制（RMs）是强化学习（RL）中用于表示和学习具有非马尔可夫奖励的稀疏、时间扩展任务的成熟机制。RMs依赖环境随观察结果同时发出的标签形式的高层信息。然而，这一概念需要用户为每个环境和任务手动输入，必须创建合适的标签函数来计算标签。这些限制导致其在广泛采用的RL框架中适用性较差。我们提出符号奖励机制（SRMs）及相应的QSRM和LSRM学习算法，以克服RMs的局限性。SRMs仅消耗环境的标准输出，并通过符号公式表示的守卫直接处理观察结果。在我们的评估中，SRM方法优于基线RL方法，并产生与现有RM方法相同的结果。同时，我们的方法遵循广泛使用的环境定义，并向用户提供可解释的任务表示。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of Reward Machines (RMs) in reinforcement learning, which require manual design of labeling functions for each environment and task, hindering broad applicability. The method introduces Symbolic Reward Machines (SRMs) with algorithms QSRM and LSRM, which process raw observations directly using symbolic formulas as guards, eliminating the need for pre-defined labels. Experimental results show that SRM methods outperform baseline RL approaches and match the performance of existing RM methods while adhering to standard environment definitions and providing interpretable task representations.
本研究的动机是克服强化学习中奖励机器的局限性，后者需要为每个环境和任务手动设计标签函数，阻碍了广泛应用。方法上提出了符号奖励机器及其学习算法QSRM和LSRM，通过符号公式作为守卫直接处理原始观察，无需预定义标签。实验结果表明，SRM方法优于基线强化学习方法，与现有RM方法性能相当，同时遵循标准环境定义并提供可解释的任务表示。
Learning Acrobatic Flight from Preferences
Authors: Colin Merk, Ismail Geles, Jiaxu Xing, Angel Romero, Giorgia Ramponi, Davide Scaramuzza
First: 2025-08-26T08:56:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T14:35:14+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Preference-based reinforcement learning (PbRL) enables agents to learn control policies without requiring manually designed reward functions, making it well-suited for tasks where objectives are difficult to formalize or inherently subjective. Acrobatic flight poses a particularly challenging problem due to its complex dynamics, rapid movements, and the importance of precise execution. However, manually designed reward functions for such tasks often fail to capture the qualities that matter: we find that hand-crafted rewards agree with human judgment only 60.7% of the time, underscoring the need for preference-driven approaches. In this work, we propose Reward Ensemble under Confidence (REC), a probabilistic reward learning framework for PbRL that explicitly models per-timestep reward uncertainty through an ensemble of distributional reward models. By propagating uncertainty into the preference loss and leveraging disagreement for exploration, REC achieves 88.4% of shaped reward performance on acrobatic quadrotor control, compared to 55.2% with standard Preference PPO. We train policies in simulation and successfully transfer them zero-shot to the real world, demonstrating complex acrobatic maneuvers learned purely from preference feedback. We further validate REC on a continuous control benchmark, confirming its applicability beyond the domain of aerial robotics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于偏好的特技飞行学习
基于偏好的强化学习（PbRL）使智能体无需手动设计奖励函数即可学习控制策略，这使其特别适用于目标难以形式化或本质主观的任务。特技飞行因其复杂的动力学特性、快速运动以及精确执行的重要性而构成一个极具挑战性的问题。然而，为此类任务手动设计的奖励函数往往难以捕捉关键质量：我们发现人工设计的奖励与人类判断的一致性仅为60.7%，这凸显了对偏好驱动方法的需求。在本研究中，我们提出置信度下的奖励集成（REC），这是一个用于PbRL的概率奖励学习框架，通过一组分布式奖励模型显式建模每个时间步的奖励不确定性。通过将不确定性传播至偏好损失函数，并利用分歧进行探索，REC在特技四旋翼控制任务中达到了人工设计奖励性能的88.4%，而标准偏好PPO仅为55.2%。我们在仿真环境中训练策略，并成功将其零样本迁移至现实世界，展示了完全从偏好反馈中学习的复杂特技飞行动作。我们还在连续控制基准测试中进一步验证了REC，证实了其适用于空中机器人领域之外的任务。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that manually designing reward functions for complex tasks like acrobatic flight is difficult and often misaligned with human judgment, agreeing only 60.7% of the time, so preference-based reinforcement learning (PbRL) is needed to learn from subjective feedback. The method introduces Reward Ensemble under Confidence (REC), a probabilistic framework that models reward uncertainty using an ensemble of distributional reward models, incorporating this uncertainty into the preference loss and using model disagreement to guide exploration. The main experimental results show that REC achieves 88.4% of the performance of a shaped reward on acrobatic quadrotor control, significantly outperforming standard Preference PPO at 55.2%, and successfully transfers learned policies zero-shot from simulation to real-world drones, demonstrating complex maneuvers learned purely from preferences, with additional validation on a continuous control benchmark confirming broader applicability.
本研究的动机在于，对于特技飞行等复杂任务，手动设计奖励函数十分困难，且常与人类判断不一致（仅60.7%的吻合度），因此需要基于偏好的强化学习（PbRL）来从主观反馈中学习。方法上提出了“置信度下的奖励集成”（REC），这是一个概率性框架，通过集成分布奖励模型来建模奖励不确定性，并将不确定性融入偏好损失函数中，同时利用模型分歧来引导探索。主要实验结果表明，REC在特技四旋翼控制任务中达到了人工设计奖励性能的88.4%，显著优于标准偏好PPO的55.2%，并且成功将策略从仿真零样本迁移到真实无人机上，实现了仅从偏好反馈学习的复杂特技动作，在连续控制基准上的进一步验证也证实了其超越空中机器人领域的适用性。
Why Does RLAIF Work At All?
Authors: Robin Young
First: 2026-03-03T13:51:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:51:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF) enables language models to improve by training on their own preference judgments, yet no theoretical account explains why this self-improvement seemingly works for value learning. We propose the latent value hypothesis, that pretraining on internet-scale data encodes human values as directions in representation space, and constitutional prompts elicit these latent values into preference judgments. We formalize this intuition under a linear model where the constitution acts as a projection operator selecting value-relevant directions. Our analysis yields several results. RLAIF improves alignment when the constitution-activated direction correlates with true values better than the model's default generation direction thus explaining the generation-judgment gap; the ceiling on RLAIF quality is determined by how well representations encode values, which scales with model capacity; and adversarial constitutions exist that can activate anti-social value directions encoded from harmful pretraining data. Our account unifies scattered empirical findings including the refusal direction, low-rank safety subspaces, and RLAIF scaling behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLAIF为何有效？
基于AI反馈的强化学习（RLAIF）使语言模型能通过自身偏好判断进行训练以提升性能，但尚无理论解释这种自我改进为何在价值学习上有效。我们提出潜在价值假说：互联网规模数据的预训练将人类价值编码为表征空间中的方向，而宪法式提示将这些潜在价值激发为偏好判断。我们在线性模型下形式化这一直觉，将宪法视为选择价值相关方向的投影算子。分析得出多项结论：当宪法激活的方向比模型默认生成方向更贴合真实价值时，RLAIF能提升对齐效果，这解释了生成-判断差距；RLAIF的质量上限取决于表征编码价值的完整度，其随模型能力扩展；存在对抗性宪法可激活从有害预训练数据编码的反社会价值方向。该理论统一了包括拒绝方向、低秩安全子空间和RLAIF扩展行为在内的分散实证发现。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the lack of theoretical understanding for why Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF) effectively enables language models to self-improve via their own preference judgments. The authors propose the latent value hypothesis, which posits that pretraining embeds human values as directions in representation space, and constitutional prompts act as projection operators to elicit these latent values for judgment. Their formal linear model analysis shows that RLAIF improves alignment when the constitution-activated direction better correlates with true values than the default generation direction, explains the generation-judgment gap, establishes that performance ceilings depend on how well representations encode values (scaling with model capacity), and reveals that adversarial constitutions can activate harmful value directions from pretraining data. This theoretical account unifies empirical observations such as refusal directions, low-rank safety subspaces, and RLAIF scaling behavior.
本文的动机在于缺乏理论解释为何基于人工智能反馈的强化学习（RLAIF）能通过模型自身的偏好判断有效实现自我改进。作者提出了潜在价值假说，认为预训练将人类价值编码为表示空间中的方向，而宪法提示作为投影算子来激发这些潜在价值以进行判断。通过形式化的线性模型分析，研究表明当宪法激活的方向比默认生成方向更贴合真实价值时，RLAIF能提升对齐性，这解释了生成与判断之间的差距；同时指出性能上限取决于表示编码价值的效果（随模型能力扩展），并揭示对抗性宪法可能激活预训练数据中的有害价值方向。该理论框架统一了包括拒绝方向、低秩安全子空间和RLAIF扩展行为在内的多项实证发现。
Contextualized Privacy Defense for LLM Agents
Authors: Yule Wen, Yanzhe Zhang, Jianxun Lian, Xiaoyuan Yi, Xing Xie, Diyi Yang
First: 2026-03-03T13:35:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:35:33+00:00
Comments: 25 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM agents increasingly act on users' personal information, yet existing privacy defenses remain limited in both design and adaptability. Most prior approaches rely on static or passive defenses, such as prompting and guarding. These paradigms are insufficient for supporting contextual, proactive privacy decisions in multi-step agent execution. We propose Contextualized Defense Instructing (CDI), a new privacy defense paradigm in which an instructor model generates step-specific, context-aware privacy guidance during execution, proactively shaping actions rather than merely constraining or vetoing them. Crucially, CDI is paired with an experience-driven optimization framework that trains the instructor via reinforcement learning (RL), where we convert failure trajectories with privacy violations into learning environments. We formalize baseline defenses and CDI as distinct intervention points in a canonical agent loop, and compare their privacy-helpfulness trade-offs within a unified simulation framework. Results show that our CDI consistently achieves a better balance between privacy preservation (94.2%) and helpfulness (80.6%) than baselines, with superior robustness to adversarial conditions and generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大语言模型智能体的情境化隐私防御
大语言模型智能体日益频繁地处理用户个人信息，但现有隐私防御机制在设计和适应性方面均存在局限。多数现有方法依赖静态或被动的防御策略，如提示与防护机制。这些范式难以支持多步骤智能体执行过程中情境化、主动式的隐私决策。本文提出情境化防御指导（CDI）这一新型隐私防御范式：通过指导模型在执行过程中生成针对具体步骤、感知情境的隐私指引，主动塑造智能体行为而非仅进行约束或否决。关键创新在于，CDI配套构建了经验驱动的优化框架，通过强化学习训练指导模型——将包含隐私违规的失败轨迹转化为学习环境。我们在规范智能体循环中形式化定义了基线防御与CDI作为不同的干预节点，并在统一仿真框架内比较其隐私保护与助益性的权衡关系。实验表明，CDI在隐私保护率（94.2%）与助益性（80.6%）之间始终取得优于基线方法的平衡，且对对抗性条件与泛化场景表现出更强的鲁棒性。

The method employs a reinforcement learning framework to train the instructor by converting failure trajectories with privacy violations into learning environments, optimizing for both privacy and helpfulness. Experimental results in a unified simulation framework demonstrate that CDI achieves a superior balance, with 94.2% privacy preservation and 80.6% helpfulness, while showing robust generalization and adversarial resilience compared to baseline defenses.
针对大语言模型代理处理个人信息时静态隐私防御的不足，本文提出了情境化防御指导（CDI）范式，通过一个指导模型在代理执行过程中主动提供基于步骤和情境的隐私指导。该方法采用强化学习框架，将包含隐私违规的失败轨迹转化为学习环境来训练指导模型，以优化隐私保护和帮助性之间的平衡。在统一模拟框架中的实验结果表明，CDI实现了94.2%的隐私保护和80.6%的帮助性，优于基线方法，并展现出更强的对抗鲁棒性和泛化能力。
LAGO: A Local-Global Optimization Framework Combining Trust Region Methods and Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Eliott Van Dieren, Tommaso Vanzan, Fabio Nobile
First: 2026-03-03T13:24:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:24:36+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce LAGO, a LocAl-Global Optimization algorithm that combines gradient-enhanced Bayesian Optimization (BO) with gradient-based trust region local refinement through an adaptive competition mechanism. At each iteration, global and local optimization strategies independently propose candidate points, and the next evaluation is selected based on predicted improvement. LAGO separates global exploration from local refinement at the proposal level: the BO acquisition function is optimized outside the active trust region, while local function and gradient evaluations are incorporated into the global gradient-enhanced Gaussian process only when they satisfy a lengthscale-based minimum-distance criterion, reducing the risk of numerical instability during the local exploitation. This enables efficient local refinement when reaching promising regions, without sacrificing a global search of the design space. As a result, the method achieves an improved exploration of the full design space compared to standard non-linear local optimization algorithms for smooth functions, while maintaining fast local convergence in regions of interest.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LAGO：融合信赖域方法与贝叶斯优化的局部-全局优化框架
本文提出LAGO算法，一种通过自适应竞争机制将梯度增强贝叶斯优化与基于梯度的信赖域局部优化相结合的局部-全局优化方法。每次迭代中，全局与局部优化策略独立生成候选点，并根据预测改进值选择下一评估点。LAGO在提案层面分离全局探索与局部优化：贝叶斯采集函数在活跃信赖域外优化，而局部函数与梯度评估仅当满足基于长度尺度的最小距离准则时才纳入全局梯度增强高斯过程，从而降低局部开发时的数值不稳定风险。该方法在抵达潜力区域时可实现高效局部优化，同时不牺牲设计空间的全局搜索能力。相较于标准非线性局部优化算法，本方法在光滑函数上实现了更全面的设计空间探索，并在关注区域保持快速局部收敛。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LAGO, a hybrid optimization algorithm motivated by the need to efficiently combine global exploration with fast local convergence for smooth functions. The method integrates gradient-enhanced Bayesian Optimization for global search and gradient-based trust region methods for local refinement through an adaptive competition mechanism; it separates these strategies at the proposal level and carefully incorporates local evaluations into the global model to avoid numerical instability. Experimental results demonstrate that LAGO achieves improved global exploration compared to standard local optimization algorithms while maintaining rapid local convergence in promising regions.
本文提出了LAGO算法，其动机在于需要为平滑函数高效结合全局探索与快速局部收敛。该方法通过自适应竞争机制，将梯度增强的贝叶斯优化用于全局搜索，将基于梯度的信赖域方法用于局部优化；它在提议层面分离这两种策略，并谨慎地将局部评估纳入全局模型以避免数值不稳定。实验结果表明，与标准的局部优化算法相比，LAGO实现了更好的全局探索，同时在有潜力的区域保持了快速的局部收敛。
Near-Constant Strong Violation and Last-Iterate Convergence for Online CMDPs via Decaying Safety Margins
Authors: Qian Zuo, Zhiyong Wang, Fengxiang He
First: 2026-02-11T14:54:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:11:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study safe online reinforcement learning in Constrained Markov Decision Processes (CMDPs) under strong regret and violation metrics, which forbid error cancellation over time. Existing primal-dual methods that achieve sublinear strong reward regret inevitably incur growing strong constraint violation or are restricted to average-iterate convergence due to inherent oscillations. To address these limitations, we propose the Flexible safety Domain Optimization via Margin-regularized Exploration (FlexDOME) algorithm, the first to provably achieve near-constant $\tilde{O}(1)$ strong constraint violation alongside sublinear strong regret and non-asymptotic last-iterate convergence. FlexDOME incorporates time-varying safety margins and regularization terms into the primal-dual framework. Our theoretical analysis relies on a novel term-wise asymptotic dominance strategy, where the safety margin is rigorously scheduled to asymptotically majorize the functional decay rates of the optimization and statistical errors, thereby clamping cumulative violations to a near-constant level. Furthermore, we establish non-asymptotic last-iterate convergence guarantees via a policy-dual Lyapunov argument. Experiments corroborate our theoretical findings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于衰减安全裕度的在线约束马尔可夫决策过程：近恒定强违反与末次迭代收敛
本研究在强遗憾和强违反度量下探索约束马尔可夫决策过程中的安全在线强化学习，该度量禁止误差随时间抵消。现有实现次线性强奖励遗憾的原对偶方法，由于固有振荡性，必然导致增长的强约束违反或仅限于平均迭代收敛。为突破这些局限，我们提出基于裕度正则化探索的柔性安全域优化算法，该算法首次可证明地实现近恒定$\tilde{O}(1)$强约束违反，同时保持次线性强遗憾与非渐近末次迭代收敛。该算法将时变安全裕度与正则化项融入原对偶框架。理论分析依托新颖的逐项渐近主导策略：通过严格调度安全裕度使其渐近主导优化误差与统计误差的函数衰减速率，从而将累积违反控制在近恒定水平。此外，我们通过策略-对偶李雅普诺夫论证建立了非渐近末次迭代收敛保证。实验数据验证了理论结论。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of achieving both sublinear strong regret and near-constant strong constraint violation in safe online reinforcement learning for Constrained Markov Decision Processes (CMDPs), where existing primal-dual methods often suffer from growing violation or only guarantee average-iterate convergence. The proposed FlexDOME algorithm introduces time-varying safety margins and regularization within a primal-dual framework to provably attain near-constant strong violation, sublinear strong regret, and non-asymptotic last-iterate convergence. Experimental results support the theoretical analysis, demonstrating that FlexDOME effectively clamps cumulative violations while maintaining performance.
本文针对约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDPs）中的安全在线强化学习问题，旨在同时实现次线性强遗憾和接近恒定的强约束违反，而现有对偶原始方法通常存在违反增长或仅保证平均迭代收敛的局限。提出的FlexDOME算法在对偶原始框架中引入了时变安全裕度和正则化项，可证明地达到接近恒定的强违反、次线性强遗憾以及非渐近的最后迭代收敛。实验结果验证了理论分析，表明FlexDOME能有效控制累积违反同时保持性能。
CGL: Advancing Continual GUI Learning via Reinforcement Fine-Tuning
Authors: Zhenquan Yao, Zitong Huang, Yihan Zeng, Jianhua Han, Hang Xu, Chun-Mei Feng, Jianwei Ma, Wangmeng Zuo
First: 2026-03-03T13:02:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T13:02:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graphical User Interface (GUI) Agents, benefiting from recent advances in multimodal large language models (MLLM), have achieved significant development. However, due to the frequent updates of GUI applications, adapting to new tasks without forgetting old tasks in GUI continual learning remains an open problem. In this work, we reveal that while Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) facilitates fast adaptation, it often triggers knowledge overwriting, whereas Reinforcement Learning (RL) demonstrates an inherent resilience that shields prior interaction logic from erasure. Based on this insight, we propose a \textbf{C}ontinual \textbf{G}UI \textbf{L}earning (CGL) framework that dynamically balances adaptation efficiency and skill retention by enhancing the synergy between SFT and RL. Specifically, we introduce an SFT proportion adjustment mechanism guided by policy entropy to dynamically control the weight allocation between the SFT and RL training phases. To resolve explicit gradient interference, we further develop a specialized gradient surgery strategy. By projecting exploratory SFT gradients onto GRPO-based anchor gradients, our method explicitly clips the components of SFT gradients that conflict with GRPO. On top of that, we establish an AndroidControl-CL benchmark, which divides GUI applications into distinct task groups to effectively simulate and evaluate the performance of continual GUI learning. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of our proposed CGL framework across continual learning scenarios. The benchmark, code, and model will be made publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CGL：通过强化微调推进持续GUI学习
得益于多模态大语言模型（MLLM）的最新进展，图形用户界面（GUI）智能体取得了显著发展。然而，由于GUI应用频繁更新，如何在持续学习中适应新任务而不遗忘旧任务仍是一个开放性问题。本研究揭示：监督微调（SFT）虽能促进快速适应，但常引发知识覆盖；而强化学习（RL）则展现出内在韧性，能保护既有交互逻辑免遭擦除。基于此洞见，我们提出持续GUI学习（CGL）框架，通过增强SFT与RL的协同作用，动态平衡适应效率与技能保留。具体而言，我们引入基于策略熵的SFT比例调节机制，动态控制SFT与RL训练阶段的权重分配。为解决显式梯度干扰，进一步开发专用梯度手术策略：通过将探索性SFT梯度投影至基于GRPO的锚定梯度，显式裁剪与GRPO冲突的SFT梯度分量。此外，我们构建了AndroidControl-CL基准测试，将GUI应用划分为独立任务组以有效模拟和评估持续GUI学习性能。实验结果表明，所提CGL框架在持续学习场景中具有显著有效性。基准测试、代码与模型将公开提供。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of continual learning for GUI agents, where adapting to new application updates often leads to catastrophic forgetting of previously learned tasks. The authors propose the Continual GUI Learning (CGL) framework, which dynamically balances adaptation and retention by synergizing supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL), incorporating an entropy-guided SFT proportion adjustment mechanism and a gradient surgery strategy to mitigate interference. Experiments on the newly introduced AndroidControl-CL benchmark show that CGL effectively maintains performance across sequential tasks, outperforming methods that rely solely on SFT or RL.
本文针对图形用户界面（GUI）智能体在持续学习中的挑战，即适应新应用更新时容易遗忘旧任务的问题，提出了持续GUI学习（CGL）框架。该方法通过结合监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL），引入基于策略熵的SFT比例调整机制和梯度手术策略，以动态平衡适应效率与技能保留。在新构建的AndroidControl-CL基准测试上的实验结果表明，CGL框架在连续任务场景中有效提升了性能，优于仅使用SFT或RL的方法。
Beyond One-Size-Fits-All: Adaptive Subgraph Denoising for Zero-Shot Graph Learning with Large Language Models
Authors: Fengzhi Li, Liang Zhang, Yuan Zuo, Ruiqing Zhao, YanSong Liu, Yunfei Ma, Fanyu Meng, Junlan Feng
First: 2026-03-03T12:47:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:47:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graph-based tasks in the zero-shot setting remain a significant challenge due to data scarcity and the inability of traditional Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) to generalize to unseen domains or label spaces. While recent advancements have transitioned toward leveraging Large Language Models (LLMs) as predictors to enhance GNNs, these methods often suffer from cross-modal alignment issues. A recent paradigm (i.e., Graph-R1) overcomes the aforementioned architectural dependencies by adopting a purely text-based format and utilizing LLM-based graph reasoning, showing improved zero-shot generalization. However, it employs a task-agnostic, one-size-fits-all subgraph extraction strategy, which inevitably introduces significant structural noise--irrelevant neighbors and edges--that distorts the LLMs' receptive field and leads to suboptimal predictions. To address this limitation, we introduce GraphSSR, a novel framework designed for adaptive subgraph extraction and denoising in zero-shot LLM-based graph reasoning. Specifically, we propose the SSR pipeline, which dynamically tailors subgraph extraction to specific contexts through a "Sample-Select-Reason" process, enabling the model to autonomously filter out task-irrelevant neighbors and overcome the one-size-fits-all issue. To internalize this capability, we develop SSR-SFT, a data synthesis strategy that generates high-quality SSR-style graph reasoning traces for supervised fine-tuning of LLMs. Furthermore, we propose SSR-RL, a two-stage reinforcement learning framework that explicitly regulates sampling and selection operations within the proposed SSR pipeline designed for adaptive subgraph denoising. By incorporating Authenticity-Reinforced and Denoising-Reinforced RL, we guide the model to achieve accurate predictions using parsimonious, denoised subgraphs for reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越通用范式：面向大语言模型零样本图学习的自适应子图去噪
零样本场景下的图学习任务因数据稀缺及传统图神经网络（GNN）难以泛化至未见领域或标签空间而面临严峻挑战。尽管近期研究转向利用大语言模型（LLM）作为预测器增强GNN，这些方法常受跨模态对齐问题制约。新兴范式Graph-R1通过采用纯文本格式与基于LLM的图推理，突破了前述架构依赖并展现出更优的零样本泛化能力，但其采用的任务无关通用子图提取策略会引入显著结构噪声（无关邻接节点与边），扭曲LLM的感知域并导致次优预测。为此，我们提出GraphSSR框架，专为零样本LLM图推理设计自适应子图提取与去噪机制。具体而言，我们构建SSR流程，通过“采样-选择-推理”三阶段动态定制上下文相关子图，使模型能自主过滤任务无关邻接节点，突破通用化局限。为内化此能力，我们开发SSR-SFT数据合成策略，生成高质量SSR风格图推理轨迹用于LLM监督微调。进一步提出SSR-RL两阶段强化学习框架，在SSR流程中显式调控采样与选择操作以实现自适应子图去噪。通过融合真实性强化与去噪强化机制，引导模型使用精简去噪子图达成精准推理预测。

This paper addresses the challenge of zero-shot graph learning by tackling the structural noise introduced by task-agnostic subgraph extraction in LLM-based methods like Graph-R1. The proposed GraphSSR framework introduces an adaptive "Sample-Select-Reason" (SSR) pipeline to dynamically tailor and denoise subgraphs for specific contexts, filtering out irrelevant neighbors. To internalize this capability, the authors develop SSR-SFT for supervised fine-tuning using synthetic reasoning traces and SSR-RL, a reinforcement learning framework that explicitly regulates the sampling and selection for denoising. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach overcomes the one-size-fits-all limitation, enabling more accurate zero-shot predictions by reasoning with parsimonious, denoised subgraphs.
本文针对零样本图学习中的挑战，解决了如Graph-R1等基于大语言模型的方法因任务无关的子图提取而引入结构噪声的问题。提出的GraphSSR框架引入了一种自适应的“采样-选择-推理”流程，能根据具体上下文动态调整和去噪子图，过滤无关邻居节点。为了内化这种能力，作者开发了SSR-SFT，利用合成的推理轨迹进行监督微调，并提出了SSR-RL这一强化学习框架，显式调控去噪过程中的采样与选择操作。实验结果表明，该方法克服了通用策略的局限，通过使用精简、去噪后的子图进行推理，实现了更准确的零样本预测。
Contextual Latent World Models for Offline Meta Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Mohammadreza Nakheai, Aidan Scannell, Kevin Luck, Joni Pajarinen
First: 2026-03-03T12:45:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:45:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline meta-reinforcement learning seeks to learn policies that generalize across related tasks from fixed datasets. Context-based methods infer a task representation from transition histories, but learning effective task representations without supervision remains a challenge. In parallel, latent world models have demonstrated strong self-supervised representation learning through temporal consistency. We introduce contextual latent world models, which condition latent world models on inferred task representations and train them jointly with the context encoder. This enforces task-conditioned temporal consistency, yielding task representations that capture task-dependent dynamics rather than merely discriminating between tasks. Our method learns more expressive task representations and significantly improves generalization to unseen tasks across MuJoCo, Contextual-DeepMind Control, and Meta-World benchmarks.

On the Structural Limitations of Weight-Based Neural Adaptation and the Role of Reversible Behavioral Learning
Authors: Pardhu Sri Rushi Varma Konduru
First: 2026-03-03T12:44:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:44:12+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 5 figures. Preprint version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural models are usually adapted through changes in parameters shared among model components via fine-tuning, alignment-based training, and reinforcement learning. These changes have been found effective in short-term optimization. However, they result in long-term alterations in the model's base behavior. In this study, we introduce the concept of structural irreversibility as a characteristic of shared-parameter model adaptation. This concept refers to the intertwining of task-specific objectives with the representational identity of the model. We show that when parameters are directly mutated, the resulting model behaves divergently from the original model. This divergence cannot be reversed deterministically without an explicit parameter snapshot. We introduce reversible behavioral learning, in which model behaviors are structurally dissociated from identity parameters and can be deterministically unloaded through an explicit unload process. We also introduce the Recoverability Factor as a normalized measure of behavioral recoverability and provide additional diagnostics based on model divergence. Experiments show that reversible model adaptation achieves rollback within numerical precision, whereas shared-parameter mutation exhibits persistent post-reset divergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：论基于权重的神经适应的结构局限性及可逆行为学习的作用
神经模型通常通过微调、基于对齐的训练和强化学习等方式，改变模型组件间共享的参数来实现适应。这些改变在短期优化中被证明有效，但会导致模型基础行为的长期改变。本研究引入结构不可逆性作为共享参数模型适应的特征概念，指任务特定目标与模型表征身份的相互交织。研究表明，当参数直接突变时，所得模型的行为会偏离原始模型，且若无明确的参数快照，这种偏离无法确定性逆转。我们提出可逆行为学习，将模型行为与身份参数在结构上解耦，可通过显式卸载过程确定性移除。同时引入可恢复性因子作为行为可恢复性的标准化度量，并提供基于模型偏离的额外诊断。实验表明，可逆模型适应能在数值精度内实现回滚，而共享参数突变则表现出重置后的持续偏离。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the structural limitations of conventional neural network adaptation methods like fine-tuning, which permanently alter a model's base behavior due to shared parameter updates, a phenomenon termed structural irreversibility. To address this, the authors propose reversible behavioral learning, a method that structurally dissociates learned behaviors from the model's core identity parameters, allowing behaviors to be deterministically unloaded. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach enables perfect behavioral rollback within numerical precision, unlike standard weight-based adaptation which shows persistent divergence even after parameter reset, as quantified by their introduced Recoverability Factor and divergence diagnostics.
本文研究了传统神经网络适应方法（如微调）的结构性局限，这些方法由于共享参数的更新会永久改变模型的基础行为，这种现象被称为结构不可逆性。为解决此问题，作者提出了可逆行为学习方法，该方法将学习到的行为与模型核心身份参数在结构上解耦，从而允许行为被确定性地卸载。实验结果表明，该方法能在数值精度内实现完美的行为回滚，而标准的基于权重的适应方法即使在参数重置后仍表现出持续的差异，这通过其引入的可恢复性因子和差异诊断指标得到了量化验证。
Learning to Evolve for Optimization via Stability-Inducing Neural Unrolling
Authors: Jiaxin Gao, Yaohua Liu, Ran Cheng, Kay Chen Tan
First: 2025-12-12T10:46:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:41:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Evolutionary algorithms serve as a powerful paradigm for tackling optimization challenges, yet their reliance on manually engineered heuristics inherently limits their adaptability across diverse landscapes. However, the transition from the hand-crafted heuristics to data-driven algorithms faces a fundamental dilemma: achieving neural \emph{plasticity} without sacrificing algorithmic stability. Although learned optimizers offer high adaptivity, their unconstrained update rules often result in unstable dynamics and brittle generalization on unseen landscapes. To address this challenge, this paper proposes Learning to Evolve (L2E), a bilevel meta-optimization framework that learns evolutionary search via stability-inducing neural unrolling. First, L2E reformulates population evolution as an unrolled fixed-point iteration via a structured neural operator. In this design, the inner loop imposes a stability-biased update structure, while the outer loop meta-trains the operator to produce effective search trajectories across tasks. Second, to balance global exploration with local refinement, a gradient-derived composite solver adaptively fuses learned evolutionary proposals with proxy numerical guidance in a differentiable manner. Extensive experiments on synthetic benchmarks and real-world control tasks demonstrate that L2E achieves substantial optimization performance, scales to high-dimensional problems, and exhibits robust zero-shot transfer across diverse test distributions.

标题：通过稳定性诱导神经展开实现优化中的学习进化
进化算法作为解决优化挑战的强大范式，其依赖人工设计启发式规则的本质限制了在不同问题场景中的适应性。然而，从手工启发式转向数据驱动算法面临一个根本困境：如何在保持算法稳定性的同时实现神经可塑性。尽管学习型优化器具有高适应性，但其无约束的更新规则常导致动态不稳定及在未见场景下的泛化脆弱性。为此，本文提出学习进化（L2E）——一种通过稳定性诱导神经展开实现进化搜索学习的双层元优化框架。首先，L2E通过结构化神经算子将种群演化重构为展开式定点迭代，其内层循环采用偏重稳定性的更新结构，外层循环则通过元训练使算子能跨任务生成有效搜索轨迹。其次，为平衡全局探索与局部优化，引入基于梯度的复合求解器，以可微分方式自适应融合学习到的进化方案与代理数值指导。在合成基准测试和实际控制任务上的大量实验表明，L2E能实现显著的优化性能，可扩展至高维问题，并在多样化的测试分布中展现出强大的零样本迁移能力。

The method reformulates population evolution as an unrolled fixed-point iteration with a structured neural operator, where an inner loop enforces stability-biased updates and an outer loop meta-trains the operator for effective search across tasks, while a gradient-derived composite solver adaptively fuses learned proposals with numerical guidance to balance exploration and refinement. Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference with Conditional Lagrangian Optimal Transport
Authors: Harry Amad, Mihaela van der Schaar
First: 2026-03-02T11:55:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:35:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural networks (NNs) often have critical behavioural trade-offs that are set at design time with hyperparameters-such as reward weights in reinforcement learning or quantile targets in regression. Post-deployment, however, user preferences can evolve, making initial settings undesirable, necessitating potentially expensive retraining. To circumvent this, we introduce the task of Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference (HTI): to learn, from observed data, how a NN's conditional output distribution changes with its hyperparameters, and construct a surrogate model that approximates the NN at unobserved hyperparameter settings. HTI requires extending existing trajectory inference approaches to incorporate conditions, exacerbating the challenge of ensuring inferred paths are feasible. We propose an approach based on conditional Lagrangian optimal transport, jointly learning the Lagrangian function governing hyperparameter-induced dynamics along with the associated optimal transport maps and geodesics between observed marginals, which form the surrogate model. We incorporate inductive biases based on the manifold hypothesis and least-action principles into the learned Lagrangian, improving surrogate model feasibility. We empirically demonstrate that our approach reconstructs NN outputs across various hyperparameter spectra better than other alternatives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于条件拉格朗日最优传输的超参数轨迹推断
神经网络（NNs）常在设计时通过超参数（如强化学习中的奖励权重或回归中的分位数目标）设定关键行为权衡。然而，部署后用户偏好可能变化，导致初始设置不再适用，需进行可能昂贵的重新训练。为规避此问题，我们提出超参数轨迹推断（HTI）任务：从观测数据中学习NN的条件输出分布如何随超参数变化，并构建一个在未观测超参数设置下近似NN的代理模型。HTI需扩展现有轨迹推断方法以纳入条件，这加剧了确保推断路径可行的挑战。我们提出一种基于条件拉格朗日最优传输的方法，联合学习控制超参数诱导动态的拉格朗日函数，以及观测边缘分布间的最优传输映射和测地线（构成代理模型）。我们将基于流形假设和最小作用原理的归纳偏置融入学习的拉格朗日函数中，提升代理模型可行性。实验表明，我们的方法在多种超参数谱上重建NN输出的效果优于其他方案。

Enhancing Generative Auto-bidding with Offline Reward Evaluation and Policy Search
Authors: Zhiyu Mou, Yiqin Lv, Miao Xu, Qi Wang, Yixiu Mao, Jinghao Chen, Qichen Ye, Chao Li, Rongquan Bai, Chuan Yu, Jian Xu, Bo Zheng
First: 2025-09-19T12:30:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:29:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Auto-bidding is a critical tool for advertisers to improve advertising performance. Recent progress has demonstrated that AI-Generated Bidding (AIGB), which learns a conditional generative planner from offline data, achieves superior performance compared to typical offline reinforcement learning (RL)-based auto-bidding methods. However, existing AIGB methods still face a performance bottleneck due to their inherent inability to explore beyond the static dataset with feedback. To address this, we propose \textbf{AIGB-Pearl} (\emph{\textbf{P}lanning with \textbf{E}valu\textbf{A}tor via \textbf{RL}}), a novel method that integrates generative planning and policy optimization. The core of AIGB-Pearl lies in constructing a trajectory evaluator to assess the quality of generated scores and designing a provably sound KL-Lipschitz-constrained score-maximization scheme to ensure safe and efficient exploration beyond the offline dataset. A practical algorithm that incorporates the synchronous coupling technique is further developed to ensure the model regularity required by the proposed scheme. Extensive experiments on both simulated and real-world advertising systems demonstrate the state-of-the-art performance of our approach.

Experimental results on simulated and real-world advertising systems show that AIGB-Pearl achieves state-of-the-art performance.
本文针对基于离线数据的AI生成竞价方法存在的性能瓶颈，即无法在静态数据集之外进行探索，提出了一种新方法AIGB-Pearl。该方法通过构建轨迹评估器来评估生成分数的质量，并设计了一种可证明安全的KL-Lipschitz约束分数最大化方案，以实现安全高效的探索。在模拟和真实广告系统上的大量实验表明，该方法取得了最先进的性能。
SAE as a Crystal Ball: Interpretable Features Predict Cross-domain Transferability of LLMs without Training
Authors: Qi Zhang, Yifei Wang, Xiaohan Wang, Jiajun Chai, Guojun Yin, Wei Lin, Yisen Wang
First: 2026-03-03T12:01:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T12:01:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In recent years, pre-trained large language models have achieved remarkable success across diverse tasks. Besides the pivotal role of self-supervised pre-training, their effectiveness in downstream applications also depends critically on the post-training process, which adapts models to task-specific data and objectives. However, this process inevitably introduces model shifts that can influence performance in different domains, and how such shifts transfer remains poorly understood. To open up the black box, we propose the SAE-based Transferability Score (STS), a new metric that leverages sparse autoencoders (SAEs) to forecast post-training transferability. Taking supervised fine-tuning as an example, STS identifies shifted dimensions in SAE representations and calculates their correlations with downstream domains, enabling reliable estimation of transferability \textit{before} fine-tuning. Extensive experiments across multiple models and domains show that STS accurately predicts the transferability of supervised fine-tuning, achieving Pearson correlation coefficients above 0.7 with actual performance changes. Beyond this, we take an initial step toward extending STS to reinforcement learning. We believe that STS can serve as an {\color{black} interpretable} tool for guiding post-training strategies in LLMs. Code is available at https://github.com/PKU-ML/STS.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SAE作为水晶球：无需训练即可通过可解释特征预测大语言模型的跨领域可迁移性
近年来，预训练大语言模型在多样化任务中取得了显著成功。除了自监督预训练的关键作用外，其在下游应用中的有效性还高度依赖于后训练过程，该过程使模型适应特定任务的数据和目标。然而，这一过程不可避免地引入模型偏移，可能影响不同领域的性能，而此类偏移如何迁移仍鲜为人知。为揭示黑箱机制，我们提出基于稀疏自编码器的可迁移性评分（STS），这是一种利用稀疏自编码器预测后训练可迁移性的新指标。以监督微调为例，STS识别SAE表示中的偏移维度，并计算其与下游领域的相关性，从而在微调前即可可靠估计可迁移性。跨多个模型和领域的广泛实验表明，STS能准确预测监督微调的可迁移性，与实际性能变化的皮尔逊相关系数超过0.7。此外，我们初步探索将STS扩展至强化学习。我们相信STS可作为一种可解释工具，用于指导大语言模型的后训练策略。代码发布于https://github.com/PKU-ML/STS。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand how post-training adaptations like fine-tuning affect large language models' performance across different domains, this paper introduces the SAE-based Transferability Score (STS). The method uses sparse autoencoders to extract interpretable features from model representations, identifying dimensions that shift during fine-tuning and correlating them with target domains to predict transferability prior to actual training. Experimental results across multiple models and domains demonstrate that STS reliably forecasts fine-tuning outcomes, achieving Pearson correlations above 0.7 with performance changes, and shows initial promise for extension to reinforcement learning settings.

VideoTemp-o3: Harmonizing Temporal Grounding and Video Understanding in Agentic Thinking-with-Videos
Authors: Wenqi Liu, Yunxiao Wang, Shijie Ma, Meng Liu, Qile Su, Tianke Zhang, Haonan Fan, Changyi Liu, Kaiyu Jiang, Jiankang Chen, Kaiyu Tang, Bin Wen, Fan Yang, Tingting Gao, Han Li, Yinwei Wei, Xuemeng Song
First: 2026-02-08T03:45:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T11:46:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In long-video understanding, conventional uniform frame sampling often fails to capture key visual evidence, leading to degraded performance and increased hallucinations. To address this, recent agentic thinking-with-videos paradigms have emerged, adopting a localize-clip-answer pipeline in which the model actively identifies relevant video segments, performs dense sampling within those clips, and then produces answers. However, existing methods remain inefficient, suffer from weak localization, and adhere to rigid workflows. To solve these issues, we propose VideoTemp-o3, a unified agentic thinking-with-videos framework that jointly models video grounding and question answering. VideoTemp-o3 exhibits strong localization capability, supports on-demand clipping, and can refine inaccurate localizations. Specifically, in the supervised fine-tuning stage, we design a unified masking mechanism that encourages exploration while preventing noise. For reinforcement learning, we introduce dedicated rewards to mitigate reward hacking. Besides, from the data perspective, we develop an effective pipeline to construct high-quality long video grounded QA data, along with a corresponding benchmark for systematic evaluation across various video durations. Experimental results demonstrate that our method achieves remarkable performance on both long video understanding and grounding.

标题：VideoTemp-o3：在视频代理思维中协调时序定位与视频理解
在长视频理解任务中，传统的均匀帧采样方法常因未能捕捉关键视觉证据而导致性能下降与幻觉增强。为应对此问题，近期兴起的视频代理思维范式采用“定位-剪辑-回答”流程，使模型能主动识别相关视频片段、进行密集采样后生成答案。然而现有方法仍存在效率低下、定位能力薄弱、流程僵化等局限。为此，我们提出VideoTemp-o3——一个统一视频代理思维框架，可联合建模视频定位与问答任务。该框架具备强定位能力，支持按需剪辑，并能修正不准确的定位结果。具体而言，在监督微调阶段，我们设计了统一掩码机制以平衡探索与噪声抑制；在强化学习阶段，引入专项奖励机制以缓解奖励攻击问题。此外，我们从数据层面构建了高质量长视频定位问答数据生成流程，并建立对应基准以系统评估不同时长视频任务。实验结果表明，该方法在长视频理解与定位任务上均取得显著性能提升。

Reducing Belief Deviation in Reinforcement Learning for Active Reasoning
Authors: Deyu Zou, Yongqiang Chen, Jianxiang Wang, Haochen Yang, Mufei Li, James Cheng, Pan Li, Yu Gong
Venue: ICLR 2026 Oral
First: 2025-10-14T08:14:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T11:42:46+00:00
Comments: Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026 (Oral)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Active reasoning requires large language model (LLM) agents to interact with external sources and strategically gather information to solve problems in multiple turns. Central to this process is belief tracking: maintaining an accurate representation of the underlying state and uncertainty in understanding and solving the problem. However, due to limited reasoning capabilities, LLM-based agents often suffer belief deviation: their internal beliefs drift from the true problem state, leading to loss of state awareness and uninformative or repetitive actions. Once this happens, errors compound in the trajectories used for reinforcement learning (RL), leading to misattributed credits and limited exploration. To address this issue, we propose to track belief deviation and develop $\mathbf{T^3}$, a simple yet principled method that detects excessive deviation and truncates training trajectories to suppress uninformative tail effects. Hence, $\mathbf{T^3}$ preserves credits for informative prefixes and systematically improves policy optimization. Across 5 challenging tasks, $\mathbf{T^3}$ consistently enhances training stability and yields performance gains of up to 30 points while cutting token cost by up to 34%. These results highlight belief control as a key principle for building robust LLM agents capable of active reasoning.

标题：强化学习中减少信念偏差以促进主动推理
主动推理要求大语言模型（LLM）智能体与外部源交互，并通过多轮策略性信息收集来解决问题。该过程的核心是信念追踪：保持对潜在状态及问题理解与求解过程中不确定性的准确表征。然而，由于推理能力有限，基于LLM的智能体常出现信念偏差：其内部信念偏离真实问题状态，导致状态感知丧失及产生无信息量或重复性行动。一旦发生这种情况，用于强化学习（RL）的轨迹中误差会不断累积，造成信用分配错误和探索受限。为解决此问题，我们提出追踪信念偏差并开发了$\mathbf{T^3}$方法——一种简洁而原则性的方法，可检测过度偏差并截断训练轨迹以抑制无信息量的尾部效应。因此，$\mathbf{T^3}$能保留信息量丰富的前缀段信用，系统性地改进策略优化。在5项挑战性任务中，$\mathbf{T^3}$持续提升训练稳定性，实现最高30个百分点的性能增益，同时降低最高34%的令牌消耗。这些结果表明信念控制是构建具备主动推理能力的鲁棒LLM智能体的关键原则。

This paper addresses the issue of belief deviation in large language model (LLM) agents performing multi-turn active reasoning, where internal beliefs drift from the true problem state, causing uninformative actions and compounding errors in reinforcement learning (RL) training. Learning Memory-Enhanced Improvement Heuristics for Flexible Job Shop Scheduling
Authors: Jiaqi Wang, Zhiguang Cao, Peng Zhao, Rui Cao, Yubin Xiao, Yuan Jiang, You Zhou
Venue: NeurIPS 2025
First: 2026-03-03T10:43:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T10:43:01+00:00
Comments: 39th Conference on Neural Information Processing Systems (NeurIPS 2025)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rise of smart manufacturing under Industry 4.0 introduces mass customization and dynamic production, demanding more advanced and flexible scheduling techniques. The flexible job-shop scheduling problem (FJSP) has attracted significant attention due to its complex constraints and strong alignment with real-world production scenarios. Current deep reinforcement learning (DRL)-based approaches to FJSP predominantly employ constructive methods. While effective, they often fall short of reaching (near-)optimal solutions. In contrast, improvement-based methods iteratively explore the neighborhood of initial solutions and are more effective in approaching optimality. However, the flexible machine allocation in FJSP poses significant challenges to the application of this framework, including accurate state representation, effective policy learning, and efficient search strategies. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a Memory-enhanced Improvement Search framework with heterogeneous graph representation--MIStar. It employs a novel heterogeneous disjunctive graph that explicitly models the operation sequences on machines to accurately represent scheduling solutions. Moreover, a memoryenhanced heterogeneous graph neural network (MHGNN) is designed for feature extraction, leveraging historical trajectories to enhance the decision-making capability of the policy network. Finally, a parallel greedy search strategy is adopted to explore the solution space, enabling superior solutions with fewer iterations. Extensive experiments on synthetic data and public benchmarks demonstrate that MIStar significantly outperforms both traditional handcrafted improvement heuristics and state-of-the-art DRL-based constructive methods.

标题：面向柔性作业车间调度的记忆增强改进启发式方法学习
工业4.0下智能制造的兴起带来了大规模定制与动态生产，对更先进、灵活的调度技术提出了需求。柔性作业车间调度问题（FJSP）因其复杂约束和与现实生产场景的高度契合而备受关注。当前基于深度强化学习（DRL）的FJSP方法主要采用构造式方法，虽有效但常难以达到（近似）最优解。相比之下，基于改进的方法通过迭代探索初始解的邻域，能更有效地逼近最优解。然而，FJSP中的柔性机器分配为该框架的应用带来了重大挑战，包括精确的状态表示、有效的策略学习和高效搜索策略。为应对这些挑战，本文提出了一种基于异构图表示的记忆增强改进搜索框架——MIStar。该框架采用新型异构图显式建模机器上的工序序列，以准确表示调度解；设计记忆增强异构图神经网络（MHGNN）进行特征提取，利用历史轨迹增强策略网络的决策能力；并采用并行贪婪搜索策略探索解空间，以更少迭代获得更优解。在合成数据和公开基准上的大量实验表明，MIStar显著优于传统手工改进启发式方法和最先进的基于DRL的构造式方法。

Experimental results on synthetic data and public benchmarks show that MIStar significantly outperforms traditional handcrafted heuristics and state-of-the-art DRL-based constructive methods, achieving superior solutions with fewer iterations.
