A Novel Evolutionary Method for Automated Skull-Face Overlay in Computer-Aided Craniofacial Superimposition
Authors: Práxedes Martínez-Moreno, Andrea Valsecchi, Pablo Mesejo, Pilar Navarro-Ramírez, Valentino Lugli, Sergio Damas
First: 2026-02-26T13:55:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T10:38:27+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 6 figures, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Craniofacial Superimposition is a forensic technique for identifying skeletal remains by comparing a post-mortem skull with ante-mortem facial photographs. A critical step in this process is Skull-Face Overlay (SFO). This stage involves aligning a 3D skull model with a 2D facial image, typically guided by cranial and facial landmarks' correspondence. However, its accuracy is undermined by individual variability in soft-tissue thickness, introducing significant uncertainty into the overlay. This paper introduces Lilium, an automated evolutionary method to enhance the accuracy and robustness of SFO. Lilium explicitly models soft-tissue variability using a 3D cone-based representation whose parameters are optimized via a Differential Evolution algorithm. The method enforces anatomical, morphological, and photographic plausibility through a combination of constraints: landmark matching, camera parameter consistency, head pose alignment, skull containment within facial boundaries, and region parallelism. This emulation of the usual forensic practitioners' approach leads Lilium to outperform the state-of-the-art method in terms of both accuracy and robustness.

Benefits and Pitfalls of Reinforcement Learning for Language Model Planning: A Theoretical Perspective
Authors: Siwei Wang, Yifei Shen, Haoran Sun, Shi Feng, Shang-Hua Teng, Li Dong, Yaru Hao, Wei Chen
First: 2025-09-26T17:39:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T09:39:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent reinforcement learning (RL) methods have substantially enhanced the planning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), yet the theoretical basis for their effectiveness remains elusive. In this work, we investigate RL's benefits and limitations through a tractable graph-based abstraction, focusing on policy gradient (PG) and Q-learning methods. Our theoretical analyses reveal that supervised fine-tuning (SFT) may introduce co-occurrence-based spurious solutions, whereas RL achieves correct planning primarily through exploration, underscoring exploration's role in enabling better generalization. However, we also show that PG suffers from diversity collapse, where output diversity decreases during training and persists even after perfect accuracy is attained. By contrast, Q-learning provides two key advantages: off-policy learning and diversity preservation at convergence. We further demonstrate that careful reward design is necessary to prevent Q-value bias in Q-learning. Finally, applying our framework to the real-world planning benchmark Blocksworld, we confirm that these behaviors manifest in practice.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习在语言模型规划中的优势与陷阱：理论视角
近期强化学习方法显著提升了大型语言模型的规划能力，但其有效性的理论基础仍不明确。本研究通过可处理的图抽象框架，聚焦策略梯度和Q学习方法，探讨了强化学习的优势与局限。理论分析表明，监督微调可能引入基于共现的伪解，而强化学习主要通过探索实现正确规划，凸显了探索对提升泛化能力的作用。然而，策略梯度存在多样性坍缩问题，即训练中输出多样性下降且在达到完全准确后仍持续减少。相比之下，Q学习具有离策略学习和收敛时保持多样性两大优势。研究进一步证明，需精心设计奖励函数以避免Q学习中的Q值偏差。最后，在真实规划基准测试Blocksworld中应用本框架，验证了这些理论发现在实践中的体现。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the unclear theoretical foundations for reinforcement learning's success in enhancing language model planning, this paper analyzes RL's benefits and limitations using a graph-based abstraction, focusing on policy gradient and Q-learning. The method involves theoretical analysis revealing that supervised fine-tuning can lead to spurious co-occurrence solutions, while RL achieves correct planning through exploration, which aids generalization; however, policy gradient suffers from diversity collapse where output diversity diminishes even after perfect accuracy. In contrast, Q-learning offers advantages in off-policy learning and diversity preservation at convergence, though it requires careful reward design to avoid Q-value bias. Experimental results on the Blocksworld benchmark confirm these theoretical behaviors in practice.
本文的动机在于强化学习在提升大语言模型规划能力方面缺乏明确的理论基础，因此通过基于图的抽象模型来分析强化学习的优势与局限，重点关注策略梯度和Q学习方法。研究方法包括理论分析，揭示监督微调可能引入基于共现的伪解，而强化学习主要通过探索实现正确规划，这有助于泛化；但策略梯度存在多样性崩溃问题，即输出多样性在训练中减少并在达到完美精度后持续。相比之下，Q学习具有离策略学习和收敛时保持多样性的优势，但需要精心设计奖励以避免Q值偏差。在Blocksworld基准上的实验结果证实了这些理论行为在实际中的表现。
Dynamic Deep-Reinforcement-Learning Algorithm in Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes
Authors: Saki Omi, Hyo-Sang Shin, Namhoon Cho, Antonios Tsourdos
First: 2023-07-29T08:52:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T09:28:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent studies have greatly improved reinforcement learning, and an increased interest in real-world implementation has emerged. In many cases, the implementation is challenged by time-varying disturbances as it introduces hidden states, which makes the problem best described with Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes. An effective approach to address this problem is to introduce a Recurrent Neural Network (RNN) in place of a state estimator. However, only a few studies have investigated the types of information to be supplied to the RNN and the network architecture to handle them. This study discusses the effectiveness of the inclusion of action along with observation and the impact of network architecture to handle them by providing interpretations of how the trajectories are summarized at LSTM networks. Specifically, three novel approaches with different architectures are introduced. All algorithms demonstrated the effectiveness of the inclusion of the action trajectories in simulation environments. In particular, one of the developed algorithms, H-TD3, differs from the typical actor and critic network as the critic network is trained by utilizing the hidden states generated by the actor network as the summarized trajectory information. This novel approach exhibited the potential improvement of the computational time while maintaining the performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程中的动态深度强化学习算法
近期研究显著推进了强化学习的发展，实际应用需求日益增长。然而，时变干扰常引入隐状态，使问题更宜用部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程描述，这对算法实现构成挑战。一种有效解决方案是用循环神经网络替代状态估计器，但现有研究较少探讨输入循环神经网络的信息类型及对应网络架构。本研究通过分析长短期记忆网络对轨迹的归纳机制，探讨了在观测信息中加入动作的有效性及网络架构的影响，并提出三种新型架构算法。仿真实验表明，所有算法均验证了动作轨迹融合的有效性。其中H-TD3算法采用创新架构：其评价网络利用行动网络生成的隐状态作为轨迹摘要信息进行训练，与传统行动者-评论家网络结构不同。该方法在保持性能的同时，展现出减少计算时间的潜力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of applying reinforcement learning in real-world environments with time-varying disturbances, which create hidden states best modeled as Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs). The method explores the use of Recurrent Neural Networks (RNNs), specifically focusing on what information to feed them and the network architecture, proposing three novel approaches that incorporate action trajectories alongside observations and interpret how Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) networks summarize these trajectories. Experimental results in simulations confirm the effectiveness of including action information, with one algorithm, H-TD3, showing particular promise by using hidden states from the actor network to train the critic, thereby maintaining performance while potentially reducing computational time.
本文针对强化学习在具有时变扰动的现实环境中的应用挑战展开研究，这些扰动引入了隐藏状态，最适合用部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDPs）来描述。方法上探讨了使用循环神经网络（RNNs），特别是关注输入信息的类型和网络架构，提出了三种新颖方法，将动作轨迹与观测结合，并解释了长短期记忆（LSTM）网络如何总结这些轨迹。在模拟环境中的实验结果表明，包含动作信息是有效的，其中一种算法H-TD3通过利用行动者网络生成的隐藏状态来训练评论者网络，显示出在保持性能的同时有潜力减少计算时间。
From Heuristic Selection to Automated Algorithm Design: LLMs Benefit from Strong Priors
Authors: Qi Huang, Furong Ye, Ananta Shahane, Thomas Bäck, Niki van Stein
First: 2026-03-03T09:27:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T09:27:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have already been widely adopted for automated algorithm design, demonstrating strong abilities in generating and evolving algorithms across various fields. Existing work has largely focused on examining their effectiveness in solving specific problems, with search strategies primarily guided by adaptive prompt designs. In this paper, through investigating the token-wise attribution of the prompts to LLM-generated algorithmic codes, we show that providing high-quality algorithmic code examples can substantially improve the performance of the LLM-driven optimization. Building upon this insight, we propose leveraging prior benchmark algorithms to guide LLM-driven optimization and demonstrate superior performance on two black-box optimization benchmarks: the pseudo-Boolean optimization suite (pbo) and the black-box optimization suite (bbob). Our findings highlight the value of integrating benchmarking studies to enhance both efficiency and robustness of the LLM-driven black-box optimization methods.

标题：从启发式选择到自动化算法设计：大语言模型受益于强先验知识

This paper is motivated by the need to improve the automated algorithm design capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), which have shown promise but often rely on adaptive prompt designs without leveraging strong algorithmic priors. Next Embedding Prediction Makes World Models Stronger
Authors: George Bredis, Nikita Balagansky, Daniil Gavrilov, Ruslan Rakhimov
First: 2026-03-03T09:04:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T09:04:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Capturing temporal dependencies is critical for model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) in partially observable, high-dimensional domains. We introduce NE-Dreamer, a decoder-free MBRL agent that leverages a temporal transformer to predict next-step encoder embeddings from latent state sequences, directly optimizing temporal predictive alignment in representation space. This approach enables NE-Dreamer to learn coherent, predictive state representations without reconstruction losses or auxiliary supervision. On the DeepMind Control Suite, NE-Dreamer matches or exceeds the performance of DreamerV3 and leading decoder-free agents. On a challenging subset of DMLab tasks involving memory and spatial reasoning, NE-Dreamer achieves substantial gains. These results establish next-embedding prediction with temporal transformers as an effective, scalable framework for MBRL in complex, partially observable environments.

标题：下一嵌入预测增强世界模型能力

Summary / 总结

Multi-Agent-Based Simulation of Archaeological Mobility in Uneven Landscapes
Authors: Chairi Kiourt, Vassilis Evangelidis, Dimitris Grigoropoulos
First: 2026-03-03T09:02:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T09:02:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Understanding mobility, movement, and interaction in archaeological landscapes is essential for interpreting past human behavior, transport strategies, and spatial organization, yet such processes are difficult to reconstruct from static archaeological evidence alone. This paper presents a multi-agent-based modeling framework for simulating archaeological mobility in uneven landscapes, integrating realistic terrain reconstruction, heterogeneous agent modeling, and adaptive navigation strategies. The proposed approach combines global path planning with local dynamic adaptation, through reinforcment learning, enabling agents to respond efficiently to dynamic obstacles and interactions without costly global replanning. Real-world digital elevation data are processed into high-fidelity three-dimensional environments, preserving slope and terrain constraints that directly influence agent movement. The framework explicitly models diverse agent types, including human groups and animal-based transport systems, each parameterized by empirically grounded mobility characteristics such as load, slope tolerance, and physical dimensions. Two archaeological-inspired use cases demonstrate the applicability of the approach: a terrain-aware pursuit and evasion scenario and a comparative transport analysis involving pack animals and wheeled carts. The results highlight the impact of terrain morphology, visibility, and agent heterogeneity on movement outcomes, while the proposed hybrid navigation strategy provides a computationally efficient and interpretable solution for large-scale, dynamic archaeological simulations.

Deep learning-guided evolutionary optimization for protein design
Authors: Erik Hartman, Di Tang, Johan Malmström
First: 2026-03-03T08:53:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T08:53:12+00:00
Comments: Code available at GitHub
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Designing novel proteins with desired characteristics remains a significant challenge due to the large sequence space and the complexity of sequence-function relationships. Efficient exploration of this space to identify sequences that meet specific design criteria is crucial for advancing therapeutics and biotechnology. Here, we present BoGA (Bayesian Optimization Genetic Algorithm), a framework that combines evolutionary search with Bayesian optimization to efficiently navigate the sequence space. By integrating a genetic algorithm as a stochastic proposal generator within a surrogate modeling loop, BoGA prioritizes candidates based on prior evaluations and surrogate model predictions, enabling data-efficient optimization. We demonstrate the utility of BoGA through benchmarking on sequence and structure design tasks, followed by its application in designing peptide binders against pneumolysin, a key virulence factor of \textit{Streptococcus pneumoniae}. BoGA accelerates the discovery of high-confidence binders, demonstrating the potential for efficient protein design across diverse objectives. The algorithm is implemented within the BoPep suite and is available under an MIT license at \href{https://github.com/ErikHartman/bopep}{GitHub}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：深度学习引导的进化优化用于蛋白质设计

Enhancing User Throughput in Multi-panel mmWave Radio Access Networks for Beam-based MU-MIMO Using a DRL Method
Authors: Ramin Hashemi, Vismika Ranasinghe, Teemu Veijalainen, Petteri Kela, Risto Wichman
First: 2026-03-03T08:46:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T08:46:49+00:00
Comments: Accepted to the IEEE International Conference on Communications (ICC) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Millimeter-wave (mmWave) communication systems, particularly those leveraging multi-user multiple-input and multiple-output (MU-MIMO) with hybrid beamforming, face challenges in optimizing user throughput and minimizing latency due to the high complexity of dynamic beam selection and management. This paper introduces a deep reinforcement learning (DRL) approach for enhancing user throughput in multi-panel mmWave radio access networks in a practical network setup. Our DRL-based formulation utilizes an adaptive beam management strategy that models the interaction between the communication agent and its environment as a Markov decision process (MDP), optimizing beam selection based on real-time observations. The proposed framework exploits spatial domain (SD) characteristics by incorporating the cross-correlation between the beams in different antenna panels, the measured reference signal received power (RSRP), and the beam usage statistics to dynamically adjust beamforming decisions. As a result, the spectral efficiency is improved and end-to-end latency is reduced. The numerical results demonstrate an increase in throughput of up to 16% and a reduction in latency by factors 3-7x compared to baseline (legacy beam management).
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的多面板毫米波无线接入网络波束多用户MIMO用户吞吐量增强方法

The method formulates beam management as a Markov decision process, using an adaptive strategy that incorporates real-time observations like beam cross-correlation across antenna panels, reference signal received power, and usage statistics to optimize beam selection. Experimental results show the approach improves spectral efficiency, achieving up to a 16% increase in throughput and reducing end-to-end latency by 3 to 7 times compared to legacy baseline methods.

Rethinking Policy Diversity in Ensemble Policy Gradient in Large-Scale Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Naoki Shitanda, Motoki Omura, Tatsuya Harada, Takayuki Osa
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T11:06:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T08:32:08+00:00
Comments: In ICLR 2026. Website at https://naoki04.github.io/paper-cpo/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Scaling reinforcement learning to tens of thousands of parallel environments requires overcoming the limited exploration capacity of a single policy. Ensemble-based policy gradient methods, which employ multiple policies to collect diverse samples, have recently been proposed to promote exploration. However, merely broadening the exploration space does not always enhance learning capability, since excessive exploration can reduce exploration quality or compromise training stability. In this work, we theoretically analyze the impact of inter-policy diversity on learning efficiency in policy ensembles, and propose Coupled Policy Optimization which regulates diversity through KL constraints between policies. The proposed method enables effective exploration and outperforms strong baselines such as SAPG, PBT, and PPO across multiple tasks, including challenging dexterous manipulation, in terms of both sample efficiency and final performance. Furthermore, analysis of policy diversity and effective sample size during training reveals that follower policies naturally distribute around the leader, demonstrating the emergence of structured and efficient exploratory behavior. Our results indicate that diverse exploration under appropriate regulation is key to achieving stable and sample-efficient learning in ensemble policy gradient methods. Project page at https://naoki04.github.io/paper-cpo/ .
中文标题/摘要
标题：大规模强化学习中集成策略梯度方法策略多样性的再思考
将强化学习扩展到数万个并行环境需要克服单一策略探索能力有限的问题。近期提出的基于集成的策略梯度方法通过使用多个策略收集多样化样本以促进探索。然而，单纯扩大探索空间并不总能提升学习能力，因为过度探索可能降低探索质量或损害训练稳定性。本文从理论上分析了策略间多样性对集成策略学习效率的影响，并提出通过策略间KL约束调控多样性的耦合策略优化方法。该方法在多个任务（包括具有挑战性的灵巧操作任务）中实现了有效探索，并在样本效率和最终性能上超越了SAPG、PBT、PPO等强基线。训练过程中对策略多样性和有效样本量的分析表明，跟随策略会自然分布在主导策略周围，展现出结构化高效探索行为的涌现。研究结果表明，在适当调控下的多样化探索是实现集成策略梯度方法稳定且样本高效学习的关键。项目页面：https://naoki04.github.io/paper-cpo/
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limited exploration capacity of single policies in large-scale reinforcement learning by using policy ensembles, while recognizing that excessive diversity can harm learning efficiency and stability. The method, Coupled Policy Optimization, theoretically analyzes the impact of inter-policy diversity and regulates it by imposing KL constraints between policies to balance exploration and training coherence. Experimental results show that this approach outperforms strong baselines like SAPG, PBT, and PPO in tasks including dexterous manipulation, achieving higher sample efficiency and final performance, with analysis revealing that follower policies naturally cluster around a leader, leading to structured and effective exploration.
本研究的动机是通过策略集成解决大规模强化学习中单一策略探索能力有限的问题，同时认识到过度的多样性可能损害学习效率和稳定性。所提出的方法称为耦合策略优化，它从理论上分析了策略间多样性的影响，并通过在策略间施加KL约束来调节多样性，以平衡探索和训练一致性。实验结果表明，该方法在包括灵巧操作在内的多个任务中超越了SAPG、PBT和PPO等强基线，实现了更高的样本效率和最终性能，分析显示跟随策略会自然地围绕主导策略分布，从而形成结构化且高效的探索行为。
The Choice of Divergence: A Neglected Key to Mitigating Diversity Collapse in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward
Authors: Long Li, Zhijian Zhou, Jiaran Hao, Jason Klein Liu, Yanting Miao, Wei Pang, Xiaoyu Tan, Wei Chu, Zhe Wang, Shirui Pan, Chao Qu, Yuan Qi
First: 2025-09-09T06:34:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T07:36:26+00:00
Comments: 27 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A central paradox in fine-tuning Large Language Models (LLMs) with Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) is the frequent degradation of multi-attempt performance (Pass@k) despite improvements in single-attempt accuracy (Pass@1). This is often accompanied by catastrophic forgetting, where models lose previously acquired skills. While various methods have been proposed, the choice and function of the divergence term have been surprisingly unexamined as a proactive solution. We argue that standard RLVR objectives -- both those using the mode-seeking reverse KL-divergence and those forgoing a divergence term entirely -- lack a crucial mechanism for knowledge retention. The reverse-KL actively accelerates this decay by narrowing the policy, while its absence provides no safeguard against the model drifting from its diverse knowledge base. We propose a fundamental shift in perspective: using the divergence term itself as the solution. Our framework, Diversity-Preserving Hybrid RL (DPH-RL), leverages mass-covering f-divergences (like forward-KL and JS-divergence) to function as a rehearsal mechanism. By continuously referencing the initial policy, this approach forces the model to maintain broad solution coverage. Extensive experiments on math and SQL generation demonstrate that DPH-RL not only resolves the Pass@k degradation but improves both Pass@1 and Pass@k in- and out-of-domain. Additionally, DPH-RL is more training-efficient because it computes f-divergence using generator functions, requiring only sampling from the initial policy and no online reference model. Our work highlights a crucial, overlooked axis for improving RLVR, demonstrating that the proper selection of a divergence measure is a powerful tool for building more general and diverse reasoning models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：散度选择：强化学习可验证奖励中缓解多样性崩溃的被忽视关键
在使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）微调大型语言模型（LLMs）时，一个核心悖论是：尽管单次尝试准确率（Pass@1）有所提升，但多次尝试性能（Pass@k）却经常下降。这通常伴随着灾难性遗忘，即模型丧失先前习得的技能。虽然已有多种方法被提出，但散度项的选择与功能作为一种主动解决方案却惊人地未被审视。我们认为，标准的RLVR目标——无论是使用寻求模式的反向KL散度，还是完全舍弃散度项——都缺乏关键的知识保留机制。反向KL散度通过收窄策略主动加速了这种衰退，而舍弃散度项则无法防止模型偏离其多样化的知识基础。我们提出一个根本性的视角转变：将散度项本身作为解决方案。我们的框架——多样性保持混合强化学习（DPH-RL）——利用质量覆盖的f-散度（如正向KL散度和JS散度）作为复现机制。通过持续参考初始策略，该方法迫使模型保持广泛的解决方案覆盖范围。在数学和SQL生成任务上的大量实验表明，DPH-RL不仅解决了Pass@k性能下降问题，还提升了领域内外的Pass@1和Pass@k性能。此外，DPH-RL具有更高的训练效率，因为它使用生成函数计算f-散度，仅需从初始策略采样，无需在线参考模型。我们的工作凸显了改进RLVR的一个关键但被忽视的维度，证明正确选择散度度量是构建更通用、更多样化推理模型的强大工具。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the paradox in fine-tuning Large Language Models with Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR), where improvements in single-attempt accuracy (Pass@1) often lead to degraded multi-attempt performance (Pass@k) and catastrophic forgetting of diverse skills. The authors identify a neglected key: the choice of divergence term in the RL objective, arguing that standard approaches using reverse KL-divergence or no divergence accelerate knowledge decay or lack safeguards. They propose a framework called Diversity-Preserving Hybrid RL (DPH-RL), which uses mass-covering f-divergences like forward-KL as a rehearsal mechanism to reference the initial policy and preserve broad solution coverage. Experimental results on math and SQL generation tasks show that DPH-RL resolves Pass@k degradation, improves both Pass@1 and Pass@k in- and out-of-domain, and enhances training efficiency by computing divergence via generator functions without an online reference model.
本文针对使用可验证奖励的强化学习微调大语言模型中的一个悖论展开研究：单次尝试准确率提升常导致多次尝试性能下降及灾难性遗忘，使模型丧失已掌握的多样技能。作者指出一个被忽视的关键因素是强化学习目标中散度项的选择，认为标准方法使用的反向KL散度或无散度项会加速知识衰减或缺乏保护机制。为此，他们提出了多样性保持混合强化学习框架，采用前向KL等质量覆盖f-散度作为复习机制，通过持续参考初始策略来维持广泛的解覆盖。在数学和SQL生成任务上的实验表明，该框架解决了多次尝试性能退化问题，同时提升了单次和多次尝试的域内和域外性能，并且通过生成函数计算散度提高了训练效率，无需在线参考模型。
Shuffle-R1: Efficient RL framework for Multimodal Large Language Models via Data-centric Dynamic Shuffle
Authors: Linghao Zhu, Yiran Guan, Dingkang Liang, Jianzhong Ju, Zhenbo Luo, Bin Qin, Jian Luan, Yuliang Liu, Xiang Bai
Venue: ICLR 2026 poster
First: 2025-08-07T17:53:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T07:07:06+00:00
Comments: This paper has been accepted by ICLR 2026. Conference link: https://iclr.cc/virtual/2026/poster/10007559 OpenReview link: https://openreview.net/forum?id=mYP33u1QBK Project page at: https://xenozlh.github.io/Shuffle-R1/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as an effective post-training paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of multimodal large language model (MLLM). However, current RL pipelines often suffer from training inefficiencies caused by two underexplored issues: Advantage Collapsing, where most advantages in a batch concentrate near zero, and Rollout Silencing, where the proportion of rollouts contributing non-zero gradients diminishes over time. These issues lead to suboptimal gradient updates and hinder long-term learning efficiency. To address these issues, we propose Shuffle-R1, a simple yet principled framework that improves RL fine-tuning efficiency by dynamically restructuring trajectory sampling and batch composition. It introduces (1) Pairwise Trajectory Sampling, which selects high-contrast trajectories with large advantages to improve gradient signal quality, and (2) Advantage-based Trajectory Shuffle, which increases exposure of valuable rollouts through informed batch reshuffling. Experiments across multiple reasoning benchmarks show that our framework consistently outperforms strong RL baselines with minimal overhead. These results highlight the importance of data-centric adaptations for more efficient RL training in MLLM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Shuffle-R1：面向多模态大语言模型的数据中心化动态洗牌高效强化学习框架
强化学习已成为提升多模态大语言模型推理能力的有效后训练范式。然而，当前强化学习流程常受两个未充分探讨问题导致的训练低效困扰：优势坍缩（批次中多数优势值趋近于零）和轨迹沉寂（贡献非零梯度的轨迹比例随时间下降）。这些问题导致梯度更新次优并阻碍长期学习效率。为解决这些问题，我们提出Shuffle-R1——一个简洁而原理清晰的框架，通过动态重组轨迹采样与批次构成来提升强化学习微调效率。该框架引入：（1）配对轨迹采样：选取具有显著优势差异的高对比度轨迹以提升梯度信号质量；（2）基于优势的轨迹洗牌：通过智能批次重组增加高价值轨迹的曝光度。在多个推理基准上的实验表明，本框架能以极低开销持续超越主流强化学习基线方法。这些结果凸显了数据中心化适配对提升多模态大语言模型强化学习训练效率的重要性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses training inefficiencies in reinforcement learning (RL) for multimodal large language models (MLLMs), specifically the issues of Advantage Collapsing and Rollout Silencing, which lead to suboptimal gradient updates. The proposed method, Shuffle-R1, introduces a data-centric framework featuring Pairwise Trajectory Sampling to select high-contrast trajectories and Advantage-based Trajectory Shuffle to reshuffle batches for better exposure of valuable rollouts. Experimental results across multiple reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that Shuffle-R1 consistently outperforms strong RL baselines with minimal overhead, highlighting the effectiveness of data-centric adaptations for efficient RL training in MLLMs.
本文针对多模态大语言模型强化学习训练中的效率低下问题，特别是优势坍缩和轨迹静默这两个导致梯度更新次优的未充分探索问题。提出的方法Shuffle-R1是一个以数据为中心的框架，引入了成对轨迹采样以选择高对比度轨迹，以及基于优势的轨迹重排来通过智能批次重组增加有价值轨迹的曝光。在多个推理基准上的实验结果表明，Shuffle-R1以最小开销持续优于强大的强化学习基线，凸显了以数据为中心的调整对于多模态大语言模型高效强化学习训练的重要性。
Improving Diffusion Planners by Self-Supervised Action Gating with Energies
Authors: Yuan Lu, Dongqi Han, Yansen Wang, Dongsheng Li
First: 2026-03-03T06:36:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T06:36:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion planners are a strong approach for offline reinforcement learning, but they can fail when value-guided selection favours trajectories that score well yet are locally inconsistent with the environment dynamics, resulting in brittle execution. We propose Self-supervised Action Gating with Energies (SAGE), an inference-time re-ranking method that penalises dynamically inconsistent plans using a latent consistency signal. SAGE trains a Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) encoder on offline state sequences and an action-conditioned latent predictor for short horizon transitions. At test time, SAGE assigns each sampled candidate an energy given by its latent prediction error and combines this feasibility score with value estimates to select actions. SAGE can integrate into existing diffusion planning pipelines that can sample trajectories and select actions via value scoring; it requires no environment rollouts and no policy re-training. Across locomotion, navigation, and manipulation benchmarks, SAGE improves the performance and robustness of diffusion planners.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过基于能量的自监督动作门控改进扩散规划器
扩散规划器是离线强化学习的有效方法，但当基于价值的选择偏好那些评分高却与环境动态局部不一致的轨迹时，可能导致执行脆弱性。我们提出基于能量的自监督动作门控（SAGE），这是一种推理时重排序方法，通过潜在一致性信号惩罚动态不一致的计划。SAGE在离线状态序列上训练联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）编码器，并构建动作条件潜在预测器用于短时域状态转移。测试时，SAGE根据潜在预测误差为每个采样候选分配能量值，并将此可行性评分与价值估计结合以选择动作。SAGE可集成至现有扩散规划流程，无需环境交互或策略重训练。在运动、导航和操作基准测试中，SAGE显著提升了扩散规划器的性能与鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the brittleness of diffusion planners in offline reinforcement learning, where value-guided selection can favor high-scoring but dynamically inconsistent trajectories, leading to execution failures. The proposed method, Self-supervised Action Gating with Energies (SAGE), introduces an inference-time re-ranking approach that penalizes inconsistent plans using a latent consistency signal derived from a Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) trained on offline state sequences and short-horizon transitions. Experimental results across locomotion, navigation, and manipulation benchmarks demonstrate that SAGE enhances the performance and robustness of diffusion planners without requiring environment rollouts or policy retraining.
该论文针对离线强化学习中扩散规划器的脆弱性问题，即基于价值的选择可能偏好得分高但与动态环境不一致的轨迹，导致执行失败。提出的方法SAGE（基于能量的自监督动作门控）采用推理时重排序策略，通过从离线状态序列和短时程转移训练的联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）中提取潜在一致性信号，对不一致计划进行惩罚。在运动、导航和操作基准测试中，实验结果表明SAGE提升了扩散规划器的性能和鲁棒性，且无需环境交互或策略重新训练。
Policy Transfer for Continuous-Time Reinforcement Learning: A (Rough) Differential Equation Approach
Authors: Xin Guo, Zijiu Lyu
First: 2025-10-16T21:57:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T06:17:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper studies policy transfer, one of the well-known transfer learning techniques adopted in large language models, for continuous-time reinforcement learning problems. In the case of continuous-time linear-quadratic systems with Shannon's entropy regularization, we fully exploit the Gaussian structure of their optimal policy and the stability of their associated Riccati equations. In the general case where the system has possibly non-linear and bounded dynamics, the key technical component is the stability of diffusion SDEs which is established by invoking the rough path theory. Our work provides the first theoretical proof of policy transfer for continuous-time RL: an optimal policy learned for one RL problem can be used to initialize to search for a near-optimal policy for another closely related RL problem, while achieving (at least) the same rate of convergence for the original algorithm. As a byproduct of our analysis, we derive the stability of a concrete class of continuous-time score-based diffusion models via their connection with LQRs. To illustrate the benefit of policy transfer for RL, we propose a novel policy learning algorithm for continuous-time LQRs, which achieves global linear convergence and local super-linear convergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续时间强化学习的策略迁移：一种（粗糙）微分方程方法
本文针对连续时间强化学习问题，研究了策略迁移——一种在大语言模型中广泛采用的迁移学习技术。对于具有香农熵正则化的连续时间线性二次系统，我们充分利用其最优策略的高斯结构及其相关Riccati方程的稳定性。在系统可能具有非线性且有界动力学的一般情形下，关键技术在于通过调用粗糙路径理论建立的扩散随机微分方程的稳定性。我们的工作首次为连续时间强化学习的策略迁移提供了理论证明：针对一个强化学习问题习得的最优策略，可用于初始化搜索另一个密切相关问题的近似最优策略，同时（至少）保持原算法的收敛速率。作为分析的副产品，我们通过其与线性二次调节器的关联，推导了一类具体连续时间基于分数的扩散模型的稳定性。为说明策略迁移对强化学习的益处，我们提出了一种新颖的连续时间线性二次调节器策略学习算法，该算法实现了全局线性收敛与局部超线性收敛。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to theoretically justify policy transfer, a technique used in transfer learning, for continuous-time reinforcement learning (RL) problems. The method leverages the structural properties of specific systems: for linear-quadratic systems with entropy regularization, it exploits the Gaussian optimal policy and Riccati equation stability, while for general nonlinear bounded dynamics, it employs rough path theory to establish the stability of diffusion stochastic differential equations. The main experimental results provide the first theoretical proof that an optimal policy from one RL problem can effectively initialize the search for a near-optimal policy in a related problem, achieving at least the same convergence rate, and as a byproduct, the analysis yields stability guarantees for a class of continuous-time score-based diffusion models linked to linear-quadratic regulators.
本文的研究动机是为连续时间强化学习中的策略迁移技术提供理论依据，该技术是迁移学习的一种常用方法。所提出的方法针对特定系统结构：对于具有熵正则化的线性二次型系统，利用了其最优策略的高斯特性和Riccati方程的稳定性；而对于一般的非线性有界动态系统，则通过粗糙路径理论建立了扩散随机微分方程的稳定性。主要实验结果首次从理论上证明，从一个强化学习问题中学到的最优策略可以有效初始化对另一个密切相关问题的近最优策略搜索，并至少保持原算法的收敛速率，同时，该分析还通过其与线性二次型调节器的关联，推导出了一类连续时间基于分数的扩散模型的具体稳定性。
Quantization-Aware Distillation for NVFP4 Inference Accuracy Recovery
Authors: Meng Xin, Sweta Priyadarshi, Jingyu Xin, Bilal Kartal, Aditya Vavre, Asma Kuriparambil Thekkumpate, Zijia Chen, Ameya Sunil Mahabaleshwarkar, Ido Shahaf, Akhiad Bercovich, Kinjal Patel, Suguna Varshini Velury, Chenjie Luo, Zhiyu Cheng, Jenny Chen, Chen-Han Yu, Wei Ping, Oleg Rybakov, Nima Tajbakhsh, Oluwatobi Olabiyi, Dusan Stosic, Di Wu, Song Han, Eric Chung, Sharath Turuvekere Sreenivas, Bryan Catanzaro, Yoshi Suhara, Tijmen Blankevoort, Huizi Mao
First: 2026-01-27T22:14:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T06:03:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This technical report presents quantization-aware distillation (QAD) and our best practices for recovering accuracy of NVFP4-quantized large language models (LLMs) and vision-language models (VLMs). QAD distills a full-precision teacher model into a quantized student model using a KL divergence loss. While applying distillation to quantized models is not a new idea, we observe key advantages of QAD for today's LLMs: 1. It shows remarkable effectiveness and stability for models trained through multi-stage post-training pipelines, including supervised fine-tuning (SFT), reinforcement learning (RL), and model merging, where traditional quantization-aware training (QAT) suffers from engineering complexity and training instability; 2. It is robust to data quality and coverage, enabling accuracy recovery without full training data. We evaluate QAD across multiple post-trained models including AceReason Nemotron, Nemotron 3 Nano, Nemotron Nano V2, Nemotron Nano V2 VL (VLM), and Llama Nemotron Super v1, showing consistent recovery to near-BF16 accuracy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向NVFP4推理精度恢复的量化感知蒸馏方法
本技术报告提出量化感知蒸馏（QAD）方法及其最佳实践，用于恢复NVFP4量化大型语言模型（LLM）和视觉语言模型（VLM）的精度。QAD通过KL散度损失将全精度教师模型蒸馏至量化学生模型。尽管对量化模型应用蒸馏并非全新概念，但我们发现QAD对当前LLM具有关键优势：1. 对于通过监督微调（SFT）、强化学习（RL）和模型融合等多阶段后训练流程训练的模型，QAD表现出卓越的效能与稳定性，而传统量化感知训练（QAT）存在工程复杂性和训练不稳定的问题；2. 该方法对数据质量与覆盖范围具有鲁棒性，无需完整训练数据即可实现精度恢复。我们在包括AceReason Nemotron、Nemotron 3 Nano、Nemotron Nano V2、Nemotron Nano V2 VL（VLM）及Llama Nemotron Super v1在内的多个后训练模型上评估QAD，均能稳定恢复至接近BF16精度水平。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces quantization-aware distillation (QAD) as a method to recover the inference accuracy of large language and vision-language models quantized to NVFP4 precision, addressing the engineering complexity and instability of traditional quantization-aware training (QAT) in multi-stage post-training pipelines like supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning. The method employs KL divergence loss to distill knowledge from a full-precision teacher model into a quantized student model, demonstrating robustness to data quality and eliminating the need for full training datasets. Experimental results on models including AceReason Nemotron and Llama Nemotron Super v1 show that QAD consistently recovers accuracy to near-BF16 levels across various post-trained models.
本文提出了量化感知蒸馏（QAD）方法，用于恢复NVFP4精度量化的大型语言和视觉语言模型的推理准确性，旨在解决传统量化感知训练（QAT）在监督微调、强化学习等多阶段后训练流程中存在的工程复杂性和训练不稳定问题。该方法使用KL散度损失将全精度教师模型的知识蒸馏到量化学生模型中，对数据质量和覆盖范围具有鲁棒性，无需完整训练数据即可实现精度恢复。在AceReason Nemotron和Llama Nemotron Super v1等多个后训练模型上的实验结果表明，QAD能一致地将准确性恢复到接近BF16精度的水平。
Post Hoc Extraction of Pareto Fronts for Continuous Control
Authors: Raghav Thakar, Gaurav Dixit, Kagan Tumer
Venue: IJCAI 2026
First: 2026-03-03T05:57:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T05:57:59+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 4 figures. Submitted to IJCAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agents in the real world must often balance multiple objectives, such as speed, stability, and energy efficiency in continuous control. To account for changing conditions and preferences, an agent must ideally learn a Pareto frontier of policies representing multiple optimal trade-offs. Recent advances in multi-policy multi-objective reinforcement learning (MORL) enable learning a Pareto front directly, but require full multi-objective consideration from the start of training. In practice, multi-objective preferences often arise after a policy has already been trained on a single specialised objective. Existing MORL methods cannot leverage these pre-trained `specialists' to learn Pareto fronts and avoid incurring the sample costs of retraining. We introduce Mixed Advantage Pareto Extraction (MAPEX), an offline MORL method that constructs a frontier of policies by reusing pre-trained specialist policies, critics, and replay buffers. MAPEX combines evaluations from specialist critics into a mixed advantage signal, and weights a behaviour cloning loss with it to train new policies that balance multiple objectives. MAPEX's post hoc Pareto front extraction preserves the simplicity of single-objective off-policy RL, and avoids retrofitting these algorithms into complex MORL frameworks. We formally describe the MAPEX procedure and evaluate MAPEX on five multi-objective MuJoCo environments. Given the same starting policies, MAPEX produces comparable fronts at $0.001\%$ the sample cost of established baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续控制中帕累托前沿的事后提取
现实世界中的智能体常需平衡多个目标，如连续控制中的速度、稳定性和能效。为适应变化的条件和偏好，理想情况下智能体应学习代表多种最优权衡的帕累托前沿策略。多策略多目标强化学习（MORL）的最新进展可直接学习帕累托前沿，但需从训练开始就全面考虑多目标。实践中，多目标偏好常在策略已针对单一专业目标训练后才出现。现有MORL方法无法利用这些预训练的“专家”策略来学习帕累托前沿，且难以避免重新训练的高样本成本。本文提出混合优势帕累托提取（MAPEX），这是一种离线MORL方法，通过复用预训练的专家策略、评论家和回放缓冲区构建策略前沿。MAPEX将专家评论家的评估合并为混合优势信号，并以此加权行为克隆损失，训练平衡多目标的新策略。该方法的事后帕累托前沿提取保留了单目标离策略强化学习的简洁性，无需将这些算法改造为复杂MORL框架。我们形式化描述了MAPEX流程，并在五个多目标MuJoCo环境中评估其性能。在相同初始策略下，MAPEX能以基线方法0.001%的样本成本生成可比拟的帕累托前沿。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the practical challenge where multi-objective preferences emerge after a single-objective policy has already been trained, as existing multi-objective reinforcement learning methods cannot reuse such pre-trained specialists without costly retraining. The authors propose Mixed Advantage Pareto Extraction (MAPEX), an offline method that constructs a Pareto frontier by leveraging pre-trained specialist policies, critics, and replay buffers; it combines specialist critic evaluations into a mixed advantage signal to weight a behavior cloning loss for training new balanced policies. Experimental results on five multi-objective MuJoCo environments demonstrate that MAPEX produces comparable Pareto fronts at only 0.001% of the sample cost of established baselines, effectively extracting frontiers post hoc while preserving the simplicity of single-objective off-policy RL.
本文针对实践中多目标偏好常在单目标策略训练完成后才出现的问题，而现有多目标强化学习方法无法重用此类预训练专家策略且避免高成本重新训练。作者提出了混合优势帕累托提取（MAPEX），这是一种离线方法，通过利用预训练的专家策略、评论家和回放缓冲区来构建帕累托前沿；该方法将专家评论家的评估组合成混合优势信号，用于加权行为克隆损失以训练新的平衡策略。在五个多目标MuJoCo环境上的实验结果表明，MAPEX能以仅为基础方法0.001%的样本成本生成可比的帕累托前沿，从而在保持单目标离策略强化学习简洁性的同时，实现了事后前沿的有效提取。
Real-Time Generative Policy via Langevin-Guided Flow Matching for Autonomous Driving
Authors: Tianze Zhu, Yinuo Wang, Wenjun Zou, Tianyi Zhang, Likun Wang, Letian Tao, Feihong Zhang, Yao Lyu, Shengbo Eben Li
First: 2026-03-03T05:35:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-03T05:35:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) is a fundamental methodology in autonomous driving systems, where generative policies exhibit considerable potential by leveraging their ability to model complex distributions to enhance exploration. However, their inherent high inference latency severely impedes their deployment in real-time decision-making and control. To address this issue, we propose diffusion actor-critic with entropy regulator via flow matching (DACER-F) by introducing flow matching into online RL, enabling the generation of competitive actions in a single inference step. By leveraging Langevin dynamics and gradients of the Q-function, DACER-F dynamically optimizes actions from experience replay toward a target distribution that balances high Q-value information with exploratory behavior. The flow policy is then trained to efficiently learn a mapping from a simple prior distribution to this dynamic target. In complex multi-lane and intersection simulations, DACER-F outperforms baselines diffusion actor-critic with entropy regulator (DACER) and distributional soft actor-critic (DSAC), while maintaining an ultra-low inference latency. DACER-F further demonstrates its scalability on standard RL benchmark DeepMind Control Suite (DMC), achieving a score of 775.8 in the humanoid-stand task and surpassing prior methods. Collectively, these results establish DACER-F as a high-performance and computationally efficient RL algorithm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于朗之万引导流匹配的自动驾驶实时生成策略
强化学习是自动驾驶系统的核心方法，其中生成策略通过建模复杂分布以增强探索能力展现出巨大潜力。然而，其固有的高推理延迟严重阻碍了在实时决策与控制中的部署。为解决该问题，我们提出基于流匹配的熵调节扩散行动者-评论家算法，通过将流匹配引入在线强化学习，实现单步推理生成优质动作。该算法利用朗之万动力学与Q函数梯度，动态优化经验回放中的动作，使其逼近平衡高Q值信息与探索行为的目标分布。流策略通过训练高效学习从简单先验分布到该动态目标的映射。在复杂多车道与交叉口仿真中，该算法在保持超低推理延迟的同时，性能优于基线方法熵调节扩散行动者-评论家算法与分布式软行动者-评论家算法。该算法在标准强化学习基准DeepMind控制套件上进一步展现了可扩展性，在人形站立任务中获得775.8分，超越现有方法。综合结果表明，该算法是一种高性能且计算高效的强化学习算法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to reduce the high inference latency of generative policies in reinforcement learning for autonomous driving, which hinders real-time deployment, this paper introduces DACER-F, a method that integrates flow matching with online RL to enable single-step action generation. The approach utilizes Langevin dynamics and Q-function gradients to dynamically optimize actions from experience replay towards a target distribution that balances high Q-values and exploration, training a flow policy to map from a simple prior to this target. Experimental results in complex driving simulations show DACER-F outperforms baselines like DACER and DSAC while maintaining ultra-low latency, and it demonstrates scalability on the DeepMind Control Suite, achieving a score of 775.8 in the humanoid-stand task, surpassing prior methods and establishing it as a high-performance, efficient algorithm.
针对强化学习中生成策略推理延迟高、阻碍自动驾驶实时部署的问题，本文提出了DACER-F方法，通过将流匹配引入在线强化学习，实现单步动作生成。该方法利用朗之万动力学和Q函数梯度，动态优化经验回放中的动作，使其趋向于平衡高Q值和探索性的目标分布，并训练流策略从简单先验映射到该目标。在复杂多车道和交叉口仿真中，DACER-F在保持超低推理延迟的同时，性能优于DACER和DSAC等基线方法；在DeepMind Control Suite基准测试中进一步展示了可扩展性，在humanoid-stand任务中获得775.8分，超越先前方法，确立了其作为高性能、计算高效算法的地位。
